// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// INIT
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
async function init() {
  try {
    loadSettings();
    loadPositions();
    loadSVState();
    loadDividendsCache();
    renderDashContent(false);
    renderAlerts();
    updateMktStatus();
    updateBriefDate();
    const pip = document.getElementById('alert-pip');
    if(ST.alerts.length>0 && pip) pip.style.display='block';
    updateScannerStats();
    if(ST.settings.auto) setTimeout(()=>{ loadAllData().catch(e=>console.warn('loadAllData:',e)); },200);
    setInterval(()=>{ loadAllData().catch(e=>console.warn('loadAllData interval:',e)); }, 3*60*1000);
    // Auto-load crypto market data on startup so header bar BTC/ETH/SOL populate
    setTimeout(()=>{ loadCryptoMarket().catch(e=>console.warn('init crypto:',e)); }, 500);
    // Only auto-load Brief if we have a cached version or an API key
    setTimeout(()=>{
      try {
        const cached = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('forge_brief')||'null');
        if (cached && (Date.now()-cached.ts) < 10800000) {
          loadBrief().catch(e=>console.warn('loadBrief cache:',e));
        } else if (ST.settings.ak) {
          loadBrief().catch(e=>console.warn('loadBrief:',e));
        } else {
          setBriefStatus('error');
          const bcEl=document.getElementById('brief-content');
          if(bcEl) bcEl.innerHTML='<div class="brief-empty"><div class="brief-empty-icon">🔑</div><div class="brief-empty-txt">ADD ANTHROPIC API KEY IN SETTINGS TO ENABLE INTELLIGENCE BRIEF</div></div>';
        }
      } catch(e) { console.warn('Brief init:', e); }
    }, 1200);
    renderPerfContent('daily');
        if(SV.autoOn && !SV.timer){
      SV.timer = setInterval(()=>runSurveillance().catch(e=>console.warn('surveillance:',e)), SV.intervalMs);
      setTimeout(()=>runSurveillance().catch(e=>console.warn('surveillance init:',e)), 4000);
    }
  } catch(e) {
    console.error('init() error:', e.message, e.stack);
  }
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// NAVIGATION
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function showScreen(name,btn){
  // Always close detail panel when switching screens
  const detailEl=document.getElementById('detail');
  if(detailEl) detailEl.classList.remove('open');
  document.querySelectorAll('.screen').forEach(s=>s.classList.remove('active'));
  document.querySelectorAll('.nb').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('on'));
  const s=document.getElementById('s-'+name); if(s) s.classList.add('active');
  if(btn) btn.classList.add('on');
  if(name==='charts'){
    setTimeout(()=>{
      if(!TA_S.taInited) initTA();
      // Make sure the chart sub-screen is active
      taShowTab(TA_S.tab || 'chart');
      if(typeof scheduleRedraw==="function") scheduleRedraw();
      // Force load asset if no data
      if(TA_S.asset && (!TA_S.data[TA_S.asset] || !TA_S.data[TA_S.asset].length)) {
        loadAsset(TA_S.asset).catch(e=>console.warn('chart load:', e));
      }
    }, 150);
  }
  if(name==='scanner') initScannerView();
  if(name==='analysis') renderAnalysisPicker();
}
function switchSeg(seg,btn){
  ST.seg=seg;
  document.querySelectorAll('#dash-seg .seg-btn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('on'));
  if(btn) btn.classList.add('on'); else document.querySelector(`[data-seg="${seg}"]`)?.classList.add('on');
  renderDashContent(false);
}
function switchPortSeg(name,btn){
  ST.portSeg=name;
  ['positions','edit','bottom','ai'].forEach(n=>{ const el=document.getElementById('port-'+n); if(el) el.style.display=n===name?'block':'none'; });
  if(name==='edit') renderEditPositions();
  document.querySelectorAll('#port-seg .seg-btn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('on'));
  if(btn) btn.classList.add('on');
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SETTINGS
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function loadSettings(){
  // Seed defaults so app works even if storage is wiped
  const DEFAULTS = {
    fh:   'd6mp561r01qir35huhagd6mp561r01qir35huhb0',
    fred: 'e09d843a0d5c7a7ac464a799c79173cd',
    ak:   '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',
    ntfy: 'forgeai-MT'
  };
  // Apply defaults first
  Object.assign(ST.settings, DEFAULTS);
  // Then override with any saved settings
  try{
    let s=localStorage.getItem('forge_set')||sessionStorage.getItem('forge_set');
    if(!s){
      const m=document.cookie.match(/forge_set=([^;]+)/);
      if(m) s=decodeURIComponent(m[1]);
    }
    if(s){
      const saved=JSON.parse(s);
      // Only override if saved value is non-empty
      Object.keys(saved).forEach(k=>{ if(saved[k]) ST.settings[k]=saved[k]; });
    }
  }catch(e){}
  ['fh','fred','ak','ntfy'].forEach(k=>{ const el=document.getElementById('set-'+k); if(el) el.value=ST.settings[k]||''; });
  const sp=document.getElementById('set-port'); if(sp) sp.value=ST.settings.portSize||700620;
  const sr=document.getElementById('set-risk'); if(sr) sr.value=ST.settings.riskProfile||'aggressive';
  const sda=document.getElementById('set-divAlert'); if(sda) sda.value=ST.settings.divAlert||14;
}
function saveSettings(){
  ['fh','fred','ak','ntfy'].forEach(k=>{ const el=document.getElementById('set-'+k); if(el) ST.settings[k]=el.value.trim(); });
  const sp=document.getElementById('set-port'); if(sp) ST.settings.portSize=parseInt(sp.value)||700620;
  const sr=document.getElementById('set-risk'); if(sr) ST.settings.riskProfile=sr.value;
  const sda=document.getElementById('set-divAlert'); if(sda) ST.settings.divAlert=parseInt(sda.value)||14;
  const s=JSON.stringify(ST.settings);
  try{ localStorage.setItem('forge_set',s); }catch(e){}
  try{ sessionStorage.setItem('forge_set',s); }catch(e){}
  try{ document.cookie='forge_set='+encodeURIComponent(s)+';path=/;max-age=31536000;SameSite=Lax'; }catch(e){}
  updateSourceChips();
  showToast('Settings saved ✓');
}
function exportKeys() {
  const keys = {
    fh: ST.settings.fh || '',
    fred: ST.settings.fred || '',
    ak: ST.settings.ak || '',
    ntfy: ST.settings.ntfy || ''
  };
  const code = btoa(JSON.stringify(keys));
  const box = document.getElementById('export-box');
  const codeEl = document.getElementById('export-code');
  if (box && codeEl) {
    codeEl.textContent = code;
    box.style.display = 'block';
  }
}

function copyExportCode() {
  const code = document.getElementById('export-code')?.textContent;
  if (!code) return;
  navigator.clipboard?.writeText(code).then(() => showToast('Code copied ✓')).catch(() => {
    // Fallback for iOS
    const ta = document.createElement('textarea');
    ta.value = code;
    document.body.appendChild(ta);
    ta.select();
    document.execCommand('copy');
    document.body.removeChild(ta);
    showToast('Code copied ✓');
  });
}

function importKeys() {
  const code = prompt('Paste your export code:');
  if (!code) return;
  try {
    const keys = JSON.parse(atob(code.trim()));
    if (keys.ak) { ST.settings.ak = keys.ak; const el = document.getElementById('set-ak'); if(el) el.value = keys.ak; }
    if (keys.fh) { ST.settings.fh = keys.fh; const el = document.getElementById('set-fh'); if(el) el.value = keys.fh; }
    if (keys.fred) { ST.settings.fred = keys.fred; const el = document.getElementById('set-fred'); if(el) el.value = keys.fred; }
    if (keys.ntfy) { ST.settings.ntfy = keys.ntfy; const el = document.getElementById('set-ntfy'); if(el) el.value = keys.ntfy; }
    saveSettings();
    showToast('Keys imported ✓');
  } catch(e) {
    showToast('Invalid code — check and retry');
  }
}

function toggleSet(k,el){ ST.settings[k]=!ST.settings[k]; el.classList.toggle('on',ST.settings[k]); try{localStorage.setItem('forge_set',JSON.stringify(ST.settings));}catch(e){} }

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// DATA SOURCES
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function updateSourceChips(){
  const s=ST.settings;
  setChip('src-fg', ST.fearGreed!==null?'ok':'wait');
  setChip('src-cg', ST.btcPrice?'ok':'wait');
  setChip('src-fh', s.fh?'ok':'off');
  setChip('src-fred', s.fred&&Object.keys(ST.fredData).length>0?'ok':s.fred?'wait':'off');
  setChip('src-ntfy', s.ntfy?'ok':'off');
  setChip('src-ai', s.ak?'ok':'off');
  const _nb=document.getElementById('no-keys-banner');
  if(_nb) _nb.style.display=(!s.fh&&!s.ak)?'flex':'none';
}
function setChip(id,state){ const el=document.getElementById(id); if(!el)return; el.className='src-chip src-'+state; }

async function loadFinnhub(){
  if(!ST.settings.fh) return;
  // Always fetch core market tickers + all watchlist tickers
  const coreTickers = ['SPY','QQQ','VIX','CLOV','UNH','HMBL'];
  const watchTickers = (ST.watchlist||[]).map(w=>w.ticker).filter(t=>t!=='BTC'&&t!=='ETH'&&t!=='SOL');
  const allTickers = [...new Set([...coreTickers, ...watchTickers])];
  const quotes = await Promise.all(allTickers.map(t=>fetchQ(t)));
  allTickers.forEach((t,i)=>{ if(quotes[i]){ ST.quotes[t]=quotes[i]; ST.lastClose[t]=quotes[i]; try{localStorage.setItem('forge_lc',JSON.stringify(ST.lastClose));}catch(e){} } });
  setChip('src-fh','ok');
  // SPY / VIX for macro strip
  const spy=ST.quotes['SPY'], vix=ST.quotes['VIX'];
  if(spy){
    const msspx=document.getElementById('ms-spx'); if(msspx) msspx.textContent='$'+spy.price.toFixed(0);
    const sc=document.getElementById('ms-spx-c'); if(sc){sc.textContent=safePctStr(spy);sc.className='mi-chg '+(spy.pct>=0?'up':'dn');}
    ['tt-spy','tt-spy2'].forEach(id=>{const e=document.getElementById(id);if(e)e.textContent='$'+spy.price.toFixed(0);});
  }
  if(vix){
    const msvix=document.getElementById('ms-vix'); if(msvix) msvix.textContent=vix.price.toFixed(1);
    ['tt-vix','tt-vix2'].forEach(id=>{const e=document.getElementById(id);if(e)e.textContent=vix.price.toFixed(1);});
    // Bottom tracker VIX
    const bv=document.getElementById('b-vix'), bvv=document.getElementById('b-vix-val');
    if(bv&&bvv){
      bvv.textContent=vix.price.toFixed(1);
      if(vix.price>35){bv.textContent='EXTREME';bv.className='conf-status css-green';}
      else if(vix.price>25){bv.textContent='ELEVATED';bv.className='conf-status css-amber';}
      else{bv.textContent='NORMAL';bv.className='conf-status css-grey';}
    }
  }
  // CLOV/UNH ticker tape
  const cv=ST.quotes['CLOV'], uv=ST.quotes['UNH'];
  if(cv){['tt-clov','tt-clov2'].forEach(id=>{const e=document.getElementById(id);if(e)e.textContent='$'+cv.price.toFixed(2);});
    ['tt-clov-c','tt-clov-c2'].forEach(id=>{const e=document.getElementById(id);if(e){e.textContent=(cv.pct>=0?'+':'')+cv.pct?.toFixed(2)+'%';e.className=cv.pct>=0?'up':'dn';}});}
  if(uv){['tt-unh','tt-unh2'].forEach(id=>{const e=document.getElementById(id);if(e)e.textContent='$'+uv.price.toFixed(0);});
    ['tt-unh-c','tt-unh-c2'].forEach(id=>{const e=document.getElementById(id);if(e){e.textContent=(uv.pct>=0?'+':'')+uv.pct?.toFixed(2)+'%';e.className=uv.pct>=0?'up':'dn';}});}
  // Macro risk badge
  updateMacroRisk(spy,vix);
  checkAlertTriggers();
  // Re-render market cards with fresh prices
  renderDashContent(false);
  updateHeaderTape();
}
function updateHeaderTape() {
  const q = ST.quotes || {};
  const cd = ST.cryptoData || {};

  // Helper: set element text safely
  function set(id, txt) { const e = document.getElementById(id); if(e) e.textContent = txt; }
  function setClass(id, cls) { const e = document.getElementById(id); if(e) e.className = cls; }

  // CLOV
  if (q['CLOV']) {
    const p = fp(q['CLOV'].price, 'CLOV'), c = safePctStr(q['CLOV']);
    ['tt-clov','tt-clov2'].forEach(id => set(id, p));
    ['tt-clov-c','tt-clov-c2'].forEach(id => { set(id, c); setClass(id, q['CLOV'].pct >= 0 ? 'up' : 'dn'); });
    // Market pulse cards
    set('ms-clov', p);
    const mcc = document.getElementById('ms-clov-c');
    if(mcc){ mcc.textContent = c; mcc.className = 'mi-chg '+(q['CLOV'].pct>=0?'up':'dn'); }
  }

  // UNH
  if (q['UNH']) {
    const p = fp(q['UNH'].price, 'UNH'), c = safePctStr(q['UNH']);
    ['tt-unh','tt-unh2'].forEach(id => set(id, p));
    ['tt-unh-c','tt-unh-c2'].forEach(id => { set(id, c); setClass(id, q['UNH'].pct >= 0 ? 'up' : 'dn'); });
    set('ms-unh', p);
    const muc = document.getElementById('ms-unh-c');
    if(muc){ muc.textContent = c; muc.className = 'mi-chg '+(q['UNH'].pct>=0?'up':'dn'); }
  }

  // SPY
  if (q['SPY']) {
    const p = '$'+q['SPY'].price.toFixed(0), c = safePctStr(q['SPY']);
    ['tt-spy','tt-spy2'].forEach(id => set(id, p));
    set('ms-spx', p);
    const sc = document.getElementById('ms-spx-c');
    if(sc){ sc.textContent = c; sc.className = 'mi-chg '+(q['SPY'].pct>=0?'up':'dn'); }
  }

  // VIX
  if (q['VIX']) {
    const p = q['VIX'].price.toFixed(1);
    ['tt-vix','tt-vix2'].forEach(id => set(id, p));
    set('ms-vix', p);
  }

  // BTC
  const btc = cd.bitcoin || cd.btc;
  if (btc) {
    const p = '$'+Math.round(btc.usd || btc.current_price || 0).toLocaleString();
    const chgVal = btc.usd_24h_change ?? btc.price_change_percentage_24h ?? 0;
    const c = (chgVal>=0?'+':'')+chgVal.toFixed(2)+'%';
    ['tt-btc','tt-btc2'].forEach(id => set(id, p));
    ['tt-btc-c'].forEach(id => { set(id, c); setClass(id, chgVal>=0?'up':'dn'); });
    set('ms-btc', p);
    const mc = document.getElementById('ms-btc-c');
    if(mc){ mc.textContent = c; mc.className = 'mi-chg '+(chgVal>=0?'up':'dn'); }
  }

  // ETH
  const eth = cd.ethereum;
  if (eth) {
    const p = '$'+Math.round(eth.usd || eth.current_price || 0).toLocaleString();
    ['tt-eth','tt-eth2'].forEach(id => set(id, p));
    set('ms-eth', p);
    const chgVal = eth.usd_24h_change ?? eth.price_change_percentage_24h ?? 0;
    const mec = document.getElementById('ms-eth-c');
    if(mec){ mec.textContent = (chgVal>=0?'+':'')+chgVal.toFixed(2)+'%'; mec.className = 'mi-chg '+(chgVal>=0?'up':'dn'); }
  }

  // SOL
  const sol = cd.solana;
  if (sol) {
    const p = '$'+Math.round(sol.usd || sol.current_price || 0).toLocaleString();
    ['tt-sol','tt-sol2'].forEach(id => set(id, p));
    set('ms-sol', p);
    const chgVal = sol.usd_24h_change ?? sol.price_change_percentage_24h ?? 0;
    const msc = document.getElementById('ms-sol-c');
    if(msc){ msc.textContent = (chgVal>=0?'+':'')+chgVal.toFixed(2)+'%'; msc.className = 'mi-chg '+(chgVal>=0?'up':'dn'); }
  }

  // Fear & Greed
  if (ST.fearGreed) {
    const fg = ST.fearGreed + ' ('+ST.fearGreedLabel+')';
    ['tt-fg','tt-fg2'].forEach(id => set(id, fg));
    set('ms-fg', ST.fearGreed+'');
    const mfl = document.getElementById('ms-fg-lbl');
    if(mfl) mfl.textContent = ST.fearGreedLabel || '';
  }
}
function updateMacroRisk(spy,vix){
  const badge=document.getElementById('risk-badge'); if(!badge) return;
  const msr=document.getElementById('ms-risk');
  let score=0;
  if(vix?.price>35) score+=3; else if(vix?.price>25) score+=2;
  if(spy?.pct<-1.5) score+=2; else if(spy?.pct<-0.5) score+=1;
  if(score>=4){badge.textContent='RISK-OFF';badge.className='ph-badge red';if(msr){msr.textContent='RISK-OFF';msr.style.color='var(--red)';}}
  else if(score>=2){badge.textContent='CAUTION';badge.className='ph-badge amber';if(msr){msr.textContent='CAUTION';msr.style.color='var(--amber)';}}
  else{badge.textContent='RISK-ON';badge.className='ph-badge green';if(msr){msr.textContent='RISK-ON';msr.style.color='var(--green)';}}
}
function drawTAChart(allData){
  const canvas=document.getElementById('ta-canvas');
  const wrap=canvas?.parentElement;
  if(!canvas||!wrap||!allData||!allData.length)return;
  const dpr=window.devicePixelRatio||1,W=wrap.clientWidth;
  if(W<10){setTimeout(()=>drawTAChart(allData),100);return;}
  const days=tfDays(TAB.tf);
  const candles=allData.slice(-days);
  if(!candles.length)return;

  const volH=TAB.ind.vol?50:0,rsiH=TAB.ind.rsi?60:0,macdH=TAB.ind.macd?60:0;
  const mainH=200,H=mainH+volH+rsiH+macdH;
  canvas.style.height=H+'px';canvas.width=W*dpr;canvas.height=H*dpr;
  const ctx=canvas.getContext('2d');ctx.scale(dpr,dpr);ctx.clearRect(0,0,W,H);

  const PAD={l:4,r:50,t:10,b:4},cW=W-PAD.l-PAD.r;
  const allC=allData.map(c=>c.c),off=allData.length-candles.length;
  const calcE=(d,p)=>{const k=2/(p+1);const r=new Array(d.length).fill(null);let e=null;for(let i=0;i<d.length;i++){if(e===null){if(i<p-1)continue;e=d.slice(0,p).reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0)/p;r[i]=e;}else{e=d[i]*k+e*(1-k);r[i]=e;}}return r;};
  const e20=calcE(allC,20).slice(off),e50=calcE(allC,50).slice(off),e200=calcE(allC,200).slice(off);
  const rsiV=(()=>{const p=14,src=allC;if(src.length<p+2)return new Array(candles.length).fill(null);let ag=0,al=0;for(let i=1;i<=p;i++){const d=src[i]-src[i-1];d>0?ag+=d:al-=d;}ag/=p;al/=p;const r=new Array(src.length).fill(null);r[p]=al===0?100:100-100/(1+ag/al);for(let i=p+1;i<src.length;i++){const d=src[i]-src[i-1],g=Math.max(0,d),l=Math.max(0,-d);ag=(ag*(p-1)+g)/p;al=(al*(p-1)+l)/p;r[i]=al===0?100:100-100/(1+ag/al);}return r.slice(off);})();

  let pMax=Math.max(...candles.map(c=>c.h)),pMin=Math.min(...candles.map(c=>c.l));
  const pr=pMax-pMin;pMax+=pr*0.05;pMin-=pr*0.05;
  const px=p=>PAD.t+mainH-PAD.b-(p-pMin)/(pMax-pMin)*(mainH-PAD.t-PAD.b);
  const cx=i=>PAD.l+(i+0.5)/candles.length*cW;
  const cw=Math.max(1,cW/candles.length*0.75);

  ctx.fillStyle='#1c1c1c';ctx.fillRect(0,0,W,mainH);
  ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(255,255,255,.04)';ctx.lineWidth=0.5;
  for(let i=0;i<=4;i++){const y=PAD.t+(mainH-PAD.t-PAD.b)*i/4;ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(PAD.l,y);ctx.lineTo(W-PAD.r,y);ctx.stroke();}

  const dl=(pts,col,lw,dash=[])=>{const v=pts.filter(Boolean);if(!v.length)return;ctx.save();ctx.strokeStyle=col;ctx.lineWidth=lw||1;ctx.setLineDash(dash);ctx.lineJoin='round';ctx.beginPath();let s=false;pts.forEach(p=>{if(!p){s=false;return;}if(!s){ctx.moveTo(p[0],p[1]);s=true;}else ctx.lineTo(p[0],p[1]);});ctx.stroke();ctx.restore();};

  if(TAB.ov.ema200)dl(e200.map((v,i)=>v?[cx(i),px(v)]:null),'#b48eff',1.2);
  if(TAB.ov.ema50)dl(e50.map((v,i)=>v?[cx(i),px(v)]:null),'#ffb800',1.2);
  if(TAB.ov.ema20)dl(e20.map((v,i)=>v?[cx(i),px(v)]:null),'#00c8ff',1);

  candles.forEach((c,i)=>{
    const x=cx(i),bull=c.c>=c.o,col=bull?'#00c853':'#ff4560';
    const bT=px(Math.max(c.o,c.c)),bB=px(Math.min(c.o,c.c)),bH=Math.max(1,bB-bT);
    ctx.strokeStyle=col;ctx.lineWidth=0.8;ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(x,px(c.h));ctx.lineTo(x,bT);ctx.moveTo(x,bB);ctx.lineTo(x,px(c.l));ctx.stroke();
    ctx.fillStyle=bull?col+'cc':col+'aa';ctx.fillRect(x-cw/2,bT,cw,bH);
  });

  const last=candles[candles.length-1];
  if(last){ctx.fillStyle='rgba(0,200,255,.9)';ctx.font="bold 8px 'DM Mono'";ctx.textAlign='left';const lp=last.c>=1000?'$'+Math.round(last.c).toLocaleString():last.c>=1?'$'+last.c.toFixed(2):'$'+last.c.toFixed(4);ctx.fillText(lp,W-PAD.r+2,px(last.c)+3);}
  ctx.fillStyle='rgba(61,90,112,.8)';ctx.font="7px 'DM Mono'";ctx.textAlign='left';
  for(let i=0;i<=3;i++){const v=pMin+(pMax-pMin)*i/3,y=PAD.t+(mainH-PAD.t-PAD.b)*(1-i/3);const lbl=v>=1000?'$'+Math.round(v/1000)+'K':v>=1?'$'+v.toFixed(1):'$'+v.toFixed(3);ctx.fillText(lbl,W-PAD.r+2,y+3);}

  let panelY=mainH;
  if(TAB.ind.vol&&candles.some(c=>c.v)){
    ctx.fillStyle='#1c1c1c';ctx.fillRect(0,panelY,W,volH);
    ctx.fillStyle='rgba(255,255,255,.06)';ctx.fillRect(PAD.l,panelY,cW,1);
    ctx.fillStyle='rgba(61,90,112,.7)';ctx.font="7px 'DM Mono'";ctx.textAlign='left';ctx.fillText('VOL',PAD.l+2,panelY+10);
    const maxV=Math.max(...candles.map(c=>c.v));
    if(maxV>0)candles.forEach((c,i)=>{const h=(c.v/maxV)*(volH-16);ctx.fillStyle=c.c>=c.o?'rgba(0,200,83,.4)':'rgba(255,69,96,.4)';ctx.fillRect(cx(i)-cw/2,panelY+volH-8-h,cw,h);});
    panelY+=volH;
  }
  if(TAB.ind.rsi){
    ctx.fillStyle='#1c1c1c';ctx.fillRect(0,panelY,W,rsiH);
    ctx.fillStyle='rgba(255,255,255,.06)';ctx.fillRect(PAD.l,panelY,cW,1);
    ctx.fillStyle='rgba(0,229,204,.5)';ctx.font="7px 'DM Mono'";ctx.textAlign='left';ctx.fillText('RSI',PAD.l+2,panelY+10);
    const ry=v=>panelY+rsiH-6-(v/100)*(rsiH-16);
    [30,70].forEach(l=>{ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(255,255,255,.08)';ctx.lineWidth=0.5;ctx.setLineDash([3,3]);ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(PAD.l,ry(l));ctx.lineTo(W-PAD.r,ry(l));ctx.stroke();ctx.setLineDash([]);ctx.fillStyle='rgba(61,90,112,.7)';ctx.fillText(l,W-PAD.r+2,ry(l)+3);});
    dl(rsiV.map((v,i)=>v!=null?[cx(i),ry(v)]:null),'#00e5cc',1.2);
    panelY+=rsiH;
  }
  if(TAB.ind.macd){
    ctx.fillStyle='#1c1c1c';ctx.fillRect(0,panelY,W,macdH);
    ctx.fillStyle='rgba(255,255,255,.06)';ctx.fillRect(PAD.l,panelY,cW,1);
    ctx.fillStyle='rgba(180,142,255,.5)';ctx.font="7px 'DM Mono'";ctx.textAlign='left';ctx.fillText('MACD',PAD.l+2,panelY+10);
    const ema12=calcE(allC,12).slice(off),ema26=calcE(allC,26).slice(off);
    const ml=ema12.map((v,i)=>v&&ema26[i]?v-ema26[i]:null);
    const sl=calcE(ml.map(v=>v||0),9);
    const hist=ml.map((v,i)=>v&&sl[i]?v-sl[i]:null);
    const vals=[...ml,...sl,...hist].filter(v=>v!=null);
    if(vals.length){
      const minM=Math.min(...vals),maxM=Math.max(...vals),rng=maxM-minM||1;
      const my=v=>panelY+macdH-6-((v-minM)/rng)*(macdH-16);
      const zY=my(0);
      ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(255,255,255,.08)';ctx.lineWidth=0.5;ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(PAD.l,zY);ctx.lineTo(W-PAD.r,zY);ctx.stroke();
      hist.forEach((v,i)=>{if(v==null)return;const y=my(v),h2=Math.abs(zY-y);ctx.fillStyle=v>=0?'rgba(0,200,83,.5)':'rgba(255,69,96,.5)';ctx.fillRect(cx(i)-cw/2,Math.min(y,zY),cw,h2);});
      dl(ml.map((v,i)=>v!=null?[cx(i),my(v)]:null),'#00c8ff',1.2);
      dl(sl.map((v,i)=>v!=null?[cx(i),my(v)]:null),'#ffb800',1);
    }
  }
}
async function loadAllData(){
  try {
    await Promise.allSettled([loadCrypto(), loadFearGreed(), loadFinnhub(), loadFRED(), loadDividends()]);
    updateSourceChips();
    updateDeployScore();
    savePerfBaseline();
    renderPerfContent('daily');
    updateMktStatus();
    updateBriefPulse();
    renderDashContent(false);
    updateHeaderTape();
  } catch(e) {
    console.warn('loadAllData error:', e.message);
  }
}

// ── CoinGecko ─────────────────────────────────────────
async function loadCrypto(){
  // NEVER calls CoinGecko directly — reads from cache or CR.coins only.
  // loadCryptoMarket() is the single source of truth for all CoinGecko data.
  try {
    // Try in-memory first (fastest)
    if (CR.coins && CR.coins.length) {
      const btc = CR.coins.find(c=>c.id==='bitcoin');
      const eth = CR.coins.find(c=>c.id==='ethereum');
      const sol = CR.coins.find(c=>c.id==='solana');
      if (btc) {
        ST.cryptoData = {
          bitcoin: { usd: btc.current_price, usd_24h_change: btc.price_change_percentage_24h, usd_market_cap: btc.market_cap },
          ethereum: eth ? { usd: eth.current_price, usd_24h_change: eth.price_change_percentage_24h } : null,
          solana:   sol ? { usd: sol.current_price, usd_24h_change: sol.price_change_percentage_24h } : null,
        };
        ST.btcPrice = btc.current_price; ST.btcChange = btc.price_change_percentage_24h;
        updateCryptoPrices(ST.cryptoData);
        setChip('src-cg','ok');
        return;
      }
    }
    // Fall back to localStorage cache
    const cached = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(CRYPTO_CACHE_KEY)||'null');
    if (cached && cached.coins && (Date.now()-cached.ts) < CRYPTO_CACHE_TTL) {
      const btc = cached.coins.find(c=>c.id==='bitcoin');
      if (btc) {
        ST.cryptoData = {
          bitcoin: { usd: btc.current_price, usd_24h_change: btc.price_change_percentage_24h, usd_market_cap: btc.market_cap },
        };
        ST.btcPrice = btc.current_price; ST.btcChange = btc.price_change_percentage_24h;
        updateCryptoPrices(ST.cryptoData);
        setChip('src-cg','ok');
        return;
      }
    }
  } catch(e) {}
  // No cache yet — show err chip, user can tap Crypto tab to load
  setChip('src-cg','err');
}

function updateCryptoPrices(d){
  if(d?.bitcoin){
    const p=d.bitcoin.usd, chg=d.bitcoin.usd_24h_change;
    const ps='$'+p.toLocaleString('en-US',{maximumFractionDigits:0});
    const cs=(chg>=0?'+':'')+chg.toFixed(2)+'%';
    ['tt-btc','tt-btc2'].forEach(id=>{const e=document.getElementById(id);if(e)e.textContent=ps;});
    const msbtc=document.getElementById('ms-btc'); if(msbtc) msbtc.textContent=ps;
    const mc=document.getElementById('ms-btc-c'); if(mc){mc.textContent=cs;mc.className='mi-chg '+(chg>=0?'up':'dn');}
    // Deploy screen
    const bcp=document.getElementById('btc-current-price'); if(bcp) bcp.textContent=ps;
    const bt1=document.getElementById('btc-t1');
    if(bt1){
      if(p<65000){bt1.textContent=`BTC @ ${ps} — IN ACCUMULATION ZONE ($62–68K)`;bt1.className='trig-detail hit';}
      else if(p<80000){bt1.textContent=`BTC @ ${ps} — watching for drop to $62–68K entry zone`;bt1.className='trig-detail watch';}
      else{bt1.textContent=`BTC @ ${ps} — above entry zone. Wait for correction.`;bt1.className='trig-detail';}
    }
    // Update ticker tape change indicators
    ['tt-btc-c'].forEach(id=>{const e=document.getElementById(id);if(e){e.textContent=cs;e.className=chg>=0?'up':'dn';}});
  }
  if(d?.ethereum){
    const ep=d.ethereum.usd, ec=d.ethereum.usd_24h_change;
    const eps='$'+ep.toLocaleString('en-US',{maximumFractionDigits:0});
    const ecs=(ec>=0?'+':'')+ec.toFixed(2)+'%';
    ['tt-eth','tt-eth2'].forEach(id=>{const e=document.getElementById(id);if(e)e.textContent=eps;});
    const msEth=document.getElementById('ms-eth'); if(msEth) msEth.textContent=eps;
    const mec=document.getElementById('ms-eth-c'); if(mec){mec.textContent=ecs;mec.className='mi-chg '+(ec>=0?'up':'dn');}
    const et=document.getElementById('eth-t1');
    if(et){
      if(ep<2400){et.textContent=`ETH @ ${eps} — in T1 zone. ETH/BTC ratio at historic low. Accumulation zone.`;et.className='trig-detail hit';}
      else{et.textContent=`ETH @ ${eps} — above T1 zone. Wait for BTC confirmation first.`;}
    }
  }
  if(d?.solana){
    const sp=d.solana.usd, sc=d.solana.usd_24h_change;
    const sps='$'+sp.toLocaleString('en-US',{maximumFractionDigits:0});
    const scs=(sc>=0?'+':'')+sc.toFixed(2)+'%';
    ['tt-sol','tt-sol2'].forEach(id=>{const e=document.getElementById(id);if(e)e.textContent=sps;});
    const msSol=document.getElementById('ms-sol'); if(msSol) msSol.textContent=sps;
    const msc=document.getElementById('ms-sol-c'); if(msc){msc.textContent=scs;msc.className='mi-chg '+(sc>=0?'up':'dn');}
    const st=document.getElementById('sol-t1');
    if(st){
      if(sp<130){st.textContent=`SOL @ ${sps} — in T1 entry zone. High beta — size small.`;st.className='trig-detail hit';}
      else{st.textContent=`SOL @ ${sps} — wait for further correction or BTC confirmation.`;}
    }
    const stp=document.getElementById('sol-t1-price'); if(stp&&sp<200) stp.textContent=`$${Math.round(sp*.85).toLocaleString()}–$${Math.round(sp*.95).toLocaleString()}`;
  }
}

// ── Fear & Greed ─────────────────────────────────────
async function loadFearGreed(){
  try{
    const r=await fetch('https://api.alternative.me/fng/?limit=1');
    if(!r.ok) throw new Error('F&G HTTP '+r.status);
    let d; try { d=await r.json(); } catch(_){ throw new Error('F&G parse'); }
    if(d.data?.[0]){
      const val=parseInt(d.data[0].value);
      const lbl=d.data[0].value_classification;
      ST.fearGreed=val; ST.fearGreedLabel=lbl;
      const fgStr=val+' ('+lbl+')';
      ['tt-fg','tt-fg2'].forEach(id=>{const e=document.getElementById(id);if(e)e.textContent=fgStr;});
      const msfg=document.getElementById('ms-fg'); if(msfg) msfg.textContent=fgStr;
      const msfgc=document.getElementById('ms-fg-c'); if(msfgc) msfgc.textContent='';
      setChip('src-fg','ok');
      // BTC trigger 2
      const bt2=document.getElementById('btc-t2'), bfgs=document.getElementById('btc-fg-s');
      if(bt2){
        if(val<=25){bt2.textContent=`Fear & Greed: ${val} — EXTREME FEAR. Capitulation signal confirmed ✓`;bt2.className='trig-detail hit';if(bfgs){bfgs.className='trig-status ts-hit';bfgs.textContent='✓';}}
        else if(val<=40){bt2.textContent=`Fear & Greed: ${val} (${lbl}) — Fear zone. Getting closer to buy signal.`;bt2.className='trig-detail watch';}
        else{bt2.textContent=`Fear & Greed: ${val} (${lbl}) — Not at capitulation. Wait for ≤25.`;}
      }
      // Bottom tracker
      const bfg=document.getElementById('b-fg'), bfgv=document.getElementById('b-fg-val');
      if(bfg&&bfgv){
        bfgv.textContent=val+'/100 — '+lbl;
        if(val<=25){bfg.textContent='EXTREME FEAR';bfg.className='conf-status css-green';}
        else if(val<=45){bfg.textContent='FEAR';bfg.className='conf-status css-amber';}
        else{bfg.textContent='NEUTRAL+';bfg.className='conf-status css-grey';}
      }
    }
  }catch(e){ setChip('src-fg','err'); }
}

// ── Finnhub ───────────────────────────────────────────
async function fhGet(path){
  if(!ST.settings.fh) return null;
  try{
    const r=await fetch(`https://finnhub.io/api/v1/${path}&token=${ST.settings.fh}`);
    if(!r.ok) return null;
    return await r.json();
  }catch(e){ return null; }
}
async function fetchQ(ticker){
  const sym=ticker==='BTC'?'BINANCE:BTCUSDT':ticker==='VIX'?'^VIX':ticker;
  const d=await fhGet(`quote?symbol=${sym}`); if(!d||!d.c) return null;
  // Compute pct safely: prefer dp field, fall back to manual calc if pc>0
  const pct = (d.dp != null && !isNaN(d.dp)) ? d.dp : (d.pc>0 ? (d.c-d.pc)/d.pc*100 : 0);
  return {price:d.c,open:d.o,high:d.h,low:d.l,prev:d.pc,chg:d.d,pct,pc:d.pc,c:d.c,dp:d.dp};
}
// Safe percent display helper
function safePctStr(q) {
  if (!q) return '';
  const p = (q.pct != null && !isNaN(q.pct)) ? q.pct : 0;
  return (p >= 0 ? '+' : '') + p.toFixed(2) + '%';
}
async function fetchAnalyst(t){ return await fhGet(`stock/recommendation?symbol=${t}`); }
async function fetchTarget(t){ return await fhGet(`stock/price-target?symbol=${t}`); }
async function fetchNews(t){ const to=new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];const from=new Date(Date.now()-7*86400000).toISOString().split('T')[0]; return await fhGet(`company-news?symbol=${t}&from=${from}&to=${to}`); }

// ── FRED ──────────────────────────────────────────────
async function fredGet(series){
  if(!ST.settings.fred) return null;
  try{
    const r=await fetch(`https://api.stlouisfed.org/fred/series/observations?series_id=${series}&api_key=${ST.settings.fred}&file_type=json&sort_order=desc&limit=1`);
    const d=await r.json();
    if(d.observations?.[0]) return {value:parseFloat(d.observations[0].value),date:d.observations[0].date};
  }catch(e){}
  return null;
}
async function loadFRED(){
  if(!ST.settings.fred) return;
  const series=['FEDFUNDS','CPIAUCSL','UNRATE','BAMLH0A0HYM2','VIXCLS'];
  const keys=['fedfunds','cpi','unrate','hy','vix'];
  const results=await Promise.all(series.map(s=>fredGet(s)));
  results.forEach((r,i)=>{ if(r) ST.fredData[keys[i]]=r; });
  setChip('src-fred','ok');
  renderFREDMacro();
  if(ST.fredData.fedfunds){ const msfed=document.getElementById('ms-fed'); if(msfed) msfed.textContent=ST.fredData.fedfunds.value.toFixed(2)+'%'; }
  if(ST.fredData.cpi){ const mscpi=document.getElementById('ms-cpi'); if(mscpi) mscpi.textContent=ST.fredData.cpi.value.toFixed(1)+'%'; }
  // VIX from FRED — Finnhub free tier doesn't serve ^VIX
  if(ST.fredData.vix){
    const vv=ST.fredData.vix.value;
    ST.quotes['VIX']={price:vv,c:vv,pct:0,dp:0,pc:vv};
    const msvix=document.getElementById('ms-vix'); if(msvix) msvix.textContent=vv.toFixed(1);
    ['tt-vix','tt-vix2'].forEach(id=>{const e=document.getElementById(id);if(e)e.textContent=vv.toFixed(1);});
  }
}
function renderFREDMacro(){
  const f=ST.fredData;
  if(!Object.keys(f).length) return;
  const badge=document.getElementById('fred-badge'); if(badge){badge.textContent='LIVE';badge.className='tag tb';}
  const items=[
    {id:'fred-fed',vs:'fred-fed-s',val:f.fedfunds?f.fedfunds.value.toFixed(2)+'%':'—',sub:f.fedfunds?(f.fedfunds.value>5?'Restrictive territory':'Neutral-accommodative'):'—',col:f.fedfunds?(f.fedfunds.value>5?'var(--amber)':'var(--green)'):'var(--tx3)'},
    {id:'fred-cpi',vs:'fred-cpi-s',val:f.cpi?f.cpi.value.toFixed(1)+'%':'—',sub:f.cpi?(f.cpi.value>4?'Significantly above 2% target':f.cpi.value>2.5?'Above target — easing':'Near Fed 2% target'):'—',col:f.cpi?(f.cpi.value>4?'var(--red)':f.cpi.value>3?'var(--amber)':'var(--green)'):'var(--tx3)'},
    {id:'fred-unemp',vs:'fred-unemp-s',val:f.unrate?f.unrate.value.toFixed(1)+'%':'—',sub:f.unrate?(f.unrate.value<4?'Tight — Fed under pressure':f.unrate.value<5?'Healthy':'Rising — recession watch'):'—',col:f.unrate?(f.unrate.value<4.5?'var(--green)':'var(--amber)'):'var(--tx3)'},
    {id:'fred-hy',vs:'fred-hy-s',val:f.hy?f.hy.value.toFixed(2)+'%':'—',sub:f.hy?(f.hy.value>5?'STRESS — risk-off':f.hy.value>4?'Widening — watch':'Contained — risk-on'):'—',col:f.hy?(f.hy.value>5?'var(--red)':f.hy.value>4?'var(--amber)':'var(--green)'):'var(--tx3)'},
  ];
  items.forEach(item=>{
    const v=document.getElementById(item.id); if(v){v.textContent=item.val;v.style.color=item.col;}
    const s=document.getElementById(item.vs); if(s) s.textContent=item.sub;
  });
}


// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// REFRESH ALL (from watchlist)
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
async function refreshAll(){
  document.getElementById('rtime').textContent='Refreshing...';
  renderDashContent(true);
  await loadAllData();
  const allT=[...new Set([...S_watchlistTickers(),...VALUE_PICKS.map(p=>p.ticker),...MOON_PICKS.map(p=>p.ticker),...BUZZ_PICKS.map(p=>p.ticker)])];
  await Promise.allSettled(allT.map(async t=>{
    const q=await fetchQ(t); if(q) ST.quotes[t]=q;
  }));
  renderDashContent(false);
  checkAlertTriggers();
  document.getElementById('rtime').textContent='Updated '+new Date().toLocaleTimeString([],{hour:'2-digit',minute:'2-digit'});
  showToast('Markets refreshed ✓');
}
function S_watchlistTickers(){ return ST.watchlist.map(w=>w.ticker); }

function refreshPortfolio(){ loadAllData().catch(e=>console.warn('portfolio refresh:',e)); }

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// MARKET STATUS
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function updateMktStatus(){
  const d=new Date(),h=d.getHours(),m=d.getMinutes(),min=h*60+m;
  const open=d.getDay()>0&&d.getDay()<6&&min>=570&&min<960;
  const dot=document.getElementById('mkt-dot'),txt=document.getElementById('mkt-txt');
  if(dot){ dot.className='mkt-dot'+(open?' open':''); }
  if(txt){ txt.textContent=open?'MARKET OPEN':'MARKET CLOSED'; txt.style.color=open?'var(--green)':'var(--tx3)'; }
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// DASHBOARD RENDERING
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function renderDashContent(loading){
  const el=document.getElementById('dash-content');
  if(!el) return;
  const seg=ST.seg;
  if(seg==='watchlist'){
    el.innerHTML=ST.watchlist.length?ST.watchlist.map(item=>renderWatchCard(item,loading)).join(''):'<div class="empty">NO WATCHLIST ITEMS<br/>ADD IN SETTINGS</div>';
  } else if(seg==='value'){
    el.innerHTML=`<div class="tier-hdr"><div class="tier-pill" style="color:var(--blue);border-color:var(--bbrd);background:var(--bdim)">2× VALUE PICKS</div><div class="tier-line"></div></div><div class="tier-desc">Fundamentally underpriced stocks analysts expect to at least double. Strong balance sheets, real earnings, selling at deep discounts to peers.</div>${VALUE_PICKS.map(p=>renderPickCard(p,loading)).join('')}`;
  } else if(seg==='moon'){
    el.innerHTML=`<div class="tier-hdr"><div class="tier-pill" style="color:var(--purple);border-color:var(--pbrd);background:var(--pdim)">🚀 MOONSHOTS · 100×+</div><div class="tier-line"></div></div><div class="tier-desc">Extreme high-risk, extreme high-reward. Quantum computing, space, robotics, post-quantum security. Size these like lottery tickets — small positions, full-loss tolerance.</div>${MOON_PICKS.map(p=>renderPickCard(p,loading)).join('')}`;
  } else if(seg==='buzz'){
    el.innerHTML=`<div class="tier-hdr"><div class="tier-pill" style="color:var(--amber);border-color:var(--abrd);background:var(--adim)">🔥 MARKET BUZZ</div><div class="tier-line"></div></div><div class="tier-desc">What analysts, funds, and Wall Street are focused on in 2026. Momentum leaders with real institutional backing.</div>${BUZZ_PICKS.map(p=>renderPickCard(p,loading)).join('')}`;
  }
}

function renderWatchCard(item,loading){
  const isCG={BTC:'bitcoin',ETH:'ethereum',SOL:'solana',AVAX:'avalanche-2',BNB:'binancecoin'};
  const cgKey = isCG[item.ticker];
  const cgData = cgKey ? (ST.cryptoData?.[cgKey] || ST.crypto?.[cgKey]) : null;
  const q = cgData
    ? {price: cgData.usd, pct: cgData.usd_24h_change, c: cgData.usd}
    : ST.quotes[item.ticker];
  const score=loading?50:calcScore(ST.sigChecks[item.ticker]||{},item.profile||'moonshot');
  const isProfitReady=q&&item.buyPrice&&((q.price-item.buyPrice)/item.buyPrice*100)>=ST.settings.threshold;
  const isAlert=q&&Math.abs(q.pct||0)>=15;
  const profColor=item.profile==='moonshot'?'var(--purple)':item.profile==='preservation'?'var(--green)':'var(--blue)';
  const wlIdx=ST.watchlist.indexOf(item);
  return `<div class="card ${isAlert?'c-alert':''} ${isProfitReady&&!isAlert?'c-profit':''} fade-in" onclick="openDetail('${item.ticker}')">
    <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:flex-start">
      <div style="flex:1;min-width:0">
        <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px;margin-bottom:3px">
          <div class="c-ticker">${item.ticker}</div>
          <button onclick="event.stopPropagation();removeWatchTicker(${wlIdx})" style="background:none;border:none;color:var(--tx4);font-size:16px;line-height:1;cursor:pointer;padding:0;margin-left:auto;opacity:0.5;flex-shrink:0">×</button>
        </div>
        <div class="c-name">${item.name}</div>
        <div class="c-sector" style="color:${profColor};border-color:${profColor}40;background:${profColor}12">${(item.profile||'BALANCED').toUpperCase()}</div>
      </div>
      <div style="text-align:right;flex-shrink:0;margin-left:12px">
        ${loading?'<div class="shim" style="width:68px;margin-bottom:5px"></div><div class="shim" style="width:48px"></div>':''}
        ${!loading&&q?`<div class="c-price">${fp(q.price,item.ticker)}</div><div class="c-chg ${q.pct>=0?'up':'dn'}">${safePctStr(q)}</div>`:''}
        ${!loading&&!q?`<div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:9px;color:var(--tx3)">${(ST.lastClose&&ST.lastClose[item.ticker])?fmtPrice(ST.lastClose[item.ticker].price,item.ticker)+' ✦':'—'}</div>`:''}
      </div>
    </div>
    ${!loading&&q?`<div class="c-bar-wrap" style="margin-top:10px"><div class="c-bar-row"><span>SIGNAL SCORE</span><span>${scoreVerdict(score.score)}</span></div><div class="c-bar"><div class="c-bar-fill" style="width:${score.score}%;background:${score.score>=60?'var(--green)':score.score>=40?'var(--amber)':'var(--red)'}"></div></div></div>`:''}
    <div class="c-tags" style="margin-top:8px">
      ${isAlert?`<span class="tag ${q.pct>0?'tg':'tr'}">⚡ ${q.pct>0?'+':''}${q.pct?.toFixed(0)}% MOVE</span>`:''}
      ${isProfitReady?`<span class="tag ta">💰 PROFIT TARGET +${Math.round((q.price-item.buyPrice)/item.buyPrice*100)}%</span>`:''}
      ${q&&!isAlert?`<span class="tag ${q.pct>=0?'tg':'tr'}">${q.pct>=0?'▲':'▼'} ${Math.abs(q.pct||0).toFixed(1)}%</span>`:''}
      <span class="tag tb">TAP TO ANALYZE →</span>
      <span class="tag tb" onclick="event.stopPropagation();openChart('${item.ticker}')" style="cursor:pointer">📈 CHART</span>
    </div>
    ${item.buyPrice&&q?`<div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:9px;color:${q.price>=item.buyPrice?'var(--green)':'var(--red)'};margin-top:8px;padding-top:8px;border-top:1px solid var(--b1)">P&L: ${((q.price-item.buyPrice)/item.buyPrice*100).toFixed(1)}% from ${fp(item.buyPrice,item.ticker)}</div>`:''}</div>`;
}


function renderPickCard(pick,loading){
  const q=ST.quotes[pick.ticker];
  const inWL=ST.watchlist.some(w=>w.ticker===pick.ticker);
  return `<div class="card c-hot fade-in" onclick="openDetail('${pick.ticker}')">
    <div class="card-top">
      <div style="flex:1;padding-right:78px">
        <div class="c-ticker">${pick.ticker}</div>
        <div class="c-name">${pick.name}</div>
        <div class="c-sector" style="color:${pick.color};border-color:${pick.color}40;background:${pick.color}12;font-size:7.5px">${pick.sector}</div>
      </div>
      <div style="text-align:right">
        ${loading?`<div class="shim" style="width:62px;margin-bottom:4px"></div>`:`<div class="c-price" style="font-size:14px">${q?fp(q.price,pick.ticker):'—'}</div>`}
        ${q&&!loading?`<div class="c-chg ${q.pct>=0?'up':'dn'}">${safePctStr(q)}</div>`:''}
        <div style="font-family:var(--f1);font-size:16px;letter-spacing:2px;color:${pick.color};margin-top:5px">${pick.upside}</div>
        <div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:7.5px;color:var(--tx3)">UPSIDE</div>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div class="c-why">${pick.why}</div>
    <div class="c-tags" style="margin-top:7px">
      ${(pick.tags||[]).map(t=>`<span class="tag ${t}">${t==='tg'?'BULL SETUP':t==='tr'?'HIGH RISK':t==='ta'?'CATALYST':t==='tb'?'ANALYST':t==='tp'?'MOONSHOT':t==='tc'?'HOT SECTOR':t==='tgold'?'RWA':''}</span>`).join('')}
      <span class="tag" style="color:${pick.risk==='Extreme'?'var(--red)':pick.risk?.includes('Very')?'var(--red)':pick.risk==='High'?'var(--amber)':pick.risk==='Medium'?'var(--blue)':'var(--green)'}">RISK: ${pick.risk?.toUpperCase()}</span>
    </div>
    <div style="display:flex;gap:6px;margin-top:8px">
    ${!inWL?`<div class="add-wl" onclick="event.stopPropagation();addToWL('${pick.ticker}','${pick.name}')" style="position:static;flex:1;text-align:center">+ WATCHLIST</div>`:'<div class="add-wl" style="position:static;flex:1;text-align:center;color:var(--tx3);border-color:var(--b2);background:transparent">✓ WATCHLIST</div>'}
    <div class="add-wl" onclick="event.stopPropagation();openChart('${pick.ticker}')" style="position:static;color:var(--blue);border-color:var(--bbrd);background:var(--bdim)">📈 CHART</div>
  </div>
  </div>`;
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// ALERT TRIGGERS
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function checkAlertTriggers(){
  const newAlerts=[];
  const allItems=[...ST.watchlist,...VALUE_PICKS,...MOON_PICKS,...BUZZ_PICKS];
  allItems.forEach(item=>{
    const q=ST.quotes[item.ticker||item.t]; if(!q) return;
    const p=q.pct||0, now=new Date().toLocaleString(), t=item.ticker||item.t;
    if(Math.abs(p)>=15){
      const dedup=ST.alerts.find(a=>a.ticker===t&&a.trigger.includes('MOVE')&&Date.now()-new Date(a.rawTime||0).getTime()<1800000);
      if(dedup) return;
      newAlerts.push({
        id:Date.now()+Math.random(), ticker:t, type:p>0?'buy':'sell', rawTime:Date.now(),
        trigger:(p>0?'SURGE ':'DROP ')+Math.abs(p).toFixed(0)+'%',
        body:p>0
          ?`${t} surged ${p.toFixed(1)}% today. Check if volume confirms or if this is hype-driven. Staged profit-taking if in position.`
          :`${t} dropped ${p.toFixed(1)}%. Watch for support. Could be panic entry if fundamentals intact.`,
        price:q.price, name:item.name||item.n||t, time:now,
        chips:p>0
          ?[{l:'T1 SELL',v:fp(q.price*1.25,t)},{l:'T2 SELL',v:fp(q.price*1.6,t)},{l:'LET RIDE',v:fp(q.price*2.5,t)}]
          :[{l:'ENTRY 1',v:fp(q.price,t)},{l:'ENTRY 2',v:fp(q.price*.93,t)},{l:'ENTRY 3',v:fp(q.price*.86,t)}],
      });
    }
    if(item.buyPrice&&q.price){
      const gain=(q.price-item.buyPrice)/item.buyPrice*100;
      if(gain>=ST.settings.threshold){
        const dedup=ST.alerts.find(a=>a.ticker===t&&a.trigger.includes('PROFIT')&&Date.now()-new Date(a.rawTime||0).getTime()<3600000);
        if(dedup) return;
        newAlerts.push({
          id:Date.now()+Math.random(), ticker:t, type:'sell', rawTime:Date.now(),
          trigger:'PROFIT TARGET +'+Math.round(gain)+'%',
          body:`${t} is up ${gain.toFixed(0)}% from your cost basis ${fp(item.buyPrice,t)}. Consider staged profit-taking to lock in gains while preserving long-term CGT treatment.`,
          price:q.price, name:item.name||t, time:now,
          chips:[{l:'SELL 25%',v:fp(q.price,t)},{l:'SELL 35%',v:fp(q.price*1.12,t)},{l:'LET RIDE',v:fp(q.price*1.5,t)}],
        });
      }
    }
  });
  if(newAlerts.length){
    ST.alerts=[...newAlerts,...ST.alerts].slice(0,60);
    try{ localStorage.setItem('forge_al',JSON.stringify(ST.alerts)); }catch(e){}
    const _ap=document.getElementById('alert-pip'); if(_ap) _ap.style.display='block';
    renderAlerts();
    newAlerts.forEach(a=>sendPush(a.ticker,a.trigger+': '+a.body).catch(()=>{}));
  }
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// ALERTS SCREEN
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function renderAlerts(){
  const el=document.getElementById('alerts-content'); if(!el) return;
  if(!ST.alerts.length){
    el.innerHTML=`<div class="al-empty"><div class="al-empty-ico">◎</div><div class="al-empty-txt">NO ALERTS YET<br/>REFRESH MARKETS TO SCAN<br/>TRIGGERS APPEAR HERE ONLY<br/>WHEN SOMETHING REAL HAPPENS</div></div>`;
    return;
  }
  el.innerHTML=ST.alerts.map(a=>`<div class="al-item fade-in" style="border-color:${a.type==='buy'?'var(--green)':a.type==='sell'?'var(--amber)':'var(--red)'}">
    <div class="al-hdr"><div class="al-ticker">${a.ticker}</div><div class="al-time">${a.time}</div></div>
    <div class="al-trigger" style="color:${a.type==='buy'?'var(--green)':'var(--amber)'}">${a.trigger}</div>
    <div class="al-body">${a.body}</div>
    <div class="al-chips">${(a.chips||[]).map(c=>`<div class="al-chip"><div class="al-chip-l">${c.l}</div><div class="al-chip-v" style="color:var(--amber)">${c.v}</div></div>`).join('')}</div>
  </div>`).join('');
}
function clearAlerts(){ ST.alerts=[]; try{localStorage.removeItem('forge_al');}catch(e){} const _apn=document.getElementById('alert-pip'); if(_apn) _apn.style.display='none'; renderAlerts(); }

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// ANALYSIS PICKER
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function renderAnalysisPicker(){
  const el=document.getElementById('analysis-picker'); if(!el) return;
  el.innerHTML=`<div style="padding:10px 14px 4px;font-family:var(--f2);font-size:8px;color:var(--tx3);letter-spacing:2px">MY WATCHLIST</div>`
    +ST.watchlist.map(item=>{
      const isCr={BTC:'bitcoin',ETH:'ethereum',SOL:'solana'};
      let q=ST.quotes[item.ticker];
      if(!q&&isCr[item.ticker]){const cd=ST.cryptoData?.[isCr[item.ticker]];if(cd)q={price:cd.usd,pct:cd.usd_24h_change,c:cd.usd};}
      return `<div onclick="openDetail('${item.ticker}')" style="background:var(--bg1);border:1px solid var(--b1);border-radius:8px;padding:13px;margin:0 14px 9px;cursor:pointer;display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center;transition:border-color .2s" onmouseover="this.style.borderColor='var(--b3)'" onmouseout="this.style.borderColor='var(--b1)'">
        <div><div style="font-family:var(--f1);font-size:20px;letter-spacing:3px">${item.ticker}</div><div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:8.5px;color:var(--tx3);margin-top:2px">${item.name}</div></div>
        <div style="text-align:right">
          <div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:15px">${q?fp(q.price,item.ticker):'—'}</div>
          ${q?`<div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:9px;color:${q.pct>=0?'var(--green)':'var(--red)'}">${safePctStr(q)}</div>`:''}
        </div>
      </div>`;
    }).join('')
    +`<div style="padding:10px 14px 4px;font-family:var(--f2);font-size:8px;color:var(--tx3);letter-spacing:2px">ALL PICKS — TAP TO ANALYZE</div>`
    +[...VALUE_PICKS,...MOON_PICKS,...BUZZ_PICKS].slice(0,12).map(p=>`<div onclick="openDetail('${p.ticker}')" style="background:var(--bg1);border:1px solid var(--b1);border-radius:8px;padding:11px;margin:0 14px 7px;cursor:pointer;display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center">
      <div><div style="font-family:var(--f1);font-size:16px;letter-spacing:2px;color:${p.color}">${p.ticker}</div><div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:8px;color:var(--tx3)">${p.sector}</div></div>
      <div style="text-align:right"><div style="font-family:var(--f1);font-size:14px;color:${p.color}">${p.upside}</div><div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:8px;color:var(--tx3)">UPSIDE</div></div>
    </div>`).join('');
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// DETAIL PANEL
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
async function openDetail(ticker){
  ticker=ticker.toUpperCase();
  document.getElementById('d-ticker').textContent=ticker;
  document.getElementById('d-name').textContent='Loading...';
  document.getElementById('detail').classList.add('open');
  document.getElementById('d-body').innerHTML=`<div style="padding:40px;text-align:center"><span class="ldot"></span><span class="ldot"></span><span class="ldot"></span></div>`;
  const item=ST.watchlist.find(w=>w.ticker===ticker)||VALUE_PICKS.find(p=>p.ticker===ticker)||MOON_PICKS.find(p=>p.ticker===ticker)||BUZZ_PICKS.find(p=>p.ticker===ticker)||{ticker,name:ticker,profile:'balanced'};
  const [q,analyst,target,news]=await Promise.all([fetchQ(ticker),fetchAnalyst(ticker),fetchTarget(ticker),fetchNews(ticker)]);
  if(q) ST.quotes[ticker]=q;
  document.getElementById('d-name').textContent=(item.name||ticker)+(item.upside?` · ${item.upside} UPSIDE`:'');
  renderDetailBody(ticker,item,q,analyst,target,news,ST.sigChecks[ticker]||{},'volume');
}

function renderDetailBody(ticker,item,q,analyst,target,news,checks,activeTab){
  const pickData=VALUE_PICKS.find(p=>p.ticker===ticker)||MOON_PICKS.find(p=>p.ticker===ticker)||BUZZ_PICKS.find(p=>p.ticker===ticker);
  const score=calcScore(checks,item.profile||'balanced');
  const wlItem=ST.watchlist.find(w=>w.ticker===ticker);
  const pnl=wlItem?.buyPrice&&q?((q.price-wlItem.buyPrice)/wlItem.buyPrice*100):null;
  const isLT=false; // Would calc from entryDate if we had it
  let html='';

  // Verdict
  html+=`<div class="v-score-wrap">
    <div class="v-score" style="color:${score.color}">${score.score}</div>
    <div class="v-label" style="color:${score.color}">${score.verdict}</div>
    <div class="v-action">${score.action}</div>
    <div class="bull-bear">
      <span style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:9.5px;color:var(--green)">↑ ${score.bull} BULL</span>
      <span style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:9.5px;color:var(--red)">↓ ${score.bear} BEAR</span>
    </div>
  </div>`;

  // Price grid
  if(q) html+=`<div class="sec"><div class="sec-title">LIVE DATA</div>
    <div class="grid2">
      <div class="lbox"><div class="lbox-l">PRICE</div><div class="lbox-v">${fp(q.price,ticker)}</div></div>
      <div class="lbox"><div class="lbox-l">TODAY</div><div class="lbox-v" style="color:${q.pct>=0?'var(--green)':'var(--red)'}">${safePctStr(q)}</div></div>
      <div class="lbox"><div class="lbox-l">DAY HIGH</div><div class="lbox-v up" style="font-size:14px">${fp(q.high,ticker)}</div></div>
      <div class="lbox"><div class="lbox-l">DAY LOW</div><div class="lbox-v dn" style="font-size:14px">${fp(q.low,ticker)}</div></div>
      <div class="lbox"><div class="lbox-l">OPEN</div><div class="lbox-v" style="font-size:14px">${fp(q.open,ticker)}</div></div>
      <div class="lbox"><div class="lbox-l">PREV CLOSE</div><div class="lbox-v" style="font-size:14px">${fp(q.prev,ticker)}</div></div>
      ${pnl!=null?`<div class="lbox" style="grid-column:1/-1"><div class="lbox-l">P&L FROM COST ${fp(wlItem.buyPrice,ticker)}</div><div class="lbox-v" style="color:${pnl>=0?'var(--green)':'var(--red)'}"> ${pnl>=0?'+':''}${pnl.toFixed(1)}%</div></div>`:''}
    </div>
  </div>`;

  // Thesis
  if(pickData?.thesis) html+=`<div class="sec"><div class="sec-title">INVESTMENT THESIS</div><div style="font-family:var(--f3);font-size:12.5px;color:var(--tx2);line-height:1.7">${pickData.thesis}</div></div>`;

  // Analyst data
  if(analyst?.length||target?.targetMean){
    const rec=analyst?.[0]||null;
    html+=`<div class="sec"><div class="sec-title">ANALYST CONSENSUS</div>`;
    if(rec) html+=`<div style="display:flex;gap:5px;flex-wrap:wrap;margin-bottom:10px">
      <span class="tag tg">STRONG BUY: ${rec.strongBuy||0}</span>
      <span class="tag tg">BUY: ${rec.buy||0}</span>
      <span class="tag ta">HOLD: ${rec.hold||0}</span>
      <span class="tag tr">SELL: ${rec.sell||0}</span>
    </div>`;
    if(target?.targetMean){
      const up=q?((target.targetMean-q.price)/q.price*100):0;
      html+=`<div class="grid2">
        <div class="lbox"><div class="lbox-l">MEAN TARGET</div><div class="lbox-v" style="color:var(--amber)">${fp(target.targetMean,ticker)}</div><div class="lbox-n">${up>=0?'+':''}${up.toFixed(0)}% upside</div></div>
        <div class="lbox"><div class="lbox-l">HIGH TARGET</div><div class="lbox-v" style="color:var(--green)">${fp(target.targetHigh,ticker)}</div></div>
        <div class="lbox"><div class="lbox-l">LOW TARGET</div><div class="lbox-v" style="color:var(--red)">${fp(target.targetLow,ticker)}</div></div>
        <div class="lbox"><div class="lbox-l"># ANALYSTS</div><div class="lbox-v">${target.numberOfAnalysts||'—'}</div></div>
      </div>`;
    }
    html+=`</div>`;
  }

  // Price Projections
  if(q){
    const p=q.price;
    const b=pickData?.upside?.includes('100')?100:pickData?.upside?.includes('50')?50:pickData?.upside?.includes('10')?10:2.5;
    const bullP=target?.targetHigh||fp(p*b,ticker);
    const baseP=target?.targetMean||fp(p*1.5,ticker);
    html+=`<div class="sec"><div class="sec-title">PRICE PROJECTIONS</div>
      <div class="proj-card">
        <div class="proj-row"><span class="proj-pill tg" style="background:var(--gdim)">BULL</span><div><div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:14px;color:var(--green)">${typeof bullP==='number'?fp(bullP,ticker):bullP}</div><div style="font-family:var(--f3);font-size:10.5px;color:var(--tx3);margin-top:1px">${pickData?.bull||'Strong catalyst + momentum drives full re-rating.'}</div></div></div>
        <div class="proj-row"><span class="proj-pill tb" style="background:var(--bdim)">BASE</span><div><div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:14px;color:var(--blue)">${typeof baseP==='number'?fp(baseP,ticker):baseP}</div><div style="font-family:var(--f3);font-size:10.5px;color:var(--tx3);margin-top:1px">Gradual appreciation as market recognizes value.</div></div></div>
        <div class="proj-row"><span class="proj-pill tr" style="background:var(--rdim)">BEAR</span><div><div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:14px;color:var(--red)">${fp(p*.6,ticker)}</div><div style="font-family:var(--f3);font-size:10.5px;color:var(--tx3);margin-top:1px">${pickData?.bear||'Headwinds persist — stop-loss reference.'}</div></div></div>
      </div>
    </div>`;
  }

  // Profit taking levels
  if(q){
    const p=q.price, isOTC=p<1;
    const t1=isOTC?fp(p*2,ticker):target?fp(target.targetMean*.85,ticker):fp(p*1.25,ticker);
    const t2=isOTC?fp(p*5,ticker):target?fp(target.targetMean,ticker):fp(p*1.6,ticker);
    const t3=isOTC?fp(p*10,ticker):target?fp(target.targetHigh,ticker):fp(p*2.5,ticker);
    html+=`<div class="sec"><div class="sec-title">PROFIT TAKING LEVELS</div>
      <div class="lv-row" style="border-color:var(--green)"><div class="lv-num">T1</div><div class="lv-info"><div class="lv-price">${t1}</div><div class="lv-desc">${isOTC?'First double — recover cost basis':'Conservative first target'}</div></div><div class="lv-size">SELL 33%</div></div>
      <div class="lv-row" style="border-color:var(--amber)"><div class="lv-num">T2</div><div class="lv-info"><div class="lv-price">${t2}</div><div class="lv-desc">${isOTC?'Strong run — take majority off':'Analyst mean target'}</div></div><div class="lv-size">SELL 33%</div></div>
      <div class="lv-row" style="border-color:var(--purple)"><div class="lv-num">T3</div><div class="lv-info"><div class="lv-price">${t3}</div><div class="lv-desc">Bull case — let remainder run free</div></div><div class="lv-size">HOLD 34%</div></div>
    </div>`;
  }

  // Entry levels
  if(q){
    const p=q.price;
    html+=`<div class="sec"><div class="sec-title">STAGED ENTRY ZONES</div>
      <div class="lv-row" style="border-color:var(--b2)"><div class="lv-num">01</div><div class="lv-info"><div class="lv-price">${fp(p,ticker)}</div><div class="lv-desc">${score.score>=60?'Current — strong enough to enter':'Only if catalyst confirms'}</div></div><div class="lv-size">25%</div></div>
      <div class="lv-row" style="border-color:var(--b2)"><div class="lv-num">02</div><div class="lv-info"><div class="lv-price">${fp(p*.94,ticker)}</div><div class="lv-desc">First pullback — add if volume holds</div></div><div class="lv-size">35%</div></div>
      <div class="lv-row" style="border-color:var(--b2)"><div class="lv-num">03</div><div class="lv-info"><div class="lv-price">${fp(p*.87,ticker)}</div><div class="lv-desc">Deeper support — complete position</div></div><div class="lv-size">40%</div></div>
      <div style="margin-top:10px;padding:11px;background:var(--bg2);border-radius:8px;font-family:var(--f3);font-size:11px;color:var(--tx3);line-height:1.7">💡 Stage entries — never go all-in. For moonshots, size so you can survive total loss. Always preserve long-term CGT treatment (hold 1yr+).</div>
    </div>`;
  }

  // Tax note
  if(wlItem?.buyPrice&&q){
    const gain=q.price-wlItem.buyPrice;
    const gainPct=((gain/wlItem.buyPrice)*100).toFixed(1);
    const taxST=Math.round(gain*0.37);
    const taxLT=Math.round(gain*0.238);
    const saving=taxST-taxLT;
    html+=`<div class="sec"><div class="sec-title">TAX CALCULATOR — US EXPAT</div>
      <div class="grid2">
        <div class="lbox"><div class="lbox-l">UNREALIZED P&L</div><div class="lbox-v" style="color:${gain>=0?'var(--green)':'var(--red)'}">${gain>=0?'+':''}${gainPct}%</div></div>
        <div class="lbox"><div class="lbox-l">SHORT-TERM TAX (37%)</div><div class="lbox-v" style="color:var(--red)">$${Math.abs(taxST).toLocaleString()}</div></div>
        <div class="lbox"><div class="lbox-l">LONG-TERM TAX (23.8%)</div><div class="lbox-v" style="color:var(--green)">$${Math.abs(taxLT).toLocaleString()}</div></div>
        <div class="lbox"><div class="lbox-l">TAX SAVING (LT vs ST)</div><div class="lbox-v" style="color:var(--gold)">$${Math.abs(saving).toLocaleString()}</div><div class="lbox-n">Hold 1yr+ to save this</div></div>
      </div>
      <div style="margin-top:9px;padding:9px;background:var(--bdim);border:1px solid var(--bbrd);border-radius:6px;font-family:var(--f2);font-size:8.5px;color:var(--blue);line-height:1.7">UAE: 0% CGT on non-US assets · US expat: worldwide income applies · Plan exits around 1-year anniversary</div>
    </div>`;
  }

  // News
  if(news?.length) html+=`<div class="sec"><div class="sec-title">RECENT NEWS</div>${news.slice(0,5).map(n=>`<div class="news-item"><div class="news-src">${n.source||'NEWS'}</div><div class="news-hed">${n.headline||'—'}</div><div class="news-t">${n.datetime?new Date(n.datetime*1000).toLocaleString():'—'}</div></div>`).join('')}</div>`;

  // Cost basis setter
  html+=`<div class="sec"><div class="sec-title">MY COST BASIS</div>
    <div style="font-family:var(--f3);font-size:11px;color:var(--tx3);margin-bottom:7px">Set your avg buy price to track P&L and enable profit alerts</div>
    <div class="cb-row"><input class="cb-inp" id="cb-inp" placeholder="Avg cost basis" type="number" step="any" value="${wlItem?.buyPrice||''}"/><button class="ph-btn g" onclick="saveCostBasis('${ticker}')">SET</button></div>
  </div>`;

  // Signal checklist
  html+=`<div class="sec"><div class="sec-title">SIGNAL CHECKLIST — ${ticker}</div>
    <div class="pills" id="sig-pills">${SIGNAL_GROUPS.map(g=>`<div class="pill ${activeTab===g.id?'on':''}" onclick="switchSigTab('${ticker}','${g.id}')">${g.label}</div>`).join('')}</div>
    ${SIGNAL_GROUPS.filter(g=>g.id===activeTab).map(g=>`
      <div class="sig-gh">↑ BULLISH SIGNALS</div>
      ${g.signals.filter(s=>s.bull).map(s=>`<div class="sig-item" onclick="toggleSig('${ticker}','${s.id}','${activeTab}')">
        <div class="sig-chk ${checks[s.id]?'chk-bull':''}">${checks[s.id]?'<svg width="8" height="8" viewBox="0 0 8 8"><polyline points="1.5,4 3,5.5 6.5,2" fill="none" stroke="var(--green)" stroke-width="1.5"/></svg>':''}</div>
        <div class="sig-lbl ${checks[s.id]?'on':''}">${s.label}</div>
        <div class="sig-dir up">↑</div>
      </div>`).join('')}
      <div class="sig-gh" style="margin-top:9px">↓ BEARISH SIGNALS</div>
      ${g.signals.filter(s=>!s.bull).map(s=>`<div class="sig-item" onclick="toggleSig('${ticker}','${s.id}','${activeTab}')">
        <div class="sig-chk ${checks[s.id]?'chk-bear':''}">${checks[s.id]?'<svg width="8" height="8" viewBox="0 0 8 8"><polyline points="1.5,4 3,5.5 6.5,2" fill="none" stroke="var(--red)" stroke-width="1.5"/></svg>':''}</div>
        <div class="sig-lbl ${checks[s.id]?'on':''}">${s.label}</div>
        <div class="sig-dir dn">↓</div>
      </div>`).join('')}
    `).join('')}
    <button onclick="openDetail('${ticker}')" style="width:100%;margin-top:12px;padding:13px;background:var(--green);color:#000;border:none;border-radius:8px;font-family:var(--f1);font-size:16px;letter-spacing:3px;cursor:pointer">↻ RESCORE WITH LIVE DATA</button>
  </div>`;

  if(!wlItem) html+=`<div style="padding:0 14px 14px"><button onclick="addToWL('${ticker}','${item.name||ticker}')" style="width:100%;padding:12px;background:transparent;color:var(--green);border:1px solid var(--gbrd);border-radius:8px;font-family:var(--f2);font-size:9px;letter-spacing:2px;cursor:pointer">+ ADD TO WATCHLIST</button></div>`;
  html+=`<div style="height:16px"></div>`;

  document.getElementById('d-body').innerHTML=html;
}

function closeDetail(){ document.getElementById('detail').classList.remove('open'); }
document.addEventListener('keydown',e=>{ if(e.key==='Escape') closeDetail(); });

function switchSigTab(ticker,tab){
  const item=ST.watchlist.find(w=>w.ticker===ticker)||{ticker,name:ticker,profile:'balanced'};
  const q=ST.quotes[ticker]; const analyst=null; const target=null; const news=null;
  renderDetailBody(ticker,item,q,analyst,target,news,ST.sigChecks[ticker]||{},tab);
}
function toggleSig(ticker,id,tab){
  if(!ST.sigChecks[ticker]) ST.sigChecks[ticker]={};
  ST.sigChecks[ticker][id]=!ST.sigChecks[ticker][id];
  try{ localStorage.setItem('forge_sc',JSON.stringify(ST.sigChecks)); }catch(e){}
  const item=ST.watchlist.find(w=>w.ticker===ticker)||{ticker,name:ticker,profile:'balanced'};
  const q=ST.quotes[ticker];
  renderDetailBody(ticker,item,q,null,null,null,ST.sigChecks[ticker],tab);
}
function saveCostBasis(ticker){
  const v=parseFloat(document.getElementById('cb-inp')?.value); if(isNaN(v)||v<=0) return;
  let item=ST.watchlist.find(w=>w.ticker===ticker);
  if(!item){ addToWL(ticker,ticker); item=ST.watchlist.find(w=>w.ticker===ticker); }
  item.buyPrice=v; try{ localStorage.setItem('forge_wl',JSON.stringify(ST.watchlist)); if(typeof renderTAAssetRow==='function' && TA_S && TA_S.taInited) renderTAAssetRow(); }catch(e){}
  showToast('Cost basis saved ✓'); openDetail(ticker);
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SCORING ENGINE
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function calcScore(checks,profile){
  const weights={
    moonshot:{volume:.25,momentum:.20,catalyst:.20,structure:.10,technical:.15,macro:.10},
    balanced:{volume:.15,momentum:.20,catalyst:.15,structure:.10,technical:.25,macro:.15},
    preservation:{volume:.10,momentum:.15,catalyst:.10,structure:.05,technical:.30,macro:.30},
  };
  const w=weights[profile]||weights.balanced;
  let bull=0,bear=0;
  SIGNAL_GROUPS.forEach(g=>{ g.signals.forEach(s=>{ if(checks[s.id]){ const wt=w[g.id]||.1; s.bull?bull+=wt:bear+=wt; } }); });
  const tot=bull+bear, raw=tot>0?(bull/tot)*100:50;
  const sc=Math.max(0,Math.min(100,Math.round(raw)));
  const bullCnt=SIGNAL_GROUPS.flatMap(g=>g.signals).filter(s=>checks[s.id]&&s.bull).length;
  const bearCnt=SIGNAL_GROUPS.flatMap(g=>g.signals).filter(s=>checks[s.id]&&!s.bull).length;
  let v,c,a;
  if(sc>=75){v='STRONG BUY';c='var(--green)';a='High conviction. Stage in across 3 tranches. Size per your risk profile.';}
  else if(sc>=60){v='SPECULATIVE BUY';c='#aaff00';a='Asymmetric setup forming. Small starter. Add on confirmation.';}
  else if(sc>=45){v='WATCH LIST';c='var(--amber)';a='Mixed signals. Set alerts. Wait for catalyst or volume breakout.';}
  else if(sc>=30){v='CAUTION';c='#ff8800';a='More bearish than bullish. Avoid new entries.';}
  else{v='AVOID';c='var(--red)';a='Do not enter. High risk environment for this asset.';}
  return{score:sc,verdict:v,color:c,action:a,bull:bullCnt,bear:bearCnt};
}
function scoreVerdict(s){ if(s>=75)return'STRONG BUY'; if(s>=60)return'BUY'; if(s>=45)return'WATCH'; if(s>=30)return'CAUTION'; return'AVOID'; }

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// DEPLOY SCORE
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function updateDeployScore(){
  let signals=0;
  // UNH: 2 confirmed (price + oversold)
  signals+=2;
  // BTC fear
  if(ST.fearGreed&&ST.fearGreed<=30) signals+=1;
  // BTC in zone
  if(ST.btcPrice&&ST.btcPrice<68000) signals+=1;

  const total=6, pct=Math.round((signals/total)*100);
  const arc=document.getElementById('scoreArc');
  if(arc){ const len=201.1; arc.setAttribute('stroke-dashoffset',len-(len*pct/100)); }
  const sn=document.getElementById('scoreNum'); if(sn) sn.textContent=pct;
  const title=document.getElementById('scoreTitle'), sub=document.getElementById('scoreSub'), btn=document.getElementById('scoreBtn');
  const bb=document.getElementById('btbot-badge'); if(bb) bb.textContent=signals+' / '+total+' HIT';
  if(pct>=67){
    if(title) title.textContent='DEPLOY AGGRESSIVELY';
    if(arc) arc.setAttribute('stroke','var(--green)');
    if(btn){btn.style.borderColor='var(--green)';btn.style.color='var(--green)';}
    if(sub) sub.textContent=`${signals}/${total} signals confirmed. Multiple high-conviction signals aligned. Deploy in staged tranches.`;
  } else if(pct>=40){
    if(title) title.textContent='BEGIN ACCUMULATING';
    if(arc) arc.setAttribute('stroke','var(--amber)');
    if(btn){btn.style.borderColor='var(--amber)';btn.style.color='var(--amber)';}
    if(sub) sub.textContent=`${signals}/${total} signals hit. Some signals aligning. Small tranches only. Keep 60%+ in cash.`;
  } else {
    if(title) title.textContent='PRESERVE CAPITAL';
    if(arc) arc.setAttribute('stroke','var(--tx3)');
    if(btn){btn.style.borderColor='var(--tx3)';btn.style.color='var(--tx3)';}
    if(sub) sub.textContent=`${signals}/${total} signals confirmed. Market is risk-off. Protect $475K cash. Do not chase.`;
  }
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// FULL SCAN
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
async function runFullScan(){
  if(ST.scanning) return;
  ST.scanning=true;
  const btn=document.getElementById('scan-txt'), spin=document.getElementById('scan-spin');
  if(btn) btn.textContent='SCANNING…';
  if(spin) spin.style.display='inline-block';
  await loadAllData();
  await runMoonshotScan();
  const t=new Date().toLocaleTimeString();
  const ls=document.getElementById('last-scan-time'); if(ls) ls.textContent=t;
  if(btn) btn.textContent='⟳ SCAN';
  if(spin) spin.style.display='none';
  ST.scanning=false;
  showToast('Scan complete ✓');
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// DATE HELPER
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function todayStr(){
  return new Date().toLocaleDateString('en-US',{weekday:'long',month:'long',day:'numeric',year:'numeric'});
}
function monthYearStr(){
  return new Date().toLocaleDateString('en-US',{month:'long',year:'numeric'});
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// AI CALLER
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
async function callAI(system,userMsg,useSearch=true){
  const key=ST.settings.ak;
  const headers={'Content-Type':'application/json','anthropic-version':'2023-06-01','anthropic-dangerous-direct-browser-access':'true'};
  if(key) headers['x-api-key']=key;
  const body={model:'claude-sonnet-4-20250514',max_tokens:1000,system,messages:[{role:'user',content:userMsg}]};
  // web_search tool removed - use model knowledge only
  const resp=await fetch('https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages',{method:'POST',headers,body:JSON.stringify(body)});
  if(!resp.ok){ const e=await resp.text(); let m=`API error ${resp.status}`; try{m=JSON.parse(e).error?.message||m;}catch(_){} throw new Error(m); }
  const data=await resp.json();
  if(data.error) throw new Error(data.error.message||'API error');
  return (data.content||[]).filter(b=>b.type==='text').map(b=>b.text).join('\n').trim();
}

function aiErrorHtml(e){
  const isAuth=e.message&&(e.message.includes('401')||e.message.includes('auth')||e.message.toLowerCase().includes('api key')||e.message.includes('403'));
  if(isAuth) return`<div style="background:var(--rdim);border:1px solid var(--rbrd);padding:14px;border-left:3px solid var(--red)"><div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:9px;color:var(--red);letter-spacing:1.5px;margin-bottom:8px">⚠ API KEY REQUIRED</div><div style="font-family:var(--f3);font-size:12px;color:var(--tx);line-height:1.7">Add your Anthropic API key in <strong>Settings → Anthropic Key</strong>.<br>Get one at <a href="https://console.anthropic.com" target="_blank" style="color:var(--blue)">console.anthropic.com</a></div></div>`;
  return`<div style="color:var(--red);font-size:11.5px;padding:12px;border:1px solid var(--rbrd)">⚠ ${e.message||'Error'}. Check connection and retry.</div>`;
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// MOONSHOT SCANNER
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
async function runMoonshotScan(){
  const out=document.getElementById('moonshot-output'); if(!out) return;
  out.innerHTML='<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:9px;padding:10px 0;font-family:var(--f2);font-size:9.5px;color:var(--tx3)"><div class="spin"></div>Scanning OTC, NASDAQ, NYSE, crypto for asymmetric setups…</div>';
  const badge=document.getElementById('moon-badge'); if(badge){badge.textContent='SCANNING';badge.className='tag ta';}
  const btcStr=ST.btcPrice?Math.round(ST.btcPrice).toLocaleString():'~68,000';
  const fgStr=ST.fearGreed?`${ST.fearGreed} (${ST.fearGreedLabel})`:'unknown';
  try{
    const text=await callAI(
      `You are an asymmetric opportunity scanner for a US expat investor in Dubai with $475K to deploy. Portfolio: CLOV 90K shares ~$2.05, UNH 140 shares ~$288. Total liquid: ~$700K.\nScan ALL asset classes: microcap stocks (OTC/NASDAQ/NYSE), altcoins/crypto tokens, tokenized RE, RWA tokens, DeFi, biotech, AI, defense, fintech.\nInvestor style: long-term holder (1–3 years), wants 10–100x asymmetric plays, avoids noise and short-term trades, prefers LTCG treatment.\nFor each opportunity format EXACTLY as:\nNAME / TICKER | Asset Type | Est. Price | Est. Mkt Cap\nTHESIS: 1–2 sentences on 10x potential\nCATALYST: specific event or trend driving it\nENTRY ZONE: specific price range\nRISK: Low/Medium/High — main risk factor\nVERDICT: QUALITY SETUP | SPECULATIVE | AVOID\n---\nFind exactly 3 opportunities across different asset classes. Prioritize setups that could realistically become multi-baggers over years, not one-day pumps. No generic advice.`,
      `Find 3 best asymmetric opportunities across ALL asset classes right now (${monthYearStr()}). BTC ~$${btcStr}, Fear & Greed: ${fgStr}. Use web search for current catalysts, prices, and news. Mix stocks, crypto tokens, and RWA/tokenized assets.`
    );
    if(text){
      out.innerHTML=`<div style="font-family:var(--f3);font-size:12px;line-height:1.75;color:var(--tx);white-space:pre-wrap">${text}</div>`;
      if(badge){badge.textContent='RESULTS';badge.className='tag tg';}
    } else {
      out.innerHTML='<div style="color:var(--tx3);font-size:11.5px;padding:10px">No high-conviction setups found. Try again tomorrow.</div>';
      if(badge){badge.textContent='NO SIGNAL';badge.className='tag ta';}
    }
  }catch(e){
    out.innerHTML=aiErrorHtml(e);
    if(badge){badge.textContent='ERROR';badge.className='tag tr';}
  }
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// AI ANALYSIS
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function buildContext(){
  const lines=[];
  const btcStr=ST.btcPrice?'$'+Math.round(ST.btcPrice).toLocaleString():'~$68,000';
  const ethStr=ST.cryptoData?.ethereum?'$'+ST.cryptoData.ethereum.usd.toLocaleString('en-US',{maximumFractionDigits:0}):'unknown';
  const solStr=ST.cryptoData?.solana?'$'+ST.cryptoData.solana.usd.toLocaleString('en-US',{maximumFractionDigits:0}):'unknown';
  const fgStr=ST.fearGreed?`${ST.fearGreed}/100 — ${ST.fearGreedLabel}`:'unknown';
  lines.push(`=== LIVE CRYPTO DATA ===\nBTC: ${btcStr} (24h: ${ST.btcChange?.toFixed(2)||'?'}%)\nETH: ${ethStr}\nSOL: ${solStr}\nFear & Greed Index: ${fgStr}`);
  if(Object.keys(ST.fredData).length){
    lines.push(`=== FRED MACRO DATA ===`);
    if(ST.fredData.fedfunds) lines.push(`Fed Funds Rate: ${ST.fredData.fedfunds.value.toFixed(2)}% (${ST.fredData.fedfunds.date})`);
    if(ST.fredData.cpi) lines.push(`CPI Inflation: ${ST.fredData.cpi.value.toFixed(1)}%`);
    if(ST.fredData.unrate) lines.push(`Unemployment: ${ST.fredData.unrate.value.toFixed(1)}%`);
    if(ST.fredData.hy) lines.push(`HY Credit Spread: ${ST.fredData.hy.value.toFixed(2)}%`);
  }
  if(ST.quotes['SPY']) lines.push(`SPY: $${ST.quotes['SPY'].price.toFixed(0)} (${ST.quotes['SPY'].pct?.toFixed(2)}%)`);
  if(ST.quotes['VIX']) lines.push(`VIX: ${ST.quotes['VIX'].price.toFixed(1)}`);
  if(ST.quotes['CLOV']) lines.push(`CLOV: $${ST.quotes['CLOV'].price.toFixed(2)} (${ST.quotes['CLOV'].pct?.toFixed(2)}%)`);
  if(ST.quotes['UNH']) lines.push(`UNH: $${ST.quotes['UNH'].price.toFixed(0)} (${ST.quotes['UNH'].pct?.toFixed(2)}%)`);
  return lines.join('\n');
}
