  }
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// WATCHLIST MANAGEMENT
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function addToWL(ticker,name){
  if(ST.watchlist.find(w=>w.ticker===ticker)) return;
  ST.watchlist.unshift({ticker,name,buyPrice:null,profile:'balanced'});
  try{localStorage.setItem('forge_wl',JSON.stringify(ST.watchlist));}catch(e){}
  renderDashContent(false);
  showToast(ticker+' added to watchlist');
}
function addWatchTicker(){
  const t=document.getElementById('new-ticker')?.value.trim().toUpperCase();
  const n=document.getElementById('new-name')?.value.trim()||t;
  if(!t) return;
  if(ST.watchlist.find(w=>w.ticker===t)){showToast('Already in watchlist');return;}
  addToWL(t,n);
  if(document.getElementById('new-ticker')) document.getElementById('new-ticker').value='';
  if(document.getElementById('new-name')) document.getElementById('new-name').value='';
  renderSettings();
}
function removeWatchTicker(i){ ST.watchlist.splice(i,1); try{localStorage.setItem('forge_wl',JSON.stringify(ST.watchlist)); if(typeof renderTAAssetRow==='function' && TA_S && TA_S.taInited) renderTAAssetRow();}catch(e){} renderSettings(); }

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SETTINGS RENDER
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function renderSettings(){
  // Watchlist
  const wl=document.getElementById('wl-manage'); if(!wl) return;
  wl.innerHTML=ST.watchlist.map((item,i)=>`<div class="wl-item">
    <div><div class="wl-ticker">${item.ticker}</div><div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:8.5px;color:var(--tx3)">${item.name}</div></div>
    <div style="display:flex;gap:6px;align-items:center">
      <select onchange="ST.watchlist[${i}].profile=this.value;localStorage.setItem('forge_wl',JSON.stringify(ST.watchlist))" style="background:var(--bg2);border:1px solid var(--b2);border-radius:4px;padding:5px 7px;color:var(--tx3);font-family:var(--f2);font-size:8px;outline:none">
        <option value="moonshot" ${item.profile==='moonshot'?'selected':''}>MOONSHOT</option>
        <option value="balanced" ${item.profile==='balanced'?'selected':''}>BALANCED</option>
        <option value="preservation" ${item.profile==='preservation'?'selected':''}>PRESERVE</option>
      </select>
      <button class="rm-btn" onclick="removeWatchTicker(${i})">×</button>
    </div>
  </div>`).join('');
  // Thresholds
  const thr=document.getElementById('thr-row'); if(!thr) return;
  thr.innerHTML=[25,50,100,200].map(v=>`<div class="thr-btn ${ST.settings.threshold===v?'on':''}" onclick="ST.settings.threshold=${v};try{localStorage.setItem('forge_set',JSON.stringify(ST.settings));}catch(e){}renderSettings()">+${v}%</div>`).join('');
  // Toggles
  ['push','auto'].forEach(k=>{const el=document.getElementById('tog-'+k);if(el)el.classList.toggle('on',!!ST.settings[k]);});
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// DATA VAULT — Versioned backup / restore
// All data lives under stable 'forge_*' keys.
// Replace the HTML file any time — data survives.
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════

const VAULT_VERSION = 10; // bump when schema changes

function vaultSave() {
  // Collect everything
  const vault = {
    _v: VAULT_VERSION,
    _saved: new Date().toISOString(),
    _app: 'ForgeAI',
    watchlist:  ST.watchlist,
    settings:   { ...ST.settings, ak: ST.settings.ak || '' }, // include API key in local export
    alerts:     ST.alerts,
    sigChecks:  ST.sigChecks,
    avKey:      localStorage.getItem('forge_av') || 'IHBPWVYIUIM8M2UQ',
    brief:      (() => { try { return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('forge_brief') || 'null'); } catch(e) { return null; } })(),
  };
  return vault;
}

function exportData() {
  const vault = vaultSave();
  // Redact API key from the downloaded file for safety
  const safe = { ...vault, settings: { ...vault.settings, ak: vault.settings.ak ? '[REDACTED — RE-ENTER AFTER RESTORE]' : '' } };
  const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(safe, null, 2)], { type: 'application/json' });
  const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  const a = document.createElement('a');
  a.href = url;
  const d = new Date();
  a.download = `forgeai-vault-${d.getFullYear()}${String(d.getMonth()+1).padStart(2,'0')}${String(d.getDate()).padStart(2,'0')}.json`;
  a.click();
  URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
  showToast('Vault exported ✓ — save this file before updating the app');
}

function exportDataFull() {
  // Full export including API key — for local device backup only
  const vault = vaultSave();
  const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(vault, null, 2)], { type: 'application/json' });
  const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  const a = document.createElement('a');
  a.href = url;
  const d = new Date();
  a.download = `forgeai-vault-FULL-${d.getFullYear()}${String(d.getMonth()+1).padStart(2,'0')}${String(d.getDate()).padStart(2,'0')}.json`;
  a.click();
  URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
  showToast('Full vault exported ✓ (includes API key — keep private)');
}

function importData() {
  const input = document.createElement('input');
  input.type = 'file';
  input.accept = '.json';
  input.onchange = e => {
    const file = e.target.files[0];
    if (!file) return;
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = ev => {
      try {
        const vault = JSON.parse(ev.target.result);
        vaultRestore(vault);
      } catch(err) {
        showToast('❌ Invalid vault file');
      }
    };
    reader.readAsText(file);
  };
  input.click();
}

function vaultRestore(vault) {
  if (!vault || !vault._app) { showToast('❌ Not a ForgeAI vault file'); return; }

  // Restore watchlist
  if (Array.isArray(vault.watchlist) && vault.watchlist.length) {
    ST.watchlist = vault.watchlist;
    localStorage.setItem('forge_wl', JSON.stringify(ST.watchlist));
  }

  // Restore settings (skip redacted API key)
  if (vault.settings) {
    const s = { ...vault.settings };
    if (s.ak && s.ak.includes('REDACTED')) delete s.ak;
    Object.assign(ST.settings, s);
    localStorage.setItem('forge_set', JSON.stringify(ST.settings));
  }

  // Restore alerts
  if (Array.isArray(vault.alerts)) {
    ST.alerts = vault.alerts;
    localStorage.setItem('forge_al', JSON.stringify(ST.alerts));
  }

  // Restore signal checks
  if (vault.sigChecks) {
    ST.sigChecks = vault.sigChecks;
    localStorage.setItem('forge_sc', JSON.stringify(ST.sigChecks));
  }

  // Restore AV key
  if (vault.avKey) {
    localStorage.setItem('forge_av', vault.avKey);
    if (typeof TA_S !== 'undefined') TA_S.avKey = vault.avKey;
  }

  // Restore brief cache
  if (vault.brief) {
    localStorage.setItem('forge_brief', JSON.stringify(vault.brief));
  }

  // Re-render everything
  renderDashContent(false);
  renderAlerts();
  renderSettings();
  if (typeof renderTAAssetRow === 'function' && TA_S && TA_S.taInited) renderTAAssetRow();

  showToast(`✓ Vault restored — v${vault._v || '?'} from ${vault._saved ? vault._saved.split('T')[0] : 'unknown date'}`);
}

// Auto-save vault to localStorage on any significant change

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// PUSH NOTIFICATIONS
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
async function sendPush(title,msg){
  if(!ST.settings.ntfy) return;
  try{ await fetch('https://ntfy.sh/'+ST.settings.ntfy,{method:'POST',headers:{'Title':'ForgeAI: '+title,'Priority':'high','Tags':'chart_with_upwards_trend'},body:msg}); }catch(e){}
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// HELPERS
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function fp(p,ticker){
  if(!p&&p!==0) return '—';
  if(ticker==='BTC') return '$'+Math.round(p).toLocaleString();
  if(p<0.00001) return '$'+p.toFixed(8);
  if(p<0.001) return '$'+p.toFixed(6);
  if(p<0.01) return '$'+p.toFixed(5);
  if(p<0.1) return '$'+p.toFixed(4);
  if(p<1) return '$'+p.toFixed(4);
  if(p<10) return '$'+p.toFixed(3);
  if(p<1000) return '$'+p.toFixed(2);
  if(p<10000) return '$'+Math.round(p).toLocaleString();
  return '$'+(p/1000).toFixed(1)+'K';
}
function showToast(msg){ const t=document.getElementById('toast'); t.textContent=msg; t.classList.add('show'); setTimeout(()=>t.classList.remove('show'),2800); };



const CRYPTO_ASSETS = ['BTC','ETH','SOL'];
const STOCK_ASSETS = ['CLOV','UNH'];

const COINGECKO_IDS = { BTC:'bitcoin', ETH:'ethereum', SOL:'solana' };
const COLORS = {
  ema20:'#ffd700', ema50:'#ff8c00', ema200:'#ff4444',
  bb:'#b48eff', fib:'#00e5cc', sr:'#ffb800',
  bull:'#00e676', bear:'#ff4560', vol:'#00c8ff',
  rsi:'#00e5cc', macd:'#b48eff', macdSig:'#ffb800',
};

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// NAVIGATION
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function taShowTab(tab) {
  TA_S.tab = tab;
  // Only toggle ta-tab-btn buttons, not all nav buttons
  document.querySelectorAll('.ta-tab-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('on'));
  // Only hide TA sub-screens (s-chart, s-signals, s-learn), not parent screens
  ['chart','signals','technicals','news','ratings','ai','learn'].forEach(t => {
    const el = document.getElementById('s-'+t);
    if (el) el.classList.remove('active');
  });
  const tabBtn = document.getElementById('ta-tab-' + tab);
  if (tabBtn) tabBtn.classList.add('on');
  const screen = document.getElementById('s-' + tab);
  if (screen) screen.classList.add('active');
  if (tab === 'chart') {
    setTimeout(() => { if (typeof scheduleRedraw === "function") scheduleRedraw(); }, 50);
  }
  if (tab === 'signals') renderSignals();
  if (tab === 'chart') setTimeout(redraw, 50);
  if (tab === 'technicals') taShowTechnicals();
  if (tab === 'news') taShowNews();
  if (tab === 'ratings') taShowRatings();
  if (tab === 'ai') taShowAI();
}

function selectAsset(asset) {
  if (asset === 'CUSTOM') return promptCustom();
  TA_S.asset = asset;
  invalidateCache();
  // Update active ticker display
  const nameEl = document.getElementById('chart-ticker-name');
  const disp = document.getElementById('chart-active-ticker');
  if (nameEl) nameEl.textContent = asset;
  if (disp) disp.style.display = 'flex';
  document.querySelectorAll('.asset-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('on'));
  const activeBtn = document.querySelector(`[data-asset="${asset}"]`);
  if (activeBtn) activeBtn.classList.add('on');
  checkAVBanner();
  loadAsset(asset).catch(e=>console.warn('selectAsset:',e));
}

function promptCustom() {
  const t = prompt('Enter any ticker (e.g. TSLA, AAPL, NVDA, IONQ, RGTI):');
  if (!t) return;
  const ticker = t.trim().toUpperCase();
  if (!TA_S.customTickers) TA_S.customTickers = [];
  if (!TA_S.customTickers.includes(ticker)) TA_S.customTickers.push(ticker);
  renderTAAssetRow();
  selectAsset(ticker);
}

function checkAVBanner() {
  const banner = document.getElementById('av-banner');
  if (!banner) return;
  if (STOCK_ASSETS.includes(TA_S.asset) && !TA_S.avKey) {
    banner.style.display = 'flex';
    banner.style.flexDirection = 'column';
  } else {
    banner.style.display = 'none';
  }
}

function saveAVKey() {
  const _ainp = document.getElementById('av-inp'); const k = _ainp ? _ainp.value.trim() : ''; if(!k) return;
  if (!k) return;
  TA_S.avKey = k;
  localStorage.setItem('forge_av', k);
  const _avb=document.getElementById('av-banner'); if(_avb) _avb.style.display='none';
  loadAsset(TA_S.asset).catch(e=>console.warn('saveAVKey:',e));
  showToast('Alpha Vantage key saved');
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// CONTROLS
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function setTF(tf) {
  TA_S.tf = tf;
  document.querySelectorAll('.tf-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.toggle('on', b.dataset.tf === tf));
  invalidateCache();
  // Check if we have enough data for this TF - refetch if not
  const needed = tfToDays(tf) + 100;
  const have = (TA_S.data[TA_S.asset] || []).length;
  if (have < needed) {
    delete TA_S.data[TA_S.asset];
    loadAsset(TA_S.asset).catch(e => console.warn('setTF reload:', e));
  } else {
    scheduleRedraw();
  }
}

function toggleOverlay(name) {
  TA_S.overlays[name] = !TA_S.overlays[name];
  const btn = document.getElementById('btn-' + name);
  if (btn) btn.classList.toggle('on', TA_S.overlays[name]);
  // SR and Fib are cached — no need to invalidate full cache, just redraw
  scheduleRedraw();
}

function toggleIndicator(name) {
  TA_S.indicators[name] = !TA_S.indicators[name];
  const btn = document.getElementById('btn-' + name);
  if (btn) btn.classList.toggle('on', TA_S.indicators[name]);
  // Indicators are cached — panel height change needs canvas resize, handled in redraw guard
  scheduleRedraw();
}

function setChartType(type) {
  TA_S.chartType = type;
  ['line','area','bars','candles'].forEach(t => {
    const btn = document.getElementById('ct-' + t);
    if (btn) btn.classList.toggle('on', t === type);
  });
  scheduleRedraw();
}

function toggleLearn(hdr) {
  hdr.classList.toggle('open');
  const body = hdr.nextElementSibling;
  body.classList.toggle('open');
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// DATA LOADING
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
async function loadAsset(asset) {
  showLoading(true);
  try {
    let candles;
    if (CRYPTO_ASSETS.includes(asset)) {
      candles = await loadCryptoData(asset);
    } else {
      candles = await loadStockData(asset);
    }
    if (candles && candles.length > 5) {
      TA_S.data[asset] = candles;
      invalidateCache();
      updateAssetChip(asset, candles);
      scheduleRedraw();
      if (TA_S.tab === 'signals') renderSignals();
    }
  } catch(e) {
    console.error('Load error:', e);
    showToast('Using demo data — add API key for live prices');
    TA_S.data[asset] = generateDemoData(asset);
    invalidateCache();
    scheduleRedraw();
  }
  showLoading(false);
  updateMarketStatus();
}

async function loadCryptoData(asset) {
  const id = COINGECKO_IDS[asset];
  if (!id) throw new Error('Unknown asset: ' + asset);
  const days = tfToDays(TA_S.tf) + 50; // extra for indicators
  const url = `https://api.coingecko.com/api/v3/coins/${id}/ohlc?vs_currency=usd&days=${Math.min(days, 365)}`;
  const r = await fetch(url);
  if (!r.ok) throw new Error('CoinGecko OHLC ' + r.status);
  const raw = await r.json();
  if (!Array.isArray(raw)) throw new Error('Bad crypto data');
  return raw.map(d => ({
    date: new Date(d[0]).toISOString().split('T')[0],
    ts: d[0],
    o: d[1], h: d[2], l: d[3], c: d[4],
    v: 0,
  })).sort((a,b) => a.ts - b.ts);
}

async function loadStockData(asset) {
  // Use Finnhub for fast time-range based fetching
  if (ST.settings.fh) {
    const days = Math.max(tfToDays(TA_S.tf) + 100, 400); // extra for indicator warmup
    const to = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);
    const from = to - days * 86400;
    const url = `https://finnhub.io/api/v1/stock/candle?symbol=${asset}&resolution=D&from=${from}&to=${to}&token=${ST.settings.fh}`;
    const r = await fetch(url, {signal: AbortSignal.timeout(15000)});
    if (!r.ok) throw new Error('Finnhub HTTP ' + r.status);
    const d = await r.json();
    if (d.s === 'ok' && d.c && d.c.length > 5) {
      return d.t.map((t, i) => ({
        date: new Date(t * 1000).toISOString().split('T')[0],
        ts: t * 1000,
        o: d.o[i], h: d.h[i], l: d.l[i], c: d.c[i], v: d.v[i]
      })).sort((a,b) => a.ts - b.ts);
    }
  }
  // Fallback to Alpha Vantage
  if (TA_S.avKey) {
    const url = `https://www.alphavantage.co/query?function=TIME_SERIES_DAILY_ADJUSTED&symbol=${asset}&outputsize=full&apikey=${TA_S.avKey}`;
    const r = await fetch(url, {signal: AbortSignal.timeout(20000)});
    if (!r.ok) throw new Error('AlphaVantage HTTP ' + r.status);
    const d = await r.json();
    const ts = d['Time Series (Daily)'];
    if (!ts) throw new Error('No AV data');
    return Object.entries(ts).map(([date, v]) => ({
      date, ts: new Date(date).getTime(),
      o: parseFloat(v['1. open']), h: parseFloat(v['2. high']),
      l: parseFloat(v['3. low']), c: parseFloat(v['4. close']),
      v: parseInt(v['6. volume']),
    })).sort((a,b) => a.ts - b.ts);
  }
  return generateDemoData(asset);
}

function tfToDays(tf) {
  return { '1D':2, '1W':7, '1M':30, '3M':90, '6M':180, '1Y':365, '2Y':730, '5Y':1825 }[tf] || 30;
}


function getTFData(asset) {
  const all = TA_S.data[asset] || [];
  const days = tfToDays(TA_S.tf);
  return all.slice(-days);
}

function updateAssetChip(asset, candles) {
  const chip = document.getElementById('chg-' + asset);
  const btn = document.querySelector(`[data-asset="${asset}"]`);
  if (!chip || candles.length < 2) return;
  // Update active ticker price display if this is current asset
  if (asset === TA_S.asset) {
    const last = candles[candles.length-1];
    const prev = candles[candles.length-2];
    const pct = ((last.c - prev.c) / prev.c * 100);
    const priceEl = document.getElementById('chart-ticker-price');
    const chgEl = document.getElementById('chart-ticker-chg');
    if (priceEl) priceEl.textContent = last.c >= 1000 ? '$'+Math.round(last.c).toLocaleString() : '$'+last.c.toFixed(last.c >= 1 ? 2 : 4);
    if (chgEl) { chgEl.textContent = (pct>=0?'+':'')+pct.toFixed(2)+'%'; chgEl.style.color = pct>=0?'var(--green)':'var(--red)'; }
  }
  const last = candles[candles.length-1];
  const prev = candles[candles.length-2];
  const pct = ((last.c - prev.c) / prev.c * 100);
  chip.textContent = `${pct >= 0 ? '+' : ''}${pct.toFixed(1)}%`;
  btn.classList.toggle('up', pct >= 0);
  btn.classList.toggle('dn', pct < 0);
}

function showLoading(v) {
  const el = document.getElementById('chart-loading');
  if(el) el.classList.toggle('hidden', !v);
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// TECHNICAL INDICATOR CALCULATIONS
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function calcEMA(data, period) {
  const k = 2 / (period + 1);
  const result = new Array(data.length).fill(null);
  let sum = 0, count = 0;
  for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
    if (data[i] === null) continue;
    if (count < period) {
      sum += data[i];
      count++;
      if (count === period) result[i] = sum / period;
    } else {
      result[i] = data[i] * k + result[i-1] * (1 - k);
    }
  }
  return result;
}

function calcSMA(data, period) {
  return data.map((_, i) => {
    if (i < period - 1) return null;
    const slice = data.slice(i - period + 1, i + 1);
    if (slice.some(v => v === null)) return null;
    return slice.reduce((a,b) => a+b, 0) / period;
  });
}

function calcRSI(closes, period = 14) {
  const result = new Array(closes.length).fill(null);
  if (closes.length < period + 1) return result;
  let avgGain = 0, avgLoss = 0;
  for (let i = 1; i <= period; i++) {
    const delta = closes[i] - closes[i-1];
    if (delta > 0) avgGain += delta;
    else avgLoss -= delta;
  }
  avgGain /= period;
  avgLoss /= period;
  result[period] = 100 - (100 / (1 + (avgLoss === 0 ? Infinity : avgGain / avgLoss)));
  for (let i = period + 1; i < closes.length; i++) {
    const delta = closes[i] - closes[i-1];
    const gain = Math.max(0, delta);
    const loss = Math.max(0, -delta);
    avgGain = (avgGain * (period - 1) + gain) / period;
    avgLoss = (avgLoss * (period - 1) + loss) / period;
    result[i] = 100 - (100 / (1 + (avgLoss === 0 ? Infinity : avgGain / avgLoss)));
  }
  return result;
}

function calcMACD(closes) {
  const ema12 = calcEMA(closes, 12);
  const ema26 = calcEMA(closes, 26);
  const macdLine = ema12.map((v,i) => v !== null && ema26[i] !== null ? v - ema26[i] : null);
  const signalLine = calcEMA(macdLine, 9);
  const histogram = macdLine.map((v,i) => v !== null && signalLine[i] !== null ? v - signalLine[i] : null);
  return { macdLine, signalLine, histogram };
}

function calcBB(closes, period = 20, mult = 2) {
  const n = closes.length;
  const result = new Array(n).fill(null).map(() => ({ upper: null, mid: null, lower: null }));
  if (n < period) return result;
  // Use sliding window sum + sum-of-squares to avoid re-slicing every candle
  let sum = 0, sumSq = 0;
  for (let i = 0; i < period; i++) { sum += closes[i]; sumSq += closes[i] * closes[i]; }
  for (let i = period - 1; i < n; i++) {
    if (i > period - 1) {
      const add = closes[i], rem = closes[i - period];
      sum   += add - rem;
      sumSq += add * add - rem * rem;
    }
    const mean = sum / period;
    const variance = sumSq / period - mean * mean;
    const std = variance > 0 ? Math.sqrt(variance) : 0;
    result[i] = { upper: mean + mult * std, mid: mean, lower: mean - mult * std };
  }
  return result;
}

function calcOBV(candles) {
  const obv = [0];
  for (let i = 1; i < candles.length; i++) {
    const delta = candles[i].c > candles[i-1].c ? candles[i].v :
                  candles[i].c < candles[i-1].c ? -candles[i].v : 0;
    obv.push(obv[i-1] + delta);
  }
  return obv;
}

function calcATR(candles, period = 14) {
  const tr = candles.map((c, i) => {
    if (i === 0) return c.h - c.l;
    return Math.max(c.h - c.l, Math.abs(c.h - candles[i-1].c), Math.abs(c.l - candles[i-1].c));
  });
  return calcSMA(tr, period);
}

function findSRLevels(candles, lookback = 10) {
  const n = candles.length;
  const levels = [];
  // O(n) scan — no slice allocations
  for (let i = lookback; i < n - lookback; i++) {
    const ch = candles[i].h, cl = candles[i].l;
    let isHigh = true, isLow = true;
    for (let j = i - lookback; j <= i + lookback; j++) {
      if (j === i) continue;
      if (candles[j].h > ch) isHigh = false;
      if (candles[j].l < cl) isLow  = false;
      if (!isHigh && !isLow) break;
    }
    if (isHigh) levels.push({ price: ch, type: 'R' });
    if (isLow)  levels.push({ price: cl, type: 'S' });
  }
  // Cluster nearby levels (within 2%)
  const clustered = [];
  const used = new Set();
  for (let i = 0; i < levels.length; i++) {
    if (used.has(i)) continue;
    let sumP = levels[i].price, count = 1;
    for (let j = i + 1; j < levels.length; j++) {
      if (!used.has(j) && Math.abs(levels[j].price - levels[i].price) / levels[i].price < 0.02) {
        sumP += levels[j].price; count++;
        used.add(j);
      }
    }
    used.add(i);
    clustered.push({ price: sumP / count, type: levels[i].type, strength: count });
  }
  return clustered.sort((a, b) => b.strength - a.strength).slice(0, 6);
}

function calcFib(candles) {
  const highs = candles.map(c => c.h);
  const lows  = candles.map(c => c.l);
  const high = Math.max(...highs);
  const low  = Math.min(...lows);
  const diff = high - low;
  return [
    { label: '0%',    price: high,            color: COLORS.fib },
    { label: '23.6%', price: high - diff * 0.236, color: COLORS.fib },
    { label: '38.2%', price: high - diff * 0.382, color: COLORS.fib },
    { label: '50%',   price: high - diff * 0.5,   color: COLORS.fib },
    { label: '61.8%', price: high - diff * 0.618, color: COLORS.fib },
    { label: '78.6%', price: high - diff * 0.786, color: COLORS.fib },
    { label: '100%',  price: low,             color: COLORS.fib },
  ];
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// INDICATOR CACHE — compute once per asset+TF change
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function cacheKey() {
  return TA_S.asset + '|' + TA_S.tf;
}

function invalidateCache() {
  delete TA_S.cache[cacheKey()];
}

function buildCache() {
  const key = cacheKey();
  if (TA_S.cache[key]) return TA_S.cache[key]; // already built

  const allCandles = TA_S.data[TA_S.asset] || [];
  if (!allCandles.length) return null;

  const allCloses = allCandles.map(c => c.c);
  const candles   = getTFData(TA_S.asset);
  const offset    = allCandles.length - candles.length;

  const ema20all  = calcEMA(allCloses, 20);
  const ema50all  = calcEMA(allCloses, 50);
  const ema200all = calcEMA(allCloses, 200);
  const rsiAll    = calcRSI(allCloses);
  const macdAll   = calcMACD(allCloses);
  const bbAll     = calcBB(allCloses);

  const entry = {
    ema20:  ema20all.slice(offset),
    ema50:  ema50all.slice(offset),
    ema200: ema200all.slice(offset),
    rsi:    rsiAll.slice(offset),
    macd: {
      macdLine:   macdAll.macdLine.slice(offset),
      signalLine: macdAll.signalLine.slice(offset),
      histogram:  macdAll.histogram.slice(offset),
    },
    bb:     bbAll.slice(offset),
    // SR and Fib are cheap enough to cache too
    sr:     findSRLevels(candles),
    fib:    calcFib(candles),
  };

  TA_S.cache[key] = entry;
  return entry;
}

// RAF-throttled redraw — guarantees at most 1 repaint per animation frame
function scheduleRedraw() {
  if (TA_S._rafPending) return;
  TA_S._rafPending = true;
  requestAnimationFrame(() => {
    TA_S._rafPending = false;
    redraw();
  });
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// CHARTING ENGINE
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function redraw() {
  const candles = getTFData(TA_S.asset);
  if (!candles.length) return;

  const canvas = document.getElementById('main-canvas');
  const wrap = document.getElementById('chart-wrap');
  if (!canvas || !wrap) return;
  const dpr = window.devicePixelRatio || 1;
  const W = wrap.clientWidth;
  if (W < 10) { setTimeout(scheduleRedraw, 80); return; }

  // Panel heights
  const volH    = TA_S.indicators.vol  ? 55 : 0;
  const rsiH    = TA_S.indicators.rsi  ? 65 : 0;
  const macdH   = TA_S.indicators.macd ? 65 : 0;
  const mainH   = 240;
  const dateAxisH = 28;
  const H = mainH + volH + rsiH + macdH + dateAxisH;

  // ── Canvas resize guard — only reallocate GPU texture when dimensions change ──
  const newW = Math.round(W * dpr), newH = Math.round(H * dpr);
  if (canvas.width !== newW || canvas.height !== newH) {
    canvas.width  = newW;
    canvas.height = newH;
    canvas.style.height = H + 'px';
    wrap.style.height   = H + 'px';
    TA_S._lastW = newW;
    TA_S._lastH = newH;
  }

  const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
  ctx.setTransform(dpr, 0, 0, dpr, 0, 0);
  ctx.clearRect(0, 0, W, H);

  const PAD  = { left: 8, right: 55, top: 14, bottom: 0 };
  const chartW = W - PAD.left - PAD.right;

  const closes = candles.map(c => c.c);
  const highs  = candles.map(c => c.h);
  const lows   = candles.map(c => c.l);
  const vols   = candles.map(c => c.v);

  // ── Read from cache — zero recalculation on mouse move ──
  const cached = buildCache();
  if (!cached) return;
  const { ema20, ema50, ema200, rsi, macd: macdData, bb } = cached;
  const srLevels  = TA_S.overlays.sr  ? cached.sr  : [];
  const fibLevels = TA_S.overlays.fib ? cached.fib : [];

  // Price range
  let priceMax = Math.max(...highs);
  let priceMin = Math.min(...lows);
  if (TA_S.overlays.bb) {
    const validUpper = bb.map(b => b.upper).filter(v => v !== null);
    const validLower = bb.map(b => b.lower).filter(v => v !== null);
    if (validUpper.length) priceMax = Math.max(priceMax, Math.max(...validUpper));
    if (validLower.length) priceMin = Math.min(priceMin, Math.min(...validLower));
  }
  const priceRange = priceMax - priceMin;
  const pricePad = priceRange * 0.06;
  priceMax += pricePad;
  priceMin -= pricePad;

  function px(price) {
    return PAD.top + mainH - PAD.top - (price - priceMin) / (priceMax - priceMin) * (mainH - PAD.top);
  }
  function cx(i) {
    return PAD.left + (i + 0.5) / candles.length * chartW;
  }
  const candleW = Math.max(1, chartW / candles.length * 0.7);

  // ─── MAIN CHART BACKGROUND ───
  drawPanelBg(ctx, 0, 0, W, mainH, '#1c1c1c');
  drawGrid(ctx, PAD, W, mainH, priceMin, priceMax, 5);

  // ─── BOLLINGER BANDS ───
  if (TA_S.overlays.bb) {
    ctx.save();
    ctx.beginPath();
    let started = false;
    bb.forEach((b, i) => {
      if (b.upper === null) return;
      const x = cx(i), y = px(b.upper);
      if (!started) { ctx.moveTo(x, y); started = true; } else ctx.lineTo(x, y);
    });
    bb.slice().reverse().forEach((b, i) => {
      if (b.lower === null) return;
      const ri = candles.length - 1 - i;
      ctx.lineTo(cx(ri), px(b.lower));
    });
    ctx.closePath();
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(180,142,255,0.06)';
    ctx.fill();
    drawLine(ctx, bb.map((b,i) => b.upper !== null ? [cx(i), px(b.upper)] : null), COLORS.bb, 1, [4,3]);
    drawLine(ctx, bb.map((b,i) => b.lower !== null ? [cx(i), px(b.lower)] : null), COLORS.bb, 1, [4,3]);
    drawLine(ctx, bb.map((b,i) => b.mid   !== null ? [cx(i), px(b.mid)]   : null), COLORS.bb, 0.5);
    ctx.restore();
  }

  // ─── FIBONACCI ───
  if (TA_S.overlays.fib) {
    fibLevels.forEach(f => {
      ctx.save();
      ctx.strokeStyle = COLORS.fib; ctx.lineWidth = 0.5; ctx.setLineDash([6,4]); ctx.globalAlpha = 0.5;
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(PAD.left, px(f.price)); ctx.lineTo(W - PAD.right, px(f.price)); ctx.stroke();
      ctx.globalAlpha = 0.8; ctx.font = `8px 'DM Mono'`; ctx.fillStyle = COLORS.fib; ctx.textAlign = 'right';
      ctx.fillText(f.label, W - 2, px(f.price) - 2);
      ctx.restore();
    });
  }

  // ─── S/R LEVELS ───
  if (TA_S.overlays.sr) {
    srLevels.forEach(sr => {
      const col = sr.type === 'R' ? COLORS.bear : COLORS.bull;
      ctx.save();
      ctx.strokeStyle = col; ctx.lineWidth = 0.8; ctx.setLineDash([3,5]); ctx.globalAlpha = 0.6;
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(PAD.left, px(sr.price)); ctx.lineTo(W - PAD.right, px(sr.price)); ctx.stroke();
      ctx.globalAlpha = 0.85; ctx.font = `7px 'DM Mono'`; ctx.fillStyle = col; ctx.textAlign = 'left';
      ctx.fillText(sr.type + ' ' + fp(sr.price), W - PAD.right + 2, px(sr.price) + 3);
      ctx.restore();
    });
  }

  // ─── EMAs ───
  if (TA_S.overlays.ema200) drawLine(ctx, ema200.map((v,i) => v !== null ? [cx(i), px(v)] : null), COLORS.ema200, 1.5);
  if (TA_S.overlays.ema50)  drawLine(ctx, ema50.map((v,i)  => v !== null ? [cx(i), px(v)] : null), COLORS.ema50,  1.5);
  if (TA_S.overlays.ema20)  drawLine(ctx, ema20.map((v,i)  => v !== null ? [cx(i), px(v)] : null), COLORS.ema20,  1.2);

  // ─── CHART TYPE RENDERING ───
  const ct = TA_S.chartType || 'line';

  if (ct === 'line') {
    // Clean close price line
    drawLine(ctx, closes.map((v,i) => [cx(i), px(v)]), 'rgba(0,200,255,0.9)', 1.8);
    // Current price dot
    const lastX = cx(candles.length - 1), lastY = px(closes[closes.length - 1]);
    ctx.save(); ctx.fillStyle = '#00c8ff';
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(lastX, lastY, 3, 0, Math.PI * 2); ctx.fill();
    ctx.restore();

  } else if (ct === 'area') {
    // Gradient area chart
    ctx.save();
    const grad = ctx.createLinearGradient(0, PAD.top, 0, mainH);
    grad.addColorStop(0, 'rgba(0,200,255,0.35)');
    grad.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(0,200,255,0.01)');
    ctx.beginPath();
    closes.forEach((v, i) => { i === 0 ? ctx.moveTo(cx(i), px(v)) : ctx.lineTo(cx(i), px(v)); });
    ctx.lineTo(cx(candles.length - 1), mainH);
    ctx.lineTo(cx(0), mainH);
    ctx.closePath();
    ctx.fillStyle = grad;
    ctx.fill();
    // Line on top
    drawLine(ctx, closes.map((v,i) => [cx(i), px(v)]), 'rgba(0,200,255,0.95)', 1.8);
    ctx.restore();

  } else if (ct === 'bars') {
    // OHLC bars
    candles.forEach((c, i) => {
      const x = cx(i);
      const isBull = c.c >= c.o;
      const col = isBull ? COLORS.bull : COLORS.bear;
      ctx.strokeStyle = col; ctx.lineWidth = Math.max(1, candleW * 0.5);
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.moveTo(x, px(c.h)); ctx.lineTo(x, px(c.l)); // vertical wick
      ctx.moveTo(x - candleW * 0.6, px(c.o)); ctx.lineTo(x, px(c.o)); // open tick left
      ctx.moveTo(x, px(c.c)); ctx.lineTo(x + candleW * 0.6, px(c.c)); // close tick right
      ctx.stroke();
    });

  } else {
    // CANDLES (full candlesticks)
    candles.forEach((c, i) => {
      const x = cx(i);
      const isBull = c.c >= c.o;
      const col = isBull ? COLORS.bull : COLORS.bear;
      const bodyTop = px(Math.max(c.o, c.c));
      const bodyBot = px(Math.min(c.o, c.c));
      const bodyH   = Math.max(1, bodyBot - bodyTop);
      ctx.strokeStyle = col; ctx.lineWidth = 1;
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(x, px(c.h)); ctx.lineTo(x, bodyTop);
      ctx.moveTo(x, bodyBot); ctx.lineTo(x, px(c.l)); ctx.stroke();
      ctx.fillStyle   = isBull ? col + 'cc' : col + 'aa';
      ctx.strokeStyle = col; ctx.lineWidth = 0.5;
      ctx.fillRect(x - candleW/2, bodyTop, candleW, bodyH);
      ctx.strokeRect(x - candleW/2, bodyTop, candleW, bodyH);
    });
  }

  // ─── CROSSHAIR + FLOATING TOOLTIP ───
  if (TA_S.mouseX >= 0 && TA_S.mouseIdx >= 0 && TA_S.mouseIdx < candles.length) {
    const ci = TA_S.mouseIdx;
    const c  = candles[ci];
    const cx_ = cx(ci), cy_ = px(c.c);

    // Crosshair lines
    ctx.save();
    ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.2)'; ctx.lineWidth = 1; ctx.setLineDash([3,3]);
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(cx_, 0); ctx.lineTo(cx_, mainH);
    ctx.moveTo(PAD.left, cy_); ctx.lineTo(W - PAD.right, cy_);
    ctx.stroke();
    ctx.restore();

    // Price label on right axis
    ctx.save();
    ctx.fillStyle = '#00c8ff'; ctx.font = `bold 9px 'DM Mono'`; ctx.textAlign = 'left';
    ctx.fillText(fp(c.c), W - PAD.right + 2, cy_ + 3);
    ctx.restore();

    // ─ Floating tooltip pill ─
    const d = new Date(c.ts || c.date);
    const months = ['Jan','Feb','Mar','Apr','May','Jun','Jul','Aug','Sep','Oct','Nov','Dec'];
    const dateStr = months[d.getMonth()] + ' ' + d.getDate() + ', ' + d.getFullYear();
    const priceStr = fp(c.c);
    const pct = ci > 0 ? ((c.c - candles[ci-1].c) / candles[ci-1].c * 100) : 0;
    const pctStr  = (pct >= 0 ? '+' : '') + pct.toFixed(2) + '%';
    const label   = priceStr + '  ' + pctStr + '  ' + dateStr;
    const fSize   = 9;
    ctx.save();
    ctx.font = `bold ${fSize}px 'DM Mono'`;
    const tw = ctx.measureText(label).width;
    const pillW = tw + 20, pillH = 20, pillR = 4;
    let pillX = cx_ - pillW / 2;
    pillX = Math.max(PAD.left, Math.min(pillX, W - PAD.right - pillW));
    const pillY = cy_ > mainH / 2 ? cy_ - pillH - 8 : cy_ + 8;
    // Pill background — manual rounded rect for broad browser/WebKit support
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(20,30,40,0.92)';
    ctx.strokeStyle = pct >= 0 ? COLORS.bull : COLORS.bear;
    ctx.lineWidth = 1;
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(pillX + pillR, pillY);
    ctx.lineTo(pillX + pillW - pillR, pillY);
    ctx.quadraticCurveTo(pillX + pillW, pillY, pillX + pillW, pillY + pillR);
    ctx.lineTo(pillX + pillW, pillY + pillH - pillR);
    ctx.quadraticCurveTo(pillX + pillW, pillY + pillH, pillX + pillW - pillR, pillY + pillH);
    ctx.lineTo(pillX + pillR, pillY + pillH);
    ctx.quadraticCurveTo(pillX, pillY + pillH, pillX, pillY + pillH - pillR);
    ctx.lineTo(pillX, pillY + pillR);
    ctx.quadraticCurveTo(pillX, pillY, pillX + pillR, pillY);
    ctx.closePath();
    ctx.fill(); ctx.stroke();
    // Pill text
    ctx.fillStyle = '#ececec'; ctx.textAlign = 'left';
    ctx.fillText(priceStr, pillX + 8, pillY + 13);
    const pw1 = ctx.measureText(priceStr + '  ').width;
    ctx.fillStyle = pct >= 0 ? COLORS.bull : COLORS.bear;
    ctx.fillText(pctStr, pillX + 8 + pw1, pillY + 13);
    const pw2 = ctx.measureText(pctStr + '  ').width;
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(180,200,220,0.7)';
    ctx.fillText(dateStr, pillX + 8 + pw1 + pw2, pillY + 13);
    ctx.restore();

    updateOHLCV(c, candles[ci > 0 ? ci-1 : 0]);
  } else {
    const last = candles[candles.length-1];
    const prev = candles[candles.length-2];
    if (last) updateOHLCV(last, prev);
  }

  // ─── PRICE AXIS ───
  drawPriceAxis(ctx, PAD, W, mainH, priceMin, priceMax, 5);

  // ─── VOLUME PANEL ───
  let panelY = mainH;
  if (TA_S.indicators.vol) {
    drawPanelBg(ctx, 0, panelY, W, volH, '#1c1c1c');
    ctx.save();
    ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0,200,255,0.15)'; ctx.lineWidth = 0.5;
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(0, panelY); ctx.lineTo(W, panelY); ctx.stroke();
    ctx.font = `8px 'DM Mono'`; ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,200,255,0.5)'; ctx.textAlign = 'left';
    ctx.fillText('VOLUME', PAD.left, panelY + 10);
    ctx.restore();

    const maxVol = Math.max(...vols.filter(v => v > 0));
    if (maxVol > 0) {
      // Average volume line
      const avgVol = vols.filter(v=>v>0).reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0) / vols.filter(v=>v>0).length;
      candles.forEach((c, i) => {
        if (!c.v) return;
        const barH = (c.v / maxVol) * (volH - 16);
        const isBull = c.c >= c.o;
        ctx.fillStyle = isBull ? 'rgba(0,200,83,0.5)' : 'rgba(255,69,96,0.4)';
        ctx.fillRect(cx(i) - candleW/2, panelY + volH - 8 - barH, candleW, barH);
      });
      // Avg line
      const avgY = panelY + volH - 8 - (avgVol / maxVol) * (volH - 16);
      ctx.save();
      ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(255,200,0,0.5)'; ctx.lineWidth = 0.8; ctx.setLineDash([3,3]);
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(PAD.left, avgY); ctx.lineTo(W - PAD.right, avgY); ctx.stroke();
      ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(255,200,0,0.7)'; ctx.font = `7px 'DM Mono'`; ctx.textAlign = 'left';
      ctx.fillText('AVG', W - PAD.right + 2, avgY + 3);
      ctx.restore();
    }
    panelY += volH;
  }

  // ─── RSI PANEL ───
  if (TA_S.indicators.rsi) {
    drawPanelBg(ctx, 0, panelY, W, rsiH, '#1c1c1c');
    ctx.save();
    ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.06)'; ctx.lineWidth = 0.5;
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(PAD.left, panelY); ctx.lineTo(W - PAD.right, panelY); ctx.stroke();
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0,229,204,0.5)'; ctx.font = `7px 'DM Mono'`; ctx.textAlign = 'left';
    ctx.fillText('RSI(14)', PAD.left + 2, panelY + 10);
    ctx.restore();

    const ry = v => panelY + rsiH - 6 - (v / 100) * (rsiH - 16);
    [30, 70].forEach(l => {
      ctx.save();
      ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.08)'; ctx.lineWidth = 0.5; ctx.setLineDash([3,3]);
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(PAD.left, ry(l)); ctx.lineTo(W - PAD.right, ry(l)); ctx.stroke();
      ctx.setLineDash([]); ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(61,90,112,0.7)'; ctx.font = `7px 'DM Mono'`; ctx.textAlign = 'left';
      ctx.fillText(l, W - PAD.right + 2, ry(l) + 3);
      ctx.restore();
    });
    drawLine(ctx, rsi.map((v,i) => v !== null ? [cx(i), ry(v)] : null), '#00e5cc', 1.2);
    // Current RSI label
    const lastRSI = rsi.filter(v => v !== null).pop();
    if (lastRSI != null) {
      ctx.save(); ctx.fillStyle = '#00e5cc'; ctx.font = `bold 8px 'DM Mono'`; ctx.textAlign = 'left';
      ctx.fillText(lastRSI.toFixed(1), W - PAD.right + 2, ry(lastRSI) + 3);
      ctx.restore();
    }
    panelY += rsiH;
  }

  // ─── MACD PANEL ───
  if (TA_S.indicators.macd) {
    drawPanelBg(ctx, 0, panelY, W, macdH, '#1c1c1c');
    ctx.save();
    ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.06)'; ctx.lineWidth = 0.5;
    ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(PAD.left, panelY); ctx.lineTo(W - PAD.right, panelY); ctx.stroke();
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(180,142,255,0.5)'; ctx.font = `7px 'DM Mono'`; ctx.textAlign = 'left';
    ctx.fillText('MACD(12,26,9)', PAD.left + 2, panelY + 10);
    ctx.restore();

    const { macdLine, signalLine, histogram } = macdData;
    const allVals = [...macdLine, ...signalLine, ...histogram].filter(v => v !== null);
    if (allVals.length) {
      const minM = Math.min(...allVals), maxM = Math.max(...allVals), rng = maxM - minM || 1;
      const macdScale = v => panelY + macdH - 6 - ((v - minM) / rng) * (macdH - 16);
      const macdMid   = macdScale(0);
      ctx.save();
      ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.08)'; ctx.lineWidth = 0.5;
      ctx.beginPath(); ctx.moveTo(PAD.left, macdMid); ctx.lineTo(W - PAD.right, macdMid); ctx.stroke();
      ctx.restore();
      histogram.forEach((v, i) => {
        if (v === null) return;
        const y = macdScale(v), col = v >= 0 ? 'rgba(0,200,83,0.6)' : 'rgba(255,69,96,0.6)';
        ctx.fillStyle = col;
        ctx.fillRect(cx(i) - candleW/2, Math.min(y, macdMid), candleW, Math.max(1, Math.abs(macdMid - y)));
      });
      drawLine(ctx, macdLine.map((v,i)   => v !== null ? [cx(i), macdScale(v)] : null), COLORS.macd,    1.2);
      drawLine(ctx, signalLine.map((v,i) => v !== null ? [cx(i), macdScale(v)] : null), COLORS.macdSig, 1, [4,2]);
    }
    panelY += macdH;
  }

  // ─── DATE AXIS (dedicated strip below all panels — never clipped) ───
  drawDateAxis(ctx, candles, PAD, W, panelY, dateAxisH, chartW);
}

function drawPanelBg(ctx, x, y, w, h, color) {
  ctx.fillStyle = color;
  ctx.fillRect(x, y, w, h);
}

function drawGrid(ctx, PAD, W, H, min, max, count) {
  ctx.save();
  for (let i = 0; i <= count; i++) {
    const v = min + (max - min) * i / count;
    const y = PAD.top + (H - PAD.top - PAD.bottom) * (1 - i / count);
    ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(30,45,60,0.8)';
    ctx.lineWidth = 0.5;
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(PAD.left, y);
    ctx.lineTo(W - PAD.right, y);
    ctx.stroke();
  }
  ctx.restore();
}

function drawPriceAxis(ctx, PAD, W, H, min, max, count) {
  ctx.save();
  ctx.font = `8px 'DM Mono'`;
  ctx.textAlign = 'left';
  for (let i = 0; i <= count; i++) {
    const v = min + (max - min) * i / count;
    const y = PAD.top + (H - PAD.top - PAD.bottom) * (1 - i / count);
    ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(100,120,140,0.7)';
    ctx.fillText(fp(v), W - PAD.right + 3, y + 3);
  }
  ctx.restore();
}

// drawDateAxis — draws in its own strip starting at stripY, height stripH
// Never shares space with indicator panels — always visible regardless of active panels
function drawDateAxis(ctx, candles, PAD, W, stripY, stripH, chartW) {
  const n = candles.length;
  if (n < 2) return;

  const MON = ['Jan','Feb','Mar','Apr','May','Jun','Jul','Aug','Sep','Oct','Nov','Dec'];
  const tf  = TA_S.tf || '1M';

  // Background strip
  ctx.fillStyle = '#161616';
  ctx.fillRect(0, stripY, W, stripH);

  // Top separator line
  ctx.save();
  ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(80,110,140,0.45)';
  ctx.lineWidth = 0.5;
  ctx.beginPath();
  ctx.moveTo(PAD.left, stripY);
  ctx.lineTo(W - PAD.right, stripY);
  ctx.stroke();
  ctx.restore();

  // Determine label format + step strategy per TF
  // step = minimum candle index gap between labels to avoid overlap
  let fmtLabel, minStep;

  if (tf === '1D') {
    // Intraday: show hours (candles are hourly)
    fmtLabel = d => {
      const h = d.getHours();
      return h === 0 ? MON[d.getMonth()] + ' ' + d.getDate()
                     : (h % 12 || 12) + (h < 12 ? 'am' : 'pm');
    };
    minStep = Math.max(1, Math.floor(n / 7));
  } else if (tf === '1W') {
    // 7 days: show day name + date
    fmtLabel = d => ['Sun','Mon','Tue','Wed','Thu','Fri','Sat'][d.getDay()] + ' ' + d.getDate();
    minStep = Math.max(1, Math.floor(n / 7));
  } else if (tf === '1M') {
    // ~30 candles: show Mon DD
    fmtLabel = d => MON[d.getMonth()] + ' ' + d.getDate();
    minStep = Math.max(1, Math.floor(n / 6));
  } else if (tf === '3M') {
    // ~90 candles: show Mon DD, group by ~2 weeks
    fmtLabel = d => MON[d.getMonth()] + ' ' + d.getDate();
    minStep = Math.max(1, Math.floor(n / 7));
  } else if (tf === '6M') {
    // ~180 candles: show Mon DD, group by month
    fmtLabel = d => MON[d.getMonth()] + ' ' + d.getDate();
    minStep = Math.max(1, Math.floor(n / 7));
  } else if (tf === '1Y') {
    // ~365 candles: show Mon + year on change
    fmtLabel = d => MON[d.getMonth()];
    minStep = Math.max(1, Math.floor(n / 8));
  } else if (tf === '2Y') {
    // ~730 candles: show Mon YYYY on year change, else Mon
    fmtLabel = d => MON[d.getMonth()];
    minStep = Math.max(1, Math.floor(n / 8));
  } else {
    // 5Y: show QX YYYY (quarters)
    fmtLabel = d => {
      const q = Math.floor(d.getMonth() / 3) + 1;
      return 'Q' + q + ' ' + d.getFullYear();
    };
    minStep = Math.max(1, Math.floor(n / 7));
  }

  // Build label positions — skip if too close to previous
  const labels = [];
  let lastX = -999;
  const minPxGap = 48; // minimum pixels between labels

  for (let i = 0; i < n; i += minStep) {
    const x = PAD.left + (i + 0.5) / n * chartW;
    if (x - lastX < minPxGap) continue;
    const d = new Date(candles[i].ts || candles[i].date);
    labels.push({ i, x, d, label: fmtLabel(d) });
    lastX = x;
  }

  // Draw tick marks + labels
  ctx.save();
  ctx.textAlign = 'center';

  const needsYear = tf === '1Y' || tf === '2Y';
  let lastYear = null;

  labels.forEach(({ x, d, label }) => {
    const yr = d.getFullYear();

    // Tick
    ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(80,110,140,0.5)';
    ctx.lineWidth = 0.5;
    ctx.beginPath();
    ctx.moveTo(x, stripY);
    ctx.lineTo(x, stripY + 5);
    ctx.stroke();

    if (needsYear) {
      // Two-line: month on top, year below on change
      ctx.font = `bold 8px 'DM Mono'`;
      ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(200,215,230,0.85)';
      ctx.fillText(label, x, stripY + 12);
      if (yr !== lastYear) {
        ctx.font = `7px 'DM Mono'`;
        ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(100,140,180,0.75)';
        ctx.fillText(yr, x, stripY + 22);
        lastYear = yr;
      }
    } else {
      // Single line centred in strip
      ctx.font = `bold 8px 'DM Mono'`;
      ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(200,215,230,0.85)';
      ctx.fillText(label, x, stripY + 16);
    }
  });

  ctx.restore();
}


function drawLine(ctx, points, color, width = 1.5, dash = []) {
  const valid = points.filter(Boolean);
  if (!valid.length) return;
  ctx.save();
  ctx.strokeStyle = color;
  ctx.lineWidth = width;
  ctx.setLineDash(dash);
  ctx.lineJoin = 'round';
  ctx.beginPath();
  let started = false;
  points.forEach(p => {
    if (!p) { started = false; return; }
    if (!started) { ctx.moveTo(p[0], p[1]); started = true; }
    else ctx.lineTo(p[0], p[1]);
  });
  ctx.stroke();
  ctx.restore();
}

function updateOHLCV(c, prev) {
  const pct = prev ? (c.c - prev.c) / prev.c * 100 : 0;
  const _ov = (id, val) => { const e = document.getElementById(id); if(e) e.textContent = val; };
  // Format date from candle
  if (c.ts || c.date) {
    const d = new Date(c.ts || c.date);
    const months = ['Jan','Feb','Mar','Apr','May','Jun','Jul','Aug','Sep','Oct','Nov','Dec'];
    const dateStr = months[d.getMonth()] + ' ' + d.getDate() + ', ' + d.getFullYear();
    _ov('ov-date', dateStr);
  }
  _ov('ov-o', fp(c.o)); _ov('ov-h', fp(c.h)); _ov('ov-l', fp(c.l)); _ov('ov-c', fp(c.c)); _ov('ov-v', fmtVol(c.v));
  const chgEl = document.getElementById('ov-chg');
  if (chgEl) { chgEl.textContent = (pct >= 0 ? '+' : '') + pct.toFixed(2) + '%'; chgEl.style.color = pct >= 0 ? COLORS.bull : COLORS.bear; }
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// MOUSE / TOUCH INTERACTION
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function initCanvasEvents() {
  const canvas = document.getElementById('main-canvas');
  const wrap = document.getElementById('chart-wrap');
  if (!canvas || !wrap) return; // guard: screen may not be visible yet

  function getIdx(clientX) {
    const rect = canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
    const relX = clientX - rect.left;
    const PAD_LEFT = 8;
    const chartW = rect.width - PAD_LEFT - 55;
    const candles = getTFData(TA_S.asset);
    if (!candles.length) return -1;
    const idx = Math.floor((relX - PAD_LEFT) / chartW * candles.length);
    return Math.max(0, Math.min(candles.length - 1, idx));
  }

  canvas.addEventListener('mousemove', e => {
    TA_S.mouseX   = e.clientX;
    TA_S.mouseIdx = getIdx(e.clientX);
    scheduleRedraw();
  });
  canvas.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => {
    TA_S.mouseX   = -1;
    TA_S.mouseIdx = -1;
    scheduleRedraw();
  });
  canvas.addEventListener('touchstart', e => {
    e.preventDefault();
    TA_S.mouseIdx = getIdx(e.touches[0].clientX);
    scheduleRedraw();
  }, { passive: false });
  canvas.addEventListener('touchmove', e => {
    e.preventDefault();
    TA_S.mouseIdx = getIdx(e.touches[0].clientX);
    scheduleRedraw();
  }, { passive: false });
  canvas.addEventListener('touchend', () => {
    setTimeout(() => { TA_S.mouseIdx = -1; scheduleRedraw(); }, 1500);
  });
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// SIGNALS & TA ANALYSIS ENGINE
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function computeTA(asset) {
  const candles = TA_S.data[asset];
  if (!candles || candles.length < 30) return null;

  const closes  = candles.map(c => c.c);
  const highs   = candles.map(c => c.h);
  const lows    = candles.map(c => c.l);
  const vols    = candles.map(c => c.v);

  const ema20  = calcEMA(closes, 20);
  const ema50  = calcEMA(closes, 50);
  const ema200 = calcEMA(closes, 200);
  const rsi    = calcRSI(closes);
  const macd   = calcMACD(closes);
  const bb     = calcBB(closes);
  const atr    = calcATR(candles);
  const obv    = calcOBV(candles);

  const n = closes.length;
  const price = closes[n-1];
  const lastEMA20  = ema20[n-1];
  const lastEMA50  = ema50[n-1];
  const lastEMA200 = ema200[n-1];
  const lastRSI    = rsi[n-1];
  const lastMACD   = macd.macdLine[n-1];
  const lastSignal = macd.signalLine[n-1];
  const lastHist   = macd.histogram[n-1];
  const prevHist   = macd.histogram[n-2];
  const lastBB     = bb[n-1];
  const lastATR    = atr[n-1];

  // Volume analysis
  const volWindow = vols.filter(v => v > 0).slice(-30);
  const avgVol = volWindow.length ? volWindow.reduce((a,b) => a+b, 0) / volWindow.length : 0;
  const lastVol = vols[n-1];
  const volRatio = avgVol > 0 ? lastVol / avgVol : 0;
  const volTrend = vols.slice(-5).filter(v=>v>0).reduce((a,b,i,arr) => i > 0 ? a + (b > arr[i-1] ? 1 : -1) : 0, 0);

  // OBV trend
  const obvTrend = obv.slice(-10);
  const obvBullish = obvTrend[obvTrend.length-1] > obvTrend[0];

  // BB analysis
  const bbWidth = lastBB && lastBB.upper && lastBB.lower
    ? (lastBB.upper - lastBB.lower) / lastBB.mid
    : null;
  const bbWidths = bb.slice(-20).filter(b => b.mid > 0).map(b => b.upper ? (b.upper - b.lower) / b.mid : null).filter(v => v !== null);
  const avgBBWidth = bbWidths.length ? bbWidths.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0)/bbWidths.length : null;
  const bbSqueeze = bbWidth && avgBBWidth ? bbWidth < avgBBWidth * 0.7 : false;

  // Pattern detection
  const recentHighs = highs.slice(-20);
  const recentLows  = lows.slice(-20);
  const higherLows  = recentLows.slice(-5).every((v,i,a) => i === 0 || v > a[i-1]);
  const lowerHighs  = recentHighs.slice(-5).every((v,i,a) => i === 0 || v < a[i-1]);

  // Golden/Death cross
  const goldenCross = lastEMA50 && lastEMA200 && lastEMA50 > lastEMA200;
  const prevEMA50 = ema50[n-3];
  const prevEMA200 = ema200[n-3];
  const justGolden = prevEMA50 && prevEMA200 && prevEMA50 <= prevEMA200 && goldenCross;
  const justDeath  = prevEMA50 && prevEMA200 && prevEMA50 >= prevEMA200 && lastEMA50 < lastEMA200;

  // RSI divergence (last 10 candles)
  const recentRSI = rsi.slice(-10).filter(v => v !== null);
  const recentClose = closes.slice(-10);
  const bullDiv = recentClose[0] > recentClose[recentClose.length-1] && recentRSI[0] < recentRSI[recentRSI.length-1];
  const bearDiv = recentClose[0] < recentClose[recentClose.length-1] && recentRSI[0] > recentRSI[recentRSI.length-1];

  // Support/Resistance
  const srLevels = findSRLevels(candles);
  const nearestSupport    = srLevels.filter(s => s.type === 'S' && s.price < price).sort((a,b) => b.price - a.price)[0];
  const nearestResistance = srLevels.filter(s => s.type === 'R' && s.price > price).sort((a,b) => a.price - b.price)[0];

  // ATR-based stop loss
  const stopLoss = lastATR ? price - 2 * lastATR : price * 0.9;

  // Score each signal
  const signals = [];

  // TREND signals
  const aboveEMA20  = price > lastEMA20;
  const aboveEMA50  = price > lastEMA50;
  const aboveEMA200 = lastEMA200 ? price > lastEMA200 : null;
  const bullStack   = aboveEMA20 && aboveEMA50 && (aboveEMA200 !== false);
  signals.push({ group:'TREND', name:'Price vs EMA20', value: lastEMA20 ? fp(lastEMA20) : '—', dir: aboveEMA20 ? 'bull' : 'bear', weight: 1, explain: aboveEMA20 ? `Price (${fp(price)}) is above EMA20 (${fp(lastEMA20)}). Short-term trend is bullish.` : `Price is below EMA20. Short-term trend is bearish.` });
  signals.push({ group:'TREND', name:'Price vs EMA50', value: lastEMA50 ? fp(lastEMA50) : '—', dir: aboveEMA50 ? 'bull' : 'bear', weight: 2, explain: aboveEMA50 ? `Price is above EMA50 (${fp(lastEMA50)}). Medium-term trend is bullish. This is the most-watched institutional level.` : `Price is below EMA50. Medium-term trend is bearish.` });
  if (lastEMA200) signals.push({ group:'TREND', name:'Price vs EMA200', value: fp(lastEMA200), dir: aboveEMA200 ? 'bull' : 'bear', weight: 3, explain: aboveEMA200 ? `Price is above EMA200 — this is a bull market for ${asset}. Long-term buyers in control.` : `Price is below EMA200 — bear market territory. Long-term trend is down.` });
  signals.push({ group:'TREND', name:'EMA Alignment', value: bullStack ? 'BULL STACK' : 'MISALIGNED', dir: bullStack ? 'bull' : (aboveEMA20 || aboveEMA50 ? 'neut' : 'bear'), weight: 2, explain: bullStack ? 'EMA20 > EMA50 > EMA200 with price above all. This is the ideal bull trend alignment. Strong trend confirmation.' : 'EMAs are not in bull alignment. Trend is mixed or bearish.' });
  if (justGolden) signals.push({ group:'TREND', name:'Golden Cross', value: 'JUST FORMED', dir:'bull', weight:3, explain:'EMA50 just crossed above EMA200 — a Golden Cross. Historically one of the strongest buy signals. Institutional momentum follows.' });
  if (justDeath)  signals.push({ group:'TREND', name:'Death Cross', value: 'JUST FORMED', dir:'bear', weight:3, explain:'EMA50 just crossed below EMA200 — a Death Cross. Historically precedes significant declines.' });

  // MOMENTUM signals
  const rsiZone = lastRSI < 30 ? 'OVERSOLD' : lastRSI > 70 ? 'OVERBOUGHT' : 'NEUTRAL';
  const rsiDir  = lastRSI < 35 ? 'bull' : lastRSI > 65 ? 'bear' : 'neut';
  signals.push({ group:'MOMENTUM', name:'RSI(14)', value: lastRSI ? lastRSI.toFixed(1) : '—', dir: rsiDir, weight: 2, explain: `RSI is ${lastRSI?.toFixed(1)} — ${rsiZone}. ${rsiZone === 'OVERSOLD' ? 'Asset may be oversold. Look for RSI to turn upward as entry confirmation.' : rsiZone === 'OVERBOUGHT' ? 'Asset may be overbought. Consider taking partial profits.' : 'Momentum is neutral — no extreme reading.'}` });
  if (bullDiv) signals.push({ group:'MOMENTUM', name:'RSI Divergence', value: 'BULLISH DIV', dir:'bull', weight:3, explain:'Bullish RSI divergence detected: price made a lower low but RSI made a higher low. Selling momentum is weakening. High-conviction reversal signal.' });
  if (bearDiv) signals.push({ group:'MOMENTUM', name:'RSI Divergence', value: 'BEARISH DIV', dir:'bear', weight:3, explain:'Bearish RSI divergence: price made a higher high but RSI made a lower high. Buying momentum is weakening. Consider reducing position.' });

  const macdBullX = lastMACD && lastSignal && lastMACD > lastSignal;
  const macdJustX = lastHist && prevHist && ((lastHist > 0 && prevHist <= 0) || (lastHist < 0 && prevHist >= 0));
  signals.push({ group:'MOMENTUM', name:'MACD Crossover', value: lastMACD ? (lastMACD > 0 ? 'POSITIVE' : 'NEGATIVE') : '—', dir: macdBullX ? 'bull' : 'bear', weight: 2, explain: macdBullX ? `MACD line (${lastMACD?.toFixed(3)}) is above signal line (${lastSignal?.toFixed(3)}). Bullish momentum. Histogram is ${lastHist > 0 ? 'positive and growing' : 'positive but fading'}.` : `MACD line is below signal line. Bearish momentum.${macdJustX ? ' Crossover just occurred — watch for follow-through.' : ''}` });
  if (macdJustX) signals.push({ group:'MOMENTUM', name:'MACD Cross Signal', value: lastHist > 0 ? 'BULLISH X' : 'BEARISH X', dir: lastHist > 0 ? 'bull' : 'bear', weight:3, explain: lastHist > 0 ? 'MACD just crossed above signal line. Fresh bullish crossover — one of the strongest MACD buy signals.' : 'MACD just crossed below signal line. Fresh bearish crossover — exit signal for shorter-term traders.' });

  // VOLATILITY signals
  if (bbWidth !== null) {
    const bbPos = lastBB && lastBB.upper && lastBB.lower ? (price - lastBB.lower) / (lastBB.upper - lastBB.lower) : 0.5;
    const bbDir = bbSqueeze ? 'neut' : bbPos > 0.85 ? 'bear' : bbPos < 0.15 ? 'bull' : 'neut';
    signals.push({ group:'VOLATILITY', name:'Bollinger Bands', value: bbSqueeze ? 'SQUEEZE' : (bbPos > 0.85 ? 'UPPER BAND' : bbPos < 0.15 ? 'LOWER BAND' : 'MID RANGE'), dir: bbDir, weight: 2, explain: bbSqueeze ? 'Bollinger Band squeeze detected. Volatility is compressing — expect a large breakout move soon. Watch volume for direction.' : bbPos > 0.85 ? `Price near upper band (${lastBB?.upper ? fp(lastBB.upper) : '—'}). May be overextended short-term.` : bbPos < 0.15 ? `Price near lower band (${lastBB?.lower ? fp(lastBB.lower) : '—'}). Oversold region — potential bounce zone.` : 'Price in mid-range. No extreme BB signal.' });
  }
  if (lastATR) signals.push({ group:'VOLATILITY', name:'ATR(14)', value: fp(lastATR), dir:'neut', weight:1, explain: `Average True Range is ${fp(lastATR)} per day (${lastATR && price ? (lastATR/price*100).toFixed(1) : '—'}% of price). This is your daily risk range — used to set stop losses. Recommended stop: 2×ATR = ${fp(stopLoss)}.` });

  // VOLUME signals
  if (avgVol > 0) {
    const volDir = volRatio > 2 ? 'bull' : volRatio < 0.5 ? 'bear' : 'neut';
    signals.push({ group:'VOLUME', name:'Volume vs Average', value: volRatio > 0 ? volRatio.toFixed(1) + '×' : '—', dir: volDir, weight: 2, explain: volRatio > 2 ? `Volume is ${volRatio.toFixed(1)}× the 30-day average. High conviction move. Significant buying or selling pressure.` : volRatio < 0.5 ? 'Volume is below average. Low conviction. Moves on low volume are unreliable.' : `Volume is near average (${volRatio.toFixed(1)}×). Normal trading activity.` });
    signals.push({ group:'VOLUME', name:'OBV Trend', value: obvBullish ? 'RISING' : 'FALLING', dir: obvBullish ? 'bull' : 'bear', weight:2, explain: obvBullish ? 'On-Balance Volume is trending up, indicating accumulation — buyers are adding on strength. Bullish smart money signal.' : 'OBV is trending down. Distribution pattern — sellers are increasing. Bearish smart money signal.' });
  }

  // STRUCTURE signals
  signals.push({ group:'STRUCTURE', name:'Price Structure', value: higherLows ? 'HIGHER LOWS' : lowerHighs ? 'LOWER HIGHS' : 'MIXED', dir: higherLows ? 'bull' : lowerHighs ? 'bear' : 'neut', weight:2, explain: higherLows ? 'Price is forming higher lows — classic bullish structure. Each pullback is getting shallower, showing increasing demand at higher prices.' : lowerHighs ? 'Price is forming lower highs — classic bearish structure. Each rally is getting weaker.' : 'Price structure is mixed. No clear directional pattern.' });
  if (nearestSupport)    signals.push({ group:'STRUCTURE', name:'Nearest Support', value: fp(nearestSupport.price), dir: (price - nearestSupport.price)/price < 0.05 ? 'bull' : 'neut', weight:1, explain: `Nearest support level: ${fp(nearestSupport.price)} (${((price-nearestSupport.price)/price*100).toFixed(1)}% below current price). This is a potential add zone if price pulls back.` });
  if (nearestResistance) signals.push({ group:'STRUCTURE', name:'Nearest Resistance', value: fp(nearestResistance.price), dir: (nearestResistance.price-price)/price < 0.05 ? 'bear' : 'neut', weight:1, explain: `Nearest resistance: ${fp(nearestResistance.price)} (${((nearestResistance.price-price)/price*100).toFixed(1)}% above). Price needs to break through this level to continue higher.` });

  // Compute overall score
  let bullScore = 0, bearScore = 0, totalWeight = 0;
  signals.forEach(s => {
    if (s.dir === 'bull') bullScore += s.weight;
    else if (s.dir === 'bear') bearScore += s.weight;
    totalWeight += s.weight;
  });
  const rawScore = totalWeight > 0 ? (bullScore - bearScore) / totalWeight : 0;
  const score = Math.round(50 + rawScore * 50);

  // Build buy/sell plan
  const recentHigh = Math.max(...highs.slice(-30));
  const recentLow  = Math.min(...lows.slice(-30));

  // Buy levels: support, fib retracements, ATR levels
  const fib382 = price - (recentHigh - recentLow) * 0.382;
  const fib618 = price - (recentHigh - recentLow) * 0.618;
  const buyLevels = [
    { label:'B1', price: nearestSupport ? nearestSupport.price * 1.005 : price * 0.97, desc: nearestSupport ? `Near support level — first staged entry. Buy 30–35% of planned position.` : `First entry — buy 30–35% on initial signal.`, size:'30–35%' },
    { label:'B2', price: Math.max(fib382, price * 0.90), desc:`38.2% Fib retracement. Core entry zone. Add 40% of position. Strong probability level.`, size:'40%' },
    { label:'B3', price: Math.max(fib618, price * 0.82), desc:`61.8% "Golden Ratio" retracement. Deepest buy zone. Final add 25–30% if reached.`, size:'25–30%' },
  ];

  // Sell levels: resistance, extensions, ATR multiples
  const sellLevels = [
    { label:'T1', price: nearestResistance ? nearestResistance.price * 0.995 : price * 1.25, desc:`Near resistance. Sell 25–30%. Lock in first profit. You can't lose from here.`, gain: nearestResistance ? `+${((nearestResistance.price/price-1)*100).toFixed(0)}%` : '+25%' },
    { label:'T2', price: recentHigh * 1.15, desc:`25% above recent high — breakout extension target. Sell 35–40% of remaining position.`, gain:`+${((recentHigh*1.15/price-1)*100).toFixed(0)}%` },
    { label:'T3', price: recentHigh * 1.5, desc:`50% above recent high — extended target for moonshot tranche. Let 25–30% ride. Review when price gets here.`, gain:`+${((recentHigh*1.5/price-1)*100).toFixed(0)}%` },
  ];

  // Stop loss
  const stopLevel = lastATR ? price - 2.5 * lastATR : nearestSupport ? nearestSupport.price * 0.97 : price * 0.88;

  // Macro context
  const macroCtx = aboveEMA200
    ? { type:'risk-on', text:`${asset} is above its 200-day EMA — it's in a structural uptrend. Macro conditions favor holding and adding on dips.` }
    : { type:'caution', text:`${asset} is below its 200-day EMA — in bear market territory. Be cautious. Only stage entries at major support. Reduce position sizes.` };

  return { signals, score, price, buyLevels, sellLevels, stopLevel, macroCtx, lastRSI, lastATR, ema20: lastEMA20, ema50: lastEMA50, ema200: lastEMA200 };
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// RENDER SIGNALS TAB
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function renderSignals() {
  const el = document.getElementById('signals-content');
  const ta = computeTA(TA_S.asset);

  if (!ta) {
    el.innerHTML = `<div style="padding:40px;text-align:center;font-family:var(--f2);font-size:10px;color:var(--tx4);letter-spacing:3px">LOAD ${TA_S.asset} CHART FIRST<br/><br/><div style="font-size:9px;color:var(--tx4)">Go to CHART tab → Select asset → Data loads automatically</div></div>`;
    return;
  }

  const { signals, score, price, buyLevels, sellLevels, stopLevel, macroCtx, lastRSI } = ta;
  const scoreColor = score >= 65 ? 'var(--green)' : score >= 45 ? 'var(--amber)' : 'var(--red)';
  const scoreLabel = score >= 75 ? 'STRONG BUY' : score >= 62 ? 'BUY SIGNAL' : score >= 50 ? 'CAUTIOUS BUY' : score >= 38 ? 'NEUTRAL' : score >= 25 ? 'CAUTION' : 'AVOID / SELL';
  const bullCount = signals.filter(s => s.dir === 'bull').length;
  const bearCount = signals.filter(s => s.dir === 'bear').length;
  const bars = Array.from({length:10}, (_,i) => {
    const filled = i < Math.round(score/10);
    const colorClass = score >= 65 ? 'fill' : score >= 45 ? 'fill mid' : 'fill low';
    return `<div class="ss-bar ${filled ? colorClass : ''}"></div>`;
  }).join('');

  const groups = ['TREND','MOMENTUM','VOLATILITY','VOLUME','STRUCTURE'];
  const signalHTML = groups.map(g => {
    const gsigs = signals.filter(s => s.group === g);
    if (!gsigs.length) return '';
    return `<div class="sig-section">
      <div class="sig-sec-title">${g}</div>
      ${gsigs.map(s => `
        <div class="sig-card fade-in">
          <div class="sig-card-top">
            <div class="sig-name">${s.name}</div>
            <div class="sig-badge badge-${s.dir}">${s.dir === 'bull' ? '↑ BULLISH' : s.dir === 'bear' ? '↓ BEARISH' : '→ NEUTRAL'}</div>
          </div>
          <div class="sig-value" style="color:${s.dir==='bull'?'var(--green)':s.dir==='bear'?'var(--red)':'var(--amber)'}">${s.value}</div>
          <div class="sig-explain">${s.explain}</div>
          <div class="sig-bar-wrap"><div class="sig-bar-fill" style="width:${s.dir==='bull'?100:s.dir==='bear'?0:50}%;background:${s.dir==='bull'?'var(--green)':s.dir==='bear'?'var(--red)':'var(--amber)'}"></div></div>
        </div>
      `).join('')}
    </div>`;
  }).join('');

  el.innerHTML = `
    <!-- Score block -->
    <div class="sig-score-block fade-in">
      <div class="ss-asset">${TA_S.asset} · ${fp(price)} · TA SCORE</div>
      <div class="ss-num" style="color:${scoreColor}">${score}</div>
      <div class="ss-label" style="color:${scoreColor}">${scoreLabel}</div>
      <div class="ss-bars">${bars}</div>
      <div style="display:flex;gap:20px;justify-content:center;margin-top:12px">
        <span style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:10px;color:var(--green)">↑ ${bullCount} BULLISH</span>
        <span style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:10px;color:var(--red)">↓ ${bearCount} BEARISH</span>
        <span style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:10px;color:var(--tx3)">${signals.length - bullCount - bearCount} NEUTRAL</span>
      </div>
    </div>

    <!-- Macro context -->
    <div class="macro-warn ${macroCtx.type} fade-in" style="margin:0 16px 12px">
      <strong style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:9px;letter-spacing:2px">${macroCtx.type === 'risk-on' ? '✅ MACRO: RISK-ON' : macroCtx.type === 'caution' ? '⚠️ MACRO: CAUTION' : '🔴 MACRO: RISK-OFF'}</strong><br/>${macroCtx.text}
    </div>

    <!-- Time horizons -->
    <div class="horizon-block fade-in">
      <div class="hor-card">
        <div class="hor-label">TIME HORIZON</div>
        <div class="hor-val" style="color:var(--green)">LONG</div>
        <div class="hor-sub">12+ months<br/>Target LTCG rate</div>
      </div>
      <div class="hor-card">
        <div class="hor-label">STOP LOSS</div>
        <div class="hor-val" style="color:var(--red)">${fp(stopLevel)}</div>
        <div class="hor-sub">2.5× ATR below<br/>entry price</div>
      </div>
      <div class="hor-card">
        <div class="hor-label">RSI NOW</div>
        <div class="hor-val" style="color:${lastRSI < 35 ? 'var(--green)' : lastRSI > 65 ? 'var(--red)' : 'var(--amber)'}">${lastRSI ? lastRSI.toFixed(0) : '—'}</div>
        <div class="hor-sub">${lastRSI < 35 ? 'Oversold zone' : lastRSI > 65 ? 'Overbought zone' : 'Neutral zone'}</div>
      </div>
    </div>

    <!-- Buy Plan -->
    <div class="plan-block plan-buy fade-in">
      <div class="plan-hdr">
        <div class="plan-title">BUY PLAN</div>
        <div class="plan-badge" style="background:var(--gdim);color:var(--green);border:1px solid var(--gbrd)">STAGED ENTRY</div>
      </div>
      ${buyLevels.map((lv,i) => `
        <div class="plan-level">
          <div class="pl-num">${i+1}</div>
          <div style="flex:1">
            <div class="pl-price" style="color:var(--green)">${fp(lv.price)}</div>
            <div class="pl-desc">${lv.desc}</div>
          </div>
          <div class="pl-gain" style="color:var(--tx3)">${lv.size}</div>
        </div>
      `).join('')}
    </div>

    <!-- Sell Plan -->
    <div class="plan-block plan-sell fade-in">
      <div class="plan-hdr">
        <div class="plan-title">SELL PLAN</div>
        <div class="plan-badge" style="background:var(--adim);color:var(--amber);border:1px solid var(--abrd)">PROFIT TARGETS</div>
      </div>
      ${sellLevels.map((lv,i) => `
        <div class="plan-level">
          <div class="pl-num">T${i+1}</div>
          <div style="flex:1">
            <div class="pl-price" style="color:var(--amber)">${fp(lv.price)}</div>
            <div class="pl-desc">${lv.desc}</div>
          </div>
          <div class="pl-gain" style="color:var(--green)">${lv.gain}</div>
        </div>
      `).join('')}
    </div>

    <!-- Stop Loss -->
    <div class="plan-block plan-stop fade-in">
      <div class="plan-hdr">
        <div class="plan-title">STOP LOSS</div>
        <div class="plan-badge" style="background:var(--rdim);color:var(--red);border:1px solid var(--rbrd)">RISK CONTROL</div>
      </div>
      <div class="plan-level">
        <div class="pl-num">SL</div>
        <div style="flex:1">
          <div class="pl-price" style="color:var(--red)">${fp(stopLevel)}</div>
          <div class="pl-desc">2.5× ATR below entry. If ${TA_S.asset} closes below this level, the setup has failed. Exit and reassess. <strong style="color:var(--tx2)">For your long-term thesis</strong>: only hard-stop if price closes below this for 2 consecutive days. A single day doesn't invalidate years-long positions.</div>
        </div>
        <div class="pl-gain" style="color:var(--red)">${price && stopLevel ? '-' + ((price-stopLevel)/price*100).toFixed(1) + '%' : '—'}</div>
      </div>
      <div class="plan-level" style="background:var(--rdim)">
        <div style="flex:1;padding-left:0">
          <div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:9px;color:var(--amber);letter-spacing:1px;margin-bottom:4px">⚠️ TAX NOTE — YOUR SITUATION</div>
          <div class="pl-desc">You pay US capital gains as an expat. ST rate: <strong style="color:var(--red)">37%</strong> (under 12 months). LT rate: <strong style="color:var(--green)">23.8%</strong> (over 12 months). On a $100K gain, that's a $13,200 difference. Plan entries to hold through the 12-month mark where possible.</div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>

    <!-- All signals -->
    ${signalHTML}

    <div style="height:20px"></div>
  `;
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// DEMO DATA (fallback when no API key)
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function generateDemoData(asset) {
  const seeds = { CLOV:2.05, UNH:288, BTC:84000, ETH:2200, SOL:130 };
  const vols  = { CLOV:8000000, UNH:4000000, BTC:0, ETH:0, SOL:0 };
  const seed  = seeds[asset] || 100;
  const vol0  = vols[asset] || 0;
  const candles = [];
  let price = seed * (0.7 + Math.random() * 0.3);
  const now = Date.now();
  for (let i = 365; i >= 0; i--) {
    const ts = now - i * 86400000;
    const drift = (seed / price - 1) * 0.01 + (Math.random() - 0.48) * 0.03;
    const open = price;
    price = price * (1 + drift);
    const high = Math.max(open, price) * (1 + Math.random() * 0.015);
    const low  = Math.min(open, price) * (1 - Math.random() * 0.015);
    candles.push({ date: new Date(ts).toISOString().split('T')[0], ts, o:open, h:high, l:low, c:price, v: vol0 * (0.5 + Math.random()) });
  }
  return candles;
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// UTILITIES
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════

function fmtVol(v) {
  if (!v) return '—';
  if (v >= 1e9) return (v/1e9).toFixed(2) + 'B';
  if (v >= 1e6) return (v/1e6).toFixed(2) + 'M';
  if (v >= 1e3) return (v/1e3).toFixed(0) + 'K';
  return v.toString();
}


function updateMarketStatus() {
  const d = new Date();
  const h = d.getUTCHours() - 5; // EST approx
  const m = d.getUTCMinutes();
  const min = ((h + 24) % 24) * 60 + m;
  const day = d.getDay();
  const open = day > 0 && day < 6 && min >= 570 && min < 960;
  const _ms=document.getElementById('mkt-status'); if(_ms) _ms.textContent=open?'● MARKET OPEN':'○ MARKET CLOSED';
  if(_ms) _ms.style.color=open?'var(--green)':'var(--tx3)';
  const _ld=document.getElementById('live-dot'); if(_ld) _ld.style.background=open?'var(--green)':'var(--tx4)';
  const _lu=document.getElementById('last-update'); if(_lu) _lu.textContent='Updated '+new Date().toLocaleTimeString([],{hour:'2-digit',minute:'2-digit'});
}


// ── Robust JSON extractor (handles markdown fences + web_search tool responses)
function extractJSON(rawText) {
  if (!rawText) return null;
  let s = rawText.trim();
  // Strip leading ```json or ``` fence
  if (s.startsWith('```json')) s = s.slice(7);
  else if (s.startsWith('```')) s = s.slice(3);
  // Strip trailing ```
  if (s.endsWith('```')) s = s.slice(0, -3);
  s = s.trim();
  // Find outermost { }
  const first = s.indexOf('{');
  const last  = s.lastIndexOf('}');
  if (first < 0 || last <= first) return null;
  try {
    return JSON.parse(s.slice(first, last + 1));
  } catch(e) {
    // Try progressively smaller substrings from the end
    for (let end = last; end > first + 10; end--) {
      if (s[end] === '}') {
        try { return JSON.parse(s.slice(first, end + 1)); } catch(e2) {}
      }
    }
    return null;
  }
}

// ── Collect text from Claude API response (handles tool_use interleaving)
function extractResponseText(raw) {
  return (raw.content || [])
    .filter(b => b.type === 'text')
    .map(b => b.text)
    .join('\n');
}

// ── openChart: jump to CHARTS tab with any ticker ──────────────
function openChart(ticker) {
  showScreen('charts', document.getElementById('nb-charts'));
  initTA();
  setTimeout(() => {
    selectAsset(ticker);
  }, 100);
}

// ── renderTAAssetRow: build asset picker from all known tickers ─
function renderTAAssetRow() {
  const row = document.getElementById('ta-asset-row');
  if (!row) return;
  // Always-pinned crypto first
  const pinned = ['BTC','ETH','SOL'];
  // All from watchlist
  const wlTickers = (ST.watchlist||[]).map(w => ({ticker:w.ticker, name:w.name}));
  // All from pick universes
  const allPicks = [...(VALUE_PICKS||[]), ...(MOON_PICKS||[]), ...(BUZZ_PICKS||[])].map(p => ({ticker:p.ticker, name:p.name}));
  // Custom tickers added by user
  const customTickers = (TA_S.customTickers||[]).map(t => ({ticker:t, name:t}));
  
  // Deduplicate
  const seen = new Set(pinned);
  const dynamic = [];
  [...wlTickers, ...allPicks, ...customTickers].forEach(({ticker, name}) => {
    if (!seen.has(ticker)) { seen.add(ticker); dynamic.push({ticker, name}); }
  });

  const allTickers = [
    ...pinned.map(t => ({ticker:t, name:t})),
    ...dynamic,
    {ticker:'CUSTOM', name:'+ TICKER'}
  ];

  row.innerHTML = allTickers.map(({ticker, name}) => {
    if (ticker === 'CUSTOM') {
      return `<button class="asset-btn" onclick="promptCustom()" style="color:var(--tx4);white-space:nowrap">+ TICKER</button>`;
    }
    const isCurrent = ticker === TA_S.asset;
    const chgId = 'chg-' + ticker;
    return `<button class="asset-btn${isCurrent?' on':''}" data-asset="${ticker}" onclick="selectAsset('${ticker}')">
      ${ticker}<span class="a-chg" id="${chgId}">—</span>
    </button>`;
  }).join('');

  // Update change chips for any cached data
  allTickers.forEach(({ticker}) => {
    if (TA_S.data && TA_S.data[ticker] && TA_S.data[ticker].length > 1) {
      updateAssetChip(ticker, TA_S.data[ticker]);
    }
  });
}

function initTA() {
  if(TA_S.taInited) return;
  TA_S.taInited = true;
  renderTAAssetRow();
  checkAVBanner();
  // Set initial ticker name display
  const nameEl = document.getElementById('chart-ticker-name');
  const disp = document.getElementById('chart-active-ticker');
  if (nameEl && TA_S.asset) nameEl.textContent = TA_S.asset;
  if (disp && TA_S.asset) disp.style.display = 'flex';
  initCanvasEvents();
  updateMarketStatus();

  // Load all assets in background for chip prices
  ['BTC','ETH','SOL'].forEach(a => {
    loadCryptoData(a).then(c => {
      if (c) { TA_S.data[a] = c; updateAssetChip(a, c); }
    }).catch(() => { TA_S.data[a] = generateDemoData(a); });
  });

  // Load default
  try { loadAsset(TA_S.asset); } catch(e) { console.warn('initTA loadAsset:', e); }

  setInterval(updateMarketStatus, 60000);

  window.addEventListener('resize', () => {
    if (TA_S.tab === 'chart') scheduleRedraw();
  });
}
