const CRYPTO_CACHE_KEY  = 'forge_crypto_market';
const CRYPTO_CACHE_TTL  = 15 * 60 * 1000; // 15 min

// Sector / category tags per coin ID
const COIN_SECTORS = {
  bitcoin:'l1', ethereum:'l1', solana:'l1', cardano:'l1', avalanche:'l1',
  polkadot:'l1', 'near-protocol':'l1', cosmos:'l1', algorand:'l1',
  tron:'l1', 'internet-computer':'l1', aptos:'l1', sui:'l1', sei:'l1',
  uniswap:'defi', 'aave':'defi', 'maker':'defi', 'compound':'defi',
  'curve-dao-token':'defi', 'pancakeswap-token':'defi', 'lido-dao':'defi',
  'the-graph':'defi', 'synthetix-network-token':'defi', yearn:'defi',
  'fetch-ai':'ai', 'singularitynet':'ai', 'ocean-protocol':'ai',
  'render-token':'ai', 'akash-network':'ai', 'numeraire':'ai',
  'worldcoin-wld':'ai', 'bittensor':'ai',
  'ondo-finance':'rwa', 'centrifuge':'rwa', 'maple':'rwa',
  'goldfinch':'rwa', 'realtoken':'rwa', 'mantra':'rwa',
  'axie-infinity':'gaming', 'the-sandbox':'gaming', 'decentraland':'gaming',
  'immutable-x':'gaming', 'gala':'gaming', 'illuvium':'gaming',
  'stepn':'gaming', 'sky-mavis':'gaming',
  'dogecoin':'meme', 'shiba-inu':'meme', 'pepe':'meme',
  'floki':'meme', 'bonk':'meme', 'dogwifcoin':'meme',
};

const COIN_EMOJI = {
  bitcoin:'₿', ethereum:'Ξ', solana:'◎', cardano:'₳', avalanche:'🔺',
  polkadot:'●', 'near-protocol':'Ⓝ', cosmos:'⚛', tron:'T',
  dogecoin:'Ð', 'shiba-inu':'🐕', ripple:'✕', litecoin:'Ł',
  chainlink:'⬡', 'uniswap':'🦄', 'ondo-finance':'Ω',
};

let CR = {
  coins: [],
  filter: 'all',
  sort: 'rank',
  loaded: false,
  loading: false,
};

async function loadCryptoMarket(force = false) {
  if (CR.loading) return;
  // Cooldown: hard limit — no more than once per 60s (even forced refresh limited to 10s)
  const now = Date.now();
  const minWait = force ? 5000 : 30000;
  if (CR._lastAttempt && (now - CR._lastAttempt) < minWait) {
    const waitSec = Math.ceil((minWait - (now - CR._lastAttempt)) / 1000);
    // Show UI feedback instead of console spam
    const _crl = document.getElementById('cr-list');
    if (_crl && !CR.loaded) {
      _crl.innerHTML = '<div class="crypto-loading"><div class="crypto-loading-icon">⏳</div><div class="crypto-loading-txt" style="color:var(--amber)">Rate limited — wait ' + waitSec + 's then tap REFRESH</div></div>';
    }
    return;
  }
  CR._lastAttempt = now;

  // Try cache first
  if (!force) {
    try {
      const cached = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(CRYPTO_CACHE_KEY) || 'null');
      if (cached && (Date.now() - cached.ts) < CRYPTO_CACHE_TTL) {
        CR.coins = cached.coins;
        CR.loaded = true;
        renderCryptoHero(cached.global);
        renderCoinList();
        return;
      }
    } catch(e) {}
  }

  CR.loading = true;
  const _crl=document.getElementById('cr-list'); if(_crl) _crl.innerHTML = `
    <div class="crypto-loading">
      <div class="crypto-loading-icon">⬡</div>
      <div class="crypto-loading-txt">FETCHING TOP 100 COINS…</div>
    </div>`;

  try {
    // Fetch top 100 by market cap + global stats in parallel
    const [mktRes, globalRes, fgRes] = await Promise.allSettled([
      fetch('https://api.coingecko.com/api/v3/coins/markets?vs_currency=usd&order=market_cap_desc&per_page=100&page=1&sparkline=true&price_change_percentage=1h,24h,7d'),
      fetch('https://api.coingecko.com/api/v3/global'),
      fetch('https://api.alternative.me/fng/')
    ]);

    let coins = [];
    let globalData = null;

    if (mktRes.status === 'fulfilled' && mktRes.value?.ok) {
      coins = await mktRes.value.json();
    } else {
      const httpStatus = mktRes.value?.status;
      if (httpStatus === 429) {
        CR._lastAttempt = now + 50000; // extra 50s penalty on top of cooldown
        throw new Error('RATE_LIMITED');
      }
      // On any failure, try to use stale cache rather than erroring
      try {
        const stale = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(CRYPTO_CACHE_KEY)||'null');
        if (stale?.coins?.length) {
          CR.coins = stale.coins; CR.loaded = true;
          renderCryptoHero(stale.global);
          renderCoinList();
          CR.loading = false;
          return;
        }
      } catch(e2) {}
      throw new Error('CoinGecko markets API failed');
    }

    if (globalRes.status === 'fulfilled' && globalRes.value.ok) {
      globalData = (await globalRes.value.json()).data;
    }

    let fgVal = ST.fearGreed;
    if (fgRes.status === 'fulfilled' && fgRes.value.ok) {
      const fgd = await fgRes.value.json();
      fgVal = parseInt(fgd?.data?.[0]?.value || fgVal);
    }

    CR.coins = coins;
    CR.loaded = true;

    // Cache it
    try {
      localStorage.setItem(CRYPTO_CACHE_KEY, JSON.stringify({ ts: Date.now(), coins, global: globalData }));
    } catch(e) {}

    renderCryptoHero(globalData, fgVal);
    renderCoinList();

    // Also update main ST.cryptoData for brief pulse and deploy tab
    const btc = coins.find(c => c.id === 'bitcoin');
    const eth = coins.find(c => c.id === 'ethereum');
    const sol = coins.find(c => c.id === 'solana');
    if (btc) {
      ST.cryptoData = ST.cryptoData || {};
      ST.cryptoData.btc = { usd: btc.current_price, usd_24h_change: btc.price_change_percentage_24h };
      ST.cryptoData.bitcoin = { usd: btc.current_price, usd_24h_change: btc.price_change_percentage_24h };
    }
    if (eth) {
      ST.cryptoData.eth = { usd: eth.current_price, usd_24h_change: eth.price_change_percentage_24h };
      ST.cryptoData.ethereum = { usd: eth.current_price, usd_24h_change: eth.price_change_percentage_24h };
    }
    if (sol) {
      ST.cryptoData.sol = { usd: sol.current_price, usd_24h_change: sol.price_change_percentage_24h };
      ST.cryptoData.solana = { usd: sol.current_price, usd_24h_change: sol.price_change_percentage_24h };
    }
    updateBriefPulse();
    updateHeaderTape();

  } catch(err) {
    const isRateLimit = err.message === 'RATE_LIMITED' || err.message.includes('rate limit') || err.message.includes('RATE');
    const errMsg = isRateLimit
      ? '⚠ RATE LIMITED — CoinGecko free tier<br><small>Wait 60s then tap ⟳ REFRESH</small>'
      : '⚠ LOAD FAILED<br><small>Check connection, then tap ⟳ REFRESH</small>';
    const crList = document.getElementById('cr-list');
    if (crList) crList.innerHTML = '<div class="crypto-loading"><div class="crypto-loading-txt" style="color:var(--amber);font-size:12px;padding:20px;text-align:center">' + errMsg + '</div></div>';
  } finally {
    CR.loading = false;
  }
}

function renderCryptoHero(g, fg) {
  if (!g) return;
  const mcap = g.total_market_cap?.usd;
  const mcapChg = g.market_cap_change_percentage_24h_usd;
  const vol = g.total_volume?.usd;
  const btcDom = g.market_cap_percentage?.btc?.toFixed(1);
  const ethDom = g.market_cap_percentage?.eth?.toFixed(1);

  const mcapEl = document.getElementById('cr-total-mcap');
  if (mcapEl && mcap) mcapEl.textContent = '$' + fmtBig(mcap);

  const chgEl = document.getElementById('cr-total-chg');
  if (chgEl && mcapChg != null) {
    const up = mcapChg >= 0;
    chgEl.textContent = (up ? '▲ +' : '▼ ') + mcapChg.toFixed(2) + '% (24h)';
    chgEl.className = 'crypto-total-chg ' + (up ? 'up' : 'dn');
  }

  const el = (id, val) => { const e = document.getElementById(id); if(e && val != null) e.textContent = val; };
  el('cr-btc-dom', btcDom ? btcDom + '%' : '—');
  el('cr-eth-dom', ethDom ? ethDom + '%' : '—');
  el('cr-vol', vol ? '$' + fmtBig(vol) : '—');

  const fgV = fg ?? ST.fearGreed;
  if (fgV != null) {
    const fgEl = document.getElementById('cr-fg');
    if (fgEl) {
      const lbl = fgV <= 25 ? 'Extreme Fear' : fgV <= 45 ? 'Fear' : fgV <= 55 ? 'Neutral' : fgV <= 75 ? 'Greed' : 'Extreme Greed';
      const col = fgV <= 25 ? 'var(--red)' : fgV <= 45 ? 'var(--amber)' : fgV >= 75 ? 'var(--green)' : 'var(--tx)';
      fgEl.textContent = fgV + ' · ' + lbl;
      fgEl.style.color = col;
    }
  }

  // Dominance bar
  if (g.market_cap_percentage) {
    const dom = g.market_cap_percentage;
    const colors = { btc: '#F7931A', eth: '#627EEA', bnb: '#F3BA2F', sol: '#9945FF', xrp: '#346AA9' };
    const order = ['btc', 'eth', 'bnb', 'sol', 'xrp'];
    let otherPct = 100;
    const segs = order.map(k => {
      const pct = dom[k] || 0;
      otherPct -= pct;
      return { k: k.toUpperCase(), pct, col: colors[k] || '#888' };
    });
    segs.push({ k: 'OTHER', pct: Math.max(0, otherPct), col: '#334' });

    const barEl = document.getElementById('cr-dom-bar');
    if (barEl) barEl.style.display = 'block';

    const trackEl = document.getElementById('cr-dom-track');
    if (trackEl) trackEl.innerHTML = segs.map(s =>
      `<div class="dom-seg" style="width:${s.pct.toFixed(1)}%;background:${s.col}"></div>`
    ).join('');

    const legEl = document.getElementById('cr-dom-legend');
    if (legEl) legEl.innerHTML = segs.slice(0, 6).map(s =>
      `<div class="dom-leg-item"><div class="dom-leg-dot" style="background:${s.col}"></div><div class="dom-leg-txt">${s.k} ${s.pct.toFixed(1)}%</div></div>`
    ).join('');
  }
}

function setCryptoFilter(f, btn) {
  CR.filter = f;
  document.querySelectorAll('.cf-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('on'));
  if (btn) btn.classList.add('on');
  renderCoinList();
}

function setCryptoSort(s, btn) {
  CR.sort = s;
  document.querySelectorAll('.cs-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('on'));
  if (btn) btn.classList.add('on');
  renderCoinList();
}

function renderCoinList() {
  if (!CR.coins.length) return;
  const listEl = document.getElementById('cr-list');
  if (!listEl) return;

  // Filter
  let coins = CR.coins.filter(c => {
    if (CR.filter === 'all') return true;
    if (CR.filter === 'watchlist') return ST.watchlist.some(w => w.ticker === c.symbol?.toUpperCase() || w.ticker === c.id?.toUpperCase());
    return COIN_SECTORS[c.id] === CR.filter;
  });

  // Sort
  if (CR.sort === 'rank')   coins.sort((a, b) => a.market_cap_rank - b.market_cap_rank);
  if (CR.sort === 'change') coins.sort((a, b) => (b.price_change_percentage_24h || 0) - (a.price_change_percentage_24h || 0));
  if (CR.sort === 'mcap')   coins.sort((a, b) => (b.market_cap || 0) - (a.market_cap || 0));
  if (CR.sort === 'vol')    coins.sort((a, b) => (b.total_volume || 0) - (a.total_volume || 0));

  // Update count
  const countEl = document.getElementById('cr-count');
  if (countEl) countEl.textContent = coins.length + ' coins';

  if (!coins.length) {
    listEl.innerHTML = `<div class="crypto-loading"><div class="crypto-loading-txt">NO COINS IN THIS FILTER</div></div>`;
    return;
  }

  listEl.innerHTML = coins.map(c => renderCoinRow(c)).join('');
}

function renderCoinRow(c) {
  const chg24 = c.price_change_percentage_24h;
  const chgUp = chg24 >= 0;
  const sector = COIN_SECTORS[c.id];
  const inWL = ST.watchlist.some(w => w.ticker === c.symbol?.toUpperCase());
  const emoji = COIN_EMOJI[c.id] || c.symbol?.charAt(0)?.toUpperCase() || '?';

  // Sparkline mini SVG
  let spark = '';
  if (c.sparkline_in_7d?.price?.length) {
    const pts = c.sparkline_in_7d.price;
    const mn = Math.min(...pts), mx = Math.max(...pts);
    const norm = pts.filter((_, i) => i % 4 === 0); // downsample
    const w = 56, h = 24;
    const x = (i) => (i / (norm.length - 1)) * w;
    const y = (v) => h - ((v - mn) / (mx - mn || 1)) * h;
    const path = norm.map((v, i) => `${i === 0 ? 'M' : 'L'}${x(i).toFixed(1)},${y(v).toFixed(1)}`).join(' ');
    const lineColor = chgUp ? 'var(--green)' : 'var(--red)';
    spark = `<svg class="coin-sparkline" width="${w}" height="${h}" viewBox="0 0 ${w} ${h}"><path d="${path}" fill="none" stroke="${lineColor}" stroke-width="1.2" opacity=".7"/></svg>`;
  }

  const sectorColors = {
    l1: 'var(--blue)', defi: 'var(--purple)', ai: 'var(--teal)',
    rwa: 'var(--green)', gaming: 'var(--amber)', meme: 'var(--red)',
  };
  const sectorTag = sector ? `<span class="coin-tag" style="color:${sectorColors[sector]};border-color:${sectorColors[sector]}40">${sector.toUpperCase()}</span>` : '';
  const wlDot = inWL ? `<div class="coin-signal coin-in-wl" title="In watchlist"></div>` : '';

  const imgSrc = c.image || '';
  const iconHtml = imgSrc
    ? `<div class="coin-icon"><img src="${imgSrc}" alt="${c.symbol}" onerror="this.parentNode.textContent='${emoji}'"/></div>`
    : `<div class="coin-icon" style="font-size:13px;color:var(--tx2)">${emoji}</div>`;

  return `<div class="coin-row" onclick="openCoinDetail('${c.id}')">
    <div class="coin-rank">#${c.market_cap_rank || '—'}</div>
    ${iconHtml}
    <div class="coin-info">
      <div class="coin-name-row">
        <span class="coin-sym">${c.symbol?.toUpperCase()}</span>
        ${wlDot}
      </div>
      <div class="coin-name">${c.name}</div>
      <div class="coin-tags">${sectorTag}</div>
    </div>
    ${spark}
    <div class="coin-prices">
      <div class="coin-price">${fpCrypto(c.current_price)}</div>
      <div class="coin-chg ${chgUp ? 'up' : 'dn'}">${chgUp ? '+' : ''}${chg24?.toFixed(2) ?? '—'}%</div>
      <div class="coin-mcap">${c.market_cap ? fmtBig(c.market_cap) : '—'}</div>
    </div>
  </div>`;
}

function openCoinDetail(coinId) {
  const coin = CR.coins.find(c => c.id === coinId);
  if (!coin) return;
  const sym = coin.symbol?.toUpperCase();
  // Go to charts tab and load this coin
  showScreen('charts', document.getElementById('nb-charts'));
  setTimeout(() => {
    if (!TA_S.customTickers) TA_S.customTickers = [];
    if (!TA_S.customTickers.includes(sym)) TA_S.customTickers.push(sym);
    renderTAAssetRow();
    selectAsset(sym);
  }, 200);
}

// Price formatters for crypto
function fpCrypto(p) {
  if (!p && p !== 0) return '—';
  if (p >= 1000) return '$' + Math.round(p).toLocaleString();
  if (p >= 1)    return '$' + p.toFixed(2);
  if (p >= 0.01) return '$' + p.toFixed(4);
  if (p >= 0.0001) return '$' + p.toFixed(6);
  return '$' + p.toFixed(8);
}

function fmtBig(n) {
  if (!n) return '—';
  if (n >= 1e12) return (n / 1e12).toFixed(2) + 'T';
  if (n >= 1e9)  return (n / 1e9).toFixed(2) + 'B';
  if (n >= 1e6)  return (n / 1e6).toFixed(1) + 'M';
  if (n >= 1e3)  return (n / 1e3).toFixed(1) + 'K';
  return n.toFixed(0);
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// AUTONOMOUS SURVEILLANCE ENGINE
// Runs every N minutes. Fires alerts only on real signals.
// Sources: Finnhub (quotes/candles/news/institutional),
//          CoinGecko (crypto), Claude AI (news classification,
//          short interest proxy, options flow proxy)
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════


function svTickers(){
  const core=['HMBL','CLOV','UNH','SPY','VIX'];
  const wl=ST.watchlist.map(w=>w.ticker).filter(t=>!['BTC','ETH','SOL'].includes(t));
  return [...new Set([...core,...wl])];
}

async function runSurveillance(manual=false){
  if(SV.running)return;
  SV.running=true; setBtnScanning(true); setProgBar(0); svLog('clear');
  svLog('Scan started '+new Date().toLocaleTimeString(),'ok');
  const fired=[]; const tickers=svTickers(); const total=tickers.length+4; let done=0;
  const tick=(msg,cls)=>{done++;setProgBar(done/total*100);svLog(msg,cls);};
  try{
    for(const ticker of tickers){
      try{ const a=await scanTicker(ticker); a.forEach(x=>fired.push(x)); tick(ticker+': '+(a.length?a.map(x=>x.trigger).join(', '):'clean'),a.length?'warn':null); }
      catch(e){tick(ticker+': error','err');}
      await sleep(300);
    }
    try{ const a=await scanCrypto(); a.forEach(x=>fired.push(x)); tick('Crypto: '+(a.length?a.map(x=>x.trigger).join(', '):'clean'),a.length?'warn':null); }catch(e){tick('Crypto error','err');}
    try{ const a=scanMacro(); a.forEach(x=>fired.push(x)); tick('Macro: '+(a.length?a.map(x=>x.trigger).join(', '):'clean'),a.length?'warn':null); }catch(e){tick('Macro error','err');}
    try{ const a=await scanInstitutional(['CLOV','UNH','HMBL']); a.forEach(x=>fired.push(x)); tick('Institutional: '+(a.length?a.length+' changes':'no changes'),a.length?'warn':null); }catch(e){tick('Inst error','err');}
    try{ const a=await scanNewsAI(tickers); a.forEach(x=>fired.push(x)); tick('AI news: '+(a.length?a.length+' signals':'no triggers'),a.length?'warn':null); }catch(e){tick('AI news error','err');}
    setProgBar(100);
  }catch(e){svLog('Scan failed: '+e.message,'err');}
  SV.running=false; SV.lastScan=Date.now(); setBtnScanning(false);
  const sevOrder={critical:0,high:1,medium:2,info:3};
  fired.sort((a,b)=>sevOrder[a.severity]-sevOrder[b.severity]);
  SV.alerts=[...fired,...SV.alerts].slice(0,50);
  saveSVState(); renderSurveillanceAlerts(); updateScannerStats(); updateScannerTimestamps();
  const pushable=fired.filter(a=>['critical','high'].includes(a.severity));
  for(const a of pushable){
    await sendPush(a.ticker+' — '+a.trigger, a.headline);
    ST.alerts=[{id:Date.now()+Math.random(),ticker:a.ticker,type:'buy',rawTime:Date.now(),trigger:a.trigger,body:a.headline,price:ST.quotes[a.ticker]?.c||0,name:a.ticker,time:new Date().toLocaleString(),chips:[]},...ST.alerts].slice(0,60);
    try{localStorage.setItem('forge_al',JSON.stringify(ST.alerts));}catch(e){}
    const pip=document.getElementById('alert-pip');if(pip)pip.style.display='block';
    renderAlerts();
  }
  if(!fired.length)svLog('No signals. All clear.','ok'); else svLog(fired.length+' signal(s). '+pushable.length+' push sent.','warn');
}

async function scanTicker(ticker){
  const alerts=[]; const fh=ST.settings.fh; if(!fh)return alerts;
  const q=await fhGet('quote?symbol='+ticker); if(!q||!q.c)return alerts;
  const price=q.c,prevClose=q.pc,vol=q.v||0;
  const pctChg=prevClose?((price-prevClose)/prevClose*100):0;
  const macro=isMacroRiskOff()?'MACRO RISK-OFF — extra caution':'';
  const now=Math.floor(Date.now()/1000),d30=now-30*86400;
  const candles=await fhGet('stock/candle?symbol='+ticker+'&resolution=D&from='+d30+'&to='+now);
  let vol30avg=0,recentVols=[];
  if(candles?.v?.length>3){ recentVols=candles.v; vol30avg=recentVols.slice(0,-1).reduce((s,v)=>s+v,0)/(recentVols.length-1); }
  SV.prevData[ticker]={...(SV.prevData[ticker]||{}),vol,vol30avg,price,recentVols};

  if(vol30avg>0&&vol>vol30avg*5){
    const ratio=(vol/vol30avg).toFixed(1);
    alerts.push(buildAlert(ticker,'VOLUME SPIKE '+ratio+'x',
      ticker+' volume is '+ratio+'x its 30-day average ('+fmtBig(vol)+' vs avg '+fmtBig(vol30avg)+')',
      vol>vol30avg*10?'critical':'high', assessVol(ticker,vol,vol30avg,pctChg,true),macro));
  }
  if(vol>1e9) alerts.push(buildAlert(ticker,'VOLUME >1B SHARES',ticker+' traded over 1B shares today — extreme OTC activity','critical',assessVol(ticker,vol,vol30avg,pctChg,false),macro));
  if(recentVols.length>=4){
    const last3=recentVols.slice(-4,-1);
    if(last3[1]>last3[0]&&last3[2]>last3[1]){
      const priceDelta=candles?.c?((candles.c.slice(-1)[0]-candles.c.slice(-4)[0])/candles.c.slice(-4)[0]*100):0;
      if(Math.abs(priceDelta)<5) alerts.push(buildAlert(ticker,'VOL RISING 3 DAYS / PRICE FLAT',ticker+' volume rising 3 consecutive days while price stayed flat — classic accumulation','high','B — POTENTIALLY SUSTAINABLE',macro));
    }
  }
  if(recentVols.length>=3){
    const [d2,d1]=recentVols.slice(-3,-1);
    if(d2>0&&d1>d2*2) alerts.push(buildAlert(ticker,'VOLUME ACCELERATION 2x',ticker+' volume doubled day-over-day: '+fmtBig(d2)+' to '+fmtBig(d1),'high',assessVol(ticker,vol,vol30avg,pctChg,false),macro));
  }
  if(Math.abs(pctChg)>15){
    const dir=pctChg>0?'UP':'DOWN';
    alerts.push(buildAlert(ticker,'PRICE '+dir+' '+Math.abs(pctChg).toFixed(1)+'%',
      ticker+' moved '+(pctChg>0?'+':'')+pctChg.toFixed(1)+'% today.',
      Math.abs(pctChg)>30?'critical':'high',assessVol(ticker,vol,vol30avg,pctChg,pctChg>0),macro));
  }
  try{
    const metrics=await fhGet('stock/metric?symbol='+ticker+'&metric=all');
    const shares=(metrics?.metric?.sharesOutstanding||0)*1e6;
    if(shares>0&&vol>shares*0.5){
      const pct=((vol/shares)*100).toFixed(0);
      alerts.push(buildAlert(ticker,'FLOAT TURNOVER '+pct+'%',ticker+' traded '+pct+'% of total shares outstanding today',vol>shares?'critical':'high',assessVol(ticker,vol,vol30avg,pctChg,false),macro));
    }
  }catch(e){}
  return alerts;
}

async function scanCrypto(){
  const alerts=[]; const coins=CR.coins||[]; const macro=isMacroRiskOff()?'MACRO RISK-OFF':'';
  const btc=coins.find(c=>c.id==='bitcoin')||{};
  const btcChg=btc.price_change_percentage_24h||0;
  if(btcChg<-8) alerts.push(buildAlert('BTC','CRASH '+btcChg.toFixed(1)+'%','Bitcoin dropped '+Math.abs(btcChg).toFixed(1)+'% in 24h. Potential capitulation zone.',btcChg<-15?'critical':'high','B — POTENTIAL ACCUMULATION ZONE',macro));
  if(btcChg>8)  alerts.push(buildAlert('BTC','SURGE +'+btcChg.toFixed(1)+'%','Bitcoin up '+btcChg.toFixed(1)+'% in 24h. Check for continuation or local top.','medium','UNCLEAR — MONITOR',macro));
  const fg=ST.fearGreed;
  if(fg!=null&&fg<=20) alerts.push(buildAlert('CRYPTO','EXTREME FEAR F&G='+fg,'Fear & Greed index at '+fg+' — historically a strong long-term accumulation signal.','high','B — HIGH-QUALITY ACCUMULATION SIGNAL',macro));
  if(fg!=null&&fg>=85) alerts.push(buildAlert('CRYPTO','EXTREME GREED F&G='+fg,'Fear & Greed at '+fg+' — Extreme Greed. Historically precedes corrections.','medium','A — CAUTION, NOT A BUY SIGNAL',macro));
  const bigMovers=coins.filter(c=>c.id!=='bitcoin'&&Math.abs(c.price_change_percentage_24h||0)>20);
  if(bigMovers.length>=5) alerts.push(buildAlert('ALTS',bigMovers.length+' ALTCOINS >20% 24H',bigMovers.length+' altcoins moved >20% today: '+bigMovers.slice(0,3).map(c=>c.symbol?.toUpperCase()).join(', '),'medium','MONITOR — ALT SEASON CONDITIONS',macro));
  return alerts;
}

function scanMacro(){
  const alerts=[]; const vix=ST.quotes['VIX']; const spy=ST.quotes['SPY'];
  if(vix?.c){
    if(vix.c>35) alerts.push(buildAlert('VIX','SPIKE TO '+vix.c.toFixed(1),'VIX hit '+vix.c.toFixed(1)+' — severe market stress. Avoid new speculative entries.',vix.c>45?'critical':'high','MACRO RISK — CAUTION',''));
    else if(vix.c>25) alerts.push(buildAlert('VIX','ELEVATED AT '+vix.c.toFixed(1),'VIX at '+vix.c.toFixed(1)+' — elevated volatility. Speculative entries carry extra risk.','medium','MACRO CAUTION',''));
  }
  if(spy?.c&&spy?.pc){
    const spyChg=((spy.c-spy.pc)/spy.pc*100);
    if(spyChg<-2.5) alerts.push(buildAlert('S&P500','DOWN '+spyChg.toFixed(1)+'%','S&P 500 dropped '+Math.abs(spyChg).toFixed(1)+'% today. Delay speculative entries.',spyChg<-4?'critical':'high','MACRO RISK — WAIT',''));
  }
  return alerts;
}

async function scanInstitutional(tickers){
  const alerts=[]; const fh=ST.settings.fh; if(!fh)return alerts;
  const BIG=['blackrock','vanguard','goldman','state street','fidelity','citadel','renaissance'];
  for(const ticker of tickers){
    try{
      const data=await fhGet('stock/institutional-ownership?symbol='+ticker);
      if(!data?.ownership?.length)continue;
      const prev=SV.prevData[ticker]?.institutional||[];
      data.ownership.forEach(inst=>{
        const name=(inst.name||'').toLowerCase();
        if(!BIG.some(b=>name.includes(b)))return;
        const prevInst=prev.find(p=>p.name===inst.name);
        if(!prevInst&&inst.share>100000){
          alerts.push(buildAlert(ticker,'NEW POSITION: '+(inst.name||'').toUpperCase(),(inst.name||'?')+' opened new position in '+ticker+' with '+fmtBig(inst.share)+' shares','high','B — INSTITUTIONAL VALIDATION',''));
        } else if(prevInst){
          const pctChg=prevInst.share>0?((inst.share-prevInst.share)/prevInst.share*100):0;
          if(pctChg>20&&inst.share>50000) alerts.push(buildAlert(ticker,(inst.name||'').toUpperCase()+' +'+pctChg.toFixed(0)+'%',(inst.name||'?')+' increased '+ticker+' position by '+pctChg.toFixed(0)+'%','high','B — INSTITUTIONAL ACCUMULATION',''));
          else if(pctChg<-25&&prevInst.share>100000) alerts.push(buildAlert(ticker,(inst.name||'').toUpperCase()+' REDUCED '+Math.abs(pctChg).toFixed(0)+'%',(inst.name||'?')+' reduced '+ticker+' by '+Math.abs(pctChg).toFixed(0)+'%','medium','MONITOR — INSTITUTIONAL EXIT',''));
        }
      });
      SV.prevData[ticker]={...SV.prevData[ticker],institutional:data.ownership};
      await sleep(400);
    }catch(e){}
  }
  return alerts;
}

async function scanNewsAI(tickers){
  const alerts=[]; const ak=ST.settings.ak; if(!ak)return alerts;
  const allNews={};
  for(const ticker of ['HMBL','CLOV','UNH']){
    try{
      const to=new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
      const from=new Date(Date.now()-2*86400000).toISOString().split('T')[0];
      const news=await fhGet('company-news?symbol='+ticker+'&from='+from+'&to='+to);
      if(news?.length) allNews[ticker]=news.slice(0,5).map(n=>n.headline).join(' | ');
      await sleep(300);
    }catch(e){}
  }
  if(!Object.keys(allNews).length)return alerts;
  const prompt='You are a market surveillance AI. Analyze these recent news headlines and return ONLY valid JSON (no markdown, no backticks).\n\nHeadlines:\n'+Object.entries(allNews).map(([t,h])=>t+': '+h).join('\n')+'\n\nFor each ticker, identify if ANY of these signals are present: SQUEEZE SETUP (short squeeze, gamma squeeze, OTM calls, unusual options), CATALYST (partnership, acquisition, AI pivot, earnings surprise, contract win), PUMP WARNING (stock promotion, dubious PR, dilution, toxic financing), RESTRUCTURING (reverse split, ticker change, CEO change), MEDICAL (MCR improvement, membership growth, CMS change for CLOV).\n\nReturn ONLY this JSON: {"signals":[{"ticker":"TICKER","type":"SQUEEZE|CATALYST|PUMP|RESTRUCTURING|MEDICAL","severity":"critical|high|medium|info","trigger":"short label","headline":"one sentence summary","verdict":"A — PUMP/SHORT-LIVED or B — POTENTIALLY SUSTAINABLE or UNCLEAR","why":"2-3 bullet explanation"}]}\n\nOnly include genuinely significant signals. Return empty signals array if nothing material.';
  try{
    const res=await fetch('https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages',{method:'POST',headers:{'Content-Type':'application/json','anthropic-version':'2023-06-01','anthropic-dangerous-direct-browser-access':'true','x-api-key':ak},body:JSON.stringify({model:'claude-sonnet-4-20250514',max_tokens:1000,messages:[{role:'user',content:prompt}]})});
    if(!res.ok){console.warn('scanNewsAI API error:',res.status);return alerts;}
    const raw=await res.json();
    const text=extractResponseText(raw);
    const parsed=extractJSON(text);
    if(!parsed)return alerts;
    (parsed.signals||[]).forEach(s=>alerts.push({id:Date.now()+Math.random(),ticker:s.ticker,trigger:s.trigger,headline:s.headline,severity:s.severity||'medium',verdict:s.verdict||'UNCLEAR',why:s.why||'',source:'AI_NEWS',macro:isMacroRiskOff()?'MACRO RISK-OFF — extra caution':'',ts:Date.now()}));
  }catch(e){}
  return alerts;
}

function buildAlert(ticker,trigger,headline,severity,verdict,macro){
  return{id:Date.now()+Math.random(),ticker,trigger,headline,severity,verdict,why:'',source:'AUTO',macro,ts:Date.now()};
}
function assessVol(ticker,vol,vol30avg,pctChg,priceUp){
  const ratio=vol30avg>0?vol/vol30avg:0;
  if(ratio>10&&pctChg>30)return'A — LIKELY PUMP (extreme vol+price, no confirmation)';
  if(ratio>5&&pctChg>15)return'A — LIKELY PUMP (monitor for reversal)';
  if(ratio>3&&pctChg<5)return'B — POTENTIALLY SUSTAINABLE (vol without price = accumulation)';
  if(!priceUp&&ratio>3)return'B — POSSIBLE ACCUMULATION (volume on flat/down price)';
  return'UNCLEAR — AWAIT CATALYST CONFIRMATION';
}
function isMacroRiskOff(){
  const vix=ST.quotes['VIX']?.c; const spy=ST.quotes['SPY'];
  if(vix&&vix>28)return true;
  if(spy?.c&&spy?.pc&&((spy.c-spy.pc)/spy.pc*100)<-2)return true;
  return false;
}
function sleep(ms){return new Promise(r=>setTimeout(r,ms));}

function renderSurveillanceAlerts(){
  const wrap=document.getElementById('sv-alerts-wrap'); if(!wrap)return;
  if(!SV.alerts.length){
    wrap.innerHTML='<div class="scan-empty"><div class="scan-empty-icon">✅</div><div class="scan-empty-h">ALL CLEAR</div><div class="scan-empty-sub">No signals in last scan.<br>Auto-monitoring active.</div></div>';
    return;
  }
  const groups={critical:[],high:[],medium:[],info:[]};
  SV.alerts.forEach(a=>(groups[a.severity]||groups.info).push(a));
  let html='';
  [['critical','🔴 CRITICAL'],['high','🟡 HIGH PRIORITY'],['medium','🔵 MEDIUM'],['info','INFORMATIONAL']].forEach(([sev,lbl])=>{
    if(!groups[sev].length)return;
    html+='<div class="scan-section-hdr"><div class="ssh-title">'+lbl+'</div><div class="ssh-line"></div><div class="ssh-count">'+groups[sev].length+'</div></div>';
    groups[sev].forEach(a=>{html+=renderSVAlert(a);});
  });
  wrap.innerHTML=html;
}

function renderSVAlert(a){
  const isPump=a.verdict?.startsWith('A'),isSustain=a.verdict?.startsWith('B');
  const vcls=isPump?'sv-pump':isSustain?'sv-sustainable':'sv-unclear';
  const vtxt=isPump?'A — LIKELY PUMP':isSustain?'B — SUSTAINABLE':'UNCLEAR';
  const ago=a.ts?timeSince(a.ts):'';
  const why=Array.isArray(a.why)?a.why.map(l=>'\u2022 '+l).join('<br>'):(a.why||'');
  const tid=String(a.id).replace(/'/g,'');
  const tticker=String(a.ticker).replace(/'/g,'');
  return [
    '<div class="sv-alert sev-'+a.severity+'">',
      '<div class="sv-alert-hdr">',
        '<div class="sv-sev-badge">'+a.severity.toUpperCase()+'</div>',
        '<div class="sv-ticker">'+tticker+'</div>',
        '<div class="sv-trigger">'+a.trigger+'</div>',
        '<div class="sv-time">'+ago+'</div>',
      '</div>',
      '<div class="sv-alert-body">',
        '<div class="sv-verdict"><span class="sv-vtype '+vcls+'">'+vtxt+'</span></div>',
        '<div class="sv-headline">'+a.headline+'</div>',
        (why ? '<div class="sv-why">'+why+'</div>' : ''),
        (a.macro ? '<div class="sv-macro-warn">⚠️ '+a.macro+'</div>' : ''),
        '<div class="sv-actions">',
          '<button class="sv-act-btn primary" onclick="openChart(\''+tticker+'\')">\ud83d\udcc8 CHART</button>',
          '<button class="sv-act-btn" onclick="runAIForTicker(\''+tticker+'\')">\ud83e\udd16 AI ANALYSIS</button>',
          '<button class="sv-act-btn" onclick="dismissSVAlert(\''+tid+'\')">\u2715 DISMISS</button>',
        '</div>',
      '</div>',
    '</div>'
  ].join('');
}

function dismissSVAlert(id){SV.alerts=SV.alerts.filter(a=>String(a.id)!==String(id));saveSVState();renderSurveillanceAlerts();updateScannerStats();}
function updateScannerStats(){
  const c={critical:0,high:0,medium:0,info:0};
  SV.alerts.forEach(a=>c[a.severity]++);
  ['crit','high','med','watch'].forEach((k,i)=>{const sev=['critical','high','medium','info'][i];const el=document.getElementById('sv-n-'+k);if(el)el.textContent=c[sev];});
  const pip=document.getElementById('scanner-pip');
  if(pip)pip.style.display=(c.critical+c.high>0)?'block':'none';
}
function updateScannerTimestamps(){
  const lastEl=document.getElementById('sv-last'),nextEl=document.getElementById('sv-next'),dot=document.getElementById('sv-dot');
  if(lastEl&&SV.lastScan)lastEl.textContent='Last: '+timeSince(SV.lastScan);
  if(nextEl&&SV.autoOn&&SV.lastScan){const ms=SV.intervalMs-(Date.now()-SV.lastScan);if(ms>0)nextEl.textContent='Next in '+Math.ceil(ms/60000)+'m';}
  if(dot)dot.className='scan-live-dot'+(SV.autoOn?' active':'');
}
function setBtnScanning(on){const btn=document.getElementById('sv-run-btn');if(!btn)return;btn.textContent=on?'⏳ SCANNING…':'⚡ SCAN NOW';btn.className='scan-run-btn'+(on?' scanning':'');btn.disabled=on;}
function setProgBar(pct){const bar=document.getElementById('sv-prog');if(bar)bar.style.width=pct+'%';}
function svLog(msg,cls){
  if(msg==='clear'){SV.logLines=[];}
  else{const t=new Date().toLocaleTimeString('en',{hour:'2-digit',minute:'2-digit',second:'2-digit'});SV.logLines.unshift({msg:'['+t+'] '+msg,cls:cls||''});SV.logLines=SV.logLines.slice(0,12);}
  const logEl=document.getElementById('sv-log');if(!logEl)return;
  logEl.innerHTML=SV.logLines.map(l=>'<div class="scan-log-line '+l.cls+'">'+l.msg+'</div>').join('');
}
function timeSince(ts){const s=Math.floor((Date.now()-ts)/1000);if(s<60)return s+'s ago';if(s<3600)return Math.floor(s/60)+'m ago';return Math.floor(s/3600)+'h ago';}
function runAIForTicker(ticker){showScreen('analyze',document.getElementById('nb-analyze'));setTimeout(()=>openDetail(ticker),100);}
function setScanInterval(mins){SV.intervalMs=parseInt(mins)*60*1000;if(SV.autoOn){clearInterval(SV.timer);SV.timer=setInterval(()=>runSurveillance().catch(e=>console.warn('sv:',e)),SV.intervalMs);}saveSVState();}
function toggleSurveillance(el){
  SV.autoOn=!SV.autoOn;
  const tog=document.getElementById('sv-auto-tog');if(tog)tog.classList.toggle('on',SV.autoOn);
  if(SV.autoOn){SV.timer=setInterval(()=>runSurveillance().catch(e=>console.warn('sv:',e)),SV.intervalMs);svLog('Auto surveillance ON — every '+SV.intervalMs/60000+'m','ok');runSurveillance().catch(e=>console.warn('sv:',e));}
  else{clearInterval(SV.timer);SV.timer=null;svLog('Auto surveillance OFF','err');}
  saveSVState();updateScannerTimestamps();
}
function saveSVState(){try{localStorage.setItem(SV_STORE_KEY,JSON.stringify({autoOn:SV.autoOn,intervalMs:SV.intervalMs,lastScan:SV.lastScan,prevData:SV.prevData}));localStorage.setItem(SV_ALERTS_KEY,JSON.stringify(SV.alerts.slice(0,50)));}catch(e){}}
function loadSVState(){
  try{
    const s=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(SV_STORE_KEY)||'null');
    if(s){SV.autoOn=!!s.autoOn;SV.intervalMs=s.intervalMs||SV.intervalMs;SV.lastScan=s.lastScan||null;SV.prevData=s.prevData||{};}
    SV.alerts=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(SV_ALERTS_KEY)||'[]');
  }catch(e){}
}
function initScannerView(){
  loadSVState();renderSurveillanceAlerts();updateScannerStats();updateScannerTimestamps();
  if(SV.autoOn&&!SV.timer){SV.timer=setInterval(()=>runSurveillance().catch(e=>console.warn('sv:',e)),SV.intervalMs);const tog=document.getElementById('sv-auto-tog');if(tog)tog.classList.add('on');}
  const sel=document.getElementById('sv-interval');if(sel)sel.value=String(SV.intervalMs/60000);
}


// MORNING INTELLIGENCE BRIEF ENGINE
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════

const BRIEF_CACHE_KEY = 'forge_brief';
const BRIEF_TTL = 1 * 60 * 60 * 1000; // 1 hour

// Auto-refresh schedule: pre-market (7am), midday (12pm), after-close (5pm) Dubai time

// Update countdown timer on Brief tab

// Update date header
function updateBriefDate() {
  const el = document.getElementById('brief-date');
  if (!el) return;
  const now = new Date();
  const days = ['SUNDAY','MONDAY','TUESDAY','WEDNESDAY','THURSDAY','FRIDAY','SATURDAY'];
  const months = ['JAN','FEB','MAR','APR','MAY','JUN','JUL','AUG','SEP','OCT','NOV','DEC'];
  el.textContent = `${days[now.getDay()]} · ${months[now.getMonth()]} ${now.getDate()}, ${now.getFullYear()}`;
}

// Update market pulse cards from live data already in ST
function updateBriefPulse() {
  const q = ST.quotes || {};
  const cg = ST.cryptoData;
  const fg = ST.fearGreed;
  // Safe pct change — guard against pc=0 or undefined, fall back to dp field
  function safePct(qt) {
    if (!qt) return null;
    if (qt.pc > 0) return ((qt.c - qt.pc) / qt.pc * 100).toFixed(2);
    if (qt.dp != null) return qt.dp.toFixed(2);
    if (qt.pct != null) return qt.pct.toFixed(2);
    return null;
  }
  const pulse = [
    { lbl:'S&P 500', val: q['SPY']?fp(q['SPY'].c):(ST.lastClose['SPY']?fp(ST.lastClose['SPY'].price)+'*':'—'), chg: q['SPY']?safePct(q['SPY']):(ST.lastClose['SPY']?safePct({...ST.lastClose['SPY'],c:ST.lastClose['SPY'].price,pc:ST.lastClose['SPY'].prev}):null) },
    { lbl:'BTC',     val: (cg?.btc||cg?.bitcoin) ? fp((cg.btc||cg.bitcoin).usd) : '—', chg: (cg?.btc||cg?.bitcoin) ? (cg.btc||cg.bitcoin).usd_24h_change?.toFixed(2) : null },
    { lbl:'VIX',     val: q['VIX']  ? fp(q['VIX'].c)      : '—', chg: safePct(q['VIX']) },
    { lbl:'CLOV', val: q['CLOV']?fp(q['CLOV'].c):(ST.lastClose['CLOV']?fp(ST.lastClose['CLOV'].price)+'*':'—'), chg: q['CLOV']?safePct(q['CLOV']):(ST.lastClose['CLOV']?null:null) },
    { lbl:'UNH', val: q['UNH']?fp(q['UNH'].c):(ST.lastClose['UNH']?fp(ST.lastClose['UNH'].price)+'*':'—'), chg: q['UNH']?safePct(q['UNH']):(ST.lastClose['UNH']?null:null) },
    { lbl:'FEAR&GREED', val: fg ? fg+'' : '—', chg: null, label: ST.fearGreedLabel },
  ];
  const container = document.getElementById('brief-pulse');
  if (!container) return;
  container.innerHTML = pulse.map(p => {
    const chgNum = parseFloat(p.chg);
    const dir = isNaN(chgNum) ? 'flat' : chgNum > 0 ? 'up' : chgNum < 0 ? 'dn' : 'flat';
    const chgColor = dir === 'up' ? 'var(--green)' : dir === 'dn' ? 'var(--red)' : 'var(--tx3)';
    const chgStr = p.label ? `<div class="bp-chg" style="color:${chgColor}">${p.label}</div>`
      : p.chg != null ? `<div class="bp-chg" style="color:${chgColor}">${chgNum > 0 ? '+' : ''}${chgNum}%</div>` : '';
    return `<div class="bp-card bp-${dir}">
      <div class="bp-lbl">${p.lbl}</div>
      <div class="bp-val">${p.val}</div>
      ${chgStr}
    </div>`;
  }).join('');
}

// Render the AI brief content
function renderBriefContent(data) {
  const el = document.getElementById('brief-content');
  if (!el || !data) return;

  let html = '';

  // ── WHAT MOVED TODAY ────────────────────────────────
  if (data.movers && data.movers.length) {
    html += `<div class="brief-sec"><div class="brief-sec-hdr">
      <div class="brief-sec-icon">🔥</div>
      <div class="brief-sec-title">WHAT MOVED TODAY</div>
      <div class="brief-sec-line"></div>
      <div class="brief-sec-count">${data.movers.length} STORIES</div>
    </div></div>`;
    data.movers.forEach(s => {
      html += renderBriefCard(s);
    });
  }

  // ── BREWING / STEALTH SIGNALS ────────────────────────
  if (data.stealth && data.stealth.length) {
    html += `<div class="brief-sec" style="margin-top:4px"><div class="brief-sec-hdr">
      <div class="brief-sec-icon">🕵️</div>
      <div class="brief-sec-title">STEALTH SIGNALS</div>
      <div class="brief-sec-line"></div>
      <div class="brief-sec-count">NOBODY'S WATCHING</div>
    </div></div>`;
    data.stealth.forEach(s => {
      html += `<div class="brief-stealth">
        <div class="bst-hdr">
          <div class="bst-icon">${s.icon || '📡'}</div>
          <div class="bst-title">${s.title}</div>
          <div class="bst-horizon">${s.horizon || 'DEVELOPING'}</div>
        </div>
        <div class="bst-body">${s.body}</div>
        ${s.tickers ? `<div class="bst-tickers">${s.tickers.map(t => `<span class="bst-tick" style="color:var(--blue);cursor:pointer" onclick="openChart('${t}')">${t}</span>`).join('')}</div>` : ''}
      </div>`;
    });
  }

  // ── MARKET SUMMARY ───────────────────────────────────
  if (data.summary) {
    html += `<div class="brief-sec" style="margin-top:4px"><div class="brief-sec-hdr">
      <div class="brief-sec-icon">📊</div>
      <div class="brief-sec-title">MARKET SUMMARY</div>
      <div class="brief-sec-line"></div>
    </div></div>
    <div class="brief-card" style="cursor:default">
      <div class="brief-card-inner">
        <div class="bc-body" style="font-size:12px;color:var(--tx2);line-height:1.75">${data.summary}</div>
      </div>
    </div>`;
  }

  // ── WATCHLIST CANDIDATES ─────────────────────────────
  if (data.candidates && data.candidates.length) {
    html += `<div class="brief-sec" style="margin-top:4px"><div class="brief-sec-hdr">
      <div class="brief-sec-icon">🎯</div>
      <div class="brief-sec-title">WATCHLIST CANDIDATES</div>
      <div class="brief-sec-line"></div>
      <div class="brief-sec-count">FUTURE TARGETS</div>
    </div></div>`;
    data.candidates.forEach(c => {
      const inWL = ST.watchlist.some(w => w.ticker === c.ticker);
      html += `<div class="brief-candidate">
        <div class="bcan-ticker" style="color:var(--green)">${c.ticker}</div>
        <div class="bcan-info">
          <div class="bcan-name">${c.name}</div>
          <div class="bcan-why">${c.why}</div>
        </div>
        <button class="bcan-add ${inWL ? 'added' : ''}" id="bcan-${c.ticker}"
          onclick="${inWL ? '' : `addToWL('${c.ticker}','${c.name}');document.getElementById('bcan-${c.ticker}').textContent='✓ ADDED';document.getElementById('bcan-${c.ticker}').classList.add('added')`}">
          ${inWL ? '✓ IN LIST' : '+ ADD'}
        </button>
      </div>`;
    });
  }

  el.innerHTML = html;
}

function renderBriefCard(s) {
  const tagClass = {
    'MOVING': 'bc-tag-heat', 'BREAKING': 'bc-tag-heat',
    'WATCH': 'bc-tag-watch', 'DEVELOPING': 'bc-tag-watch',
    'BREWING': 'bc-tag-brew', 'UNDER RADAR': 'bc-tag-brew',
    'MACRO': 'bc-tag-macro', 'POLICY': 'bc-tag-macro',
    'ENTRY': 'bc-tag-entry', 'SETUP': 'bc-tag-entry',
    'STEALTH': 'bc-tag-stealth',
  }[s.tag?.toUpperCase()] || 'bc-tag-watch';

  const actionClass = s.action === 'BUY ZONE' ? 'act-buy' : s.action ? 'act-watch' : '';

  return `<div class="brief-card" onclick="${s.ticker ? `openChart('${s.ticker}')` : ''}">
    <div class="brief-card-inner">
      <div class="bc-tag-row">
        <span class="bc-tag ${tagClass}">${s.tag || 'WATCH'}</span>
        ${s.ticker ? `<span class="bc-ticker" style="color:var(--blue);cursor:pointer">${s.ticker}</span>` : ''}
        ${s.sector ? `<span class="bc-ticker" style="color:var(--tx4)">${s.sector}</span>` : ''}
      </div>
      <div class="bc-headline">${s.headline}</div>
      <div class="bc-body">${s.body}</div>
      <div class="bc-footer">
        <div class="bc-relevance">Impact: <span>${s.impact || 'MEDIUM'}</span></div>
        ${s.action ? `<div class="bc-action ${actionClass}">${s.action}</div>` : ''}
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>`;
}

// Main load function
async function loadBrief(force = false) {
  updateBriefDate();
  updateBriefPulse();

  // Check cache
  if (!force) {
    try {
      const cached = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(BRIEF_CACHE_KEY) || 'null');
      if (cached && (Date.now() - cached.ts) < BRIEF_TTL) {
        renderBriefContent(cached.data);
        setBriefStatus('ready', cached.ts);
        return;
      }
    } catch(e) {}
  }

  setBriefStatus('loading');

  const today = new Date().toLocaleDateString('en-US', {weekday:'long', year:'numeric', month:'long', day:'numeric'});
  const btcPrice = ST.cryptoData?.btc?.usd ? `$${Math.round(ST.cryptoData.btc.usd).toLocaleString()}` : 'unknown';
  const fg = ST.fearGreed ? `${ST.fearGreed} (${ST.fearGreedLabel})` : 'unknown';

  const prompt = `Today is ${today}. You are a market intelligence analyst for a high-net-worth US expat investor in Dubai. Portfolio: CLOV 90K shares ~$2.05, UNH 140 shares ~$288, $475K cash ready to deploy. BTC currently ${btcPrice}. Fear & Greed: ${fg}.

CRITICAL: Do NOT mention CLOV, UNH, HMBL, or BTC in movers or stealth — those are monitored separately. Scan the ENTIRE market for fresh stories the investor has not seen yet.

CRITICAL: Return ONLY raw JSON starting with { and ending with } - no markdown fences, no backticks, no explanation:

{
  "movers": [
    {
      "tag": "MOVING|BREAKING|WATCH|DEVELOPING|MACRO|ENTRY",
      "ticker": "TICKER or null",
      "sector": "sector label",
      "headline": "punchy 1-line headline",
      "body": "2-3 sentences. What happened, why it matters, what to watch.",
      "impact": "HIGH|MEDIUM|LOW",
      "action": "WATCH|HOLD|BUY ZONE|AVOID or null"
    }
  ],
  "stealth": [
    {
      "icon": "emoji",
      "title": "SIGNAL TITLE IN CAPS",
      "horizon": "NEAR-TERM|6-12 MONTHS|1-3 YEARS|DEVELOPING",
      "body": "2-3 sentences on a brewing story with zero mainstream coverage. Regulatory, demographic, geopolitical, supply chain, niche tech. Be specific.",
      "tickers": ["TICKER1","TICKER2"]
    }
  ],
  "summary": "3-4 sentences. Market character today: risk-on or risk-off, what is driving it, what smart money is doing, one key thing to watch this week.",
  "candidates": [
    {
      "ticker": "TICKER",
      "name": "Company Name",
      "why": "1 sentence: why this is worth watching now"
    }
  ]
}

Rules:
- movers: EXACTLY 8 items covering broad market — tech, macro, commodities, international, small caps, biotech, defense, energy, crypto, ETFs. Fresh names only, no portfolio stocks.
- stealth: EXACTLY 4 truly under-the-radar signals. Not portfolio stocks. Think like a macro hedge fund.
- candidates: 3 new asymmetric setups under $5B market cap. Do NOT suggest CLOV, UNH, HMBL, BTC.
- Be specific. Name prices, percentages, dates, catalysts. No vague statements.
`;

  if (!ST.settings.ak) {
    setBriefStatus('error');
    const bcEl=document.getElementById('brief-content'); if(bcEl) bcEl.innerHTML = '<div class="brief-empty"><div class="brief-empty-icon">🔑</div><div class="brief-empty-txt">ADD ANTHROPIC API KEY IN SETTINGS</div></div>';
    return;
  }

  try {
    // Direct API call — no tools, no loop. Clean JSON response every time.
    const headers = {
      'Content-Type': 'application/json',
      'anthropic-version': '2023-06-01',
      'anthropic-dangerous-direct-browser-access': 'true',
      'x-api-key': ST.settings.ak
    };
    // ── XHR-based API call (works from file:// on iOS Safari) ──
    const xhrResult = await new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      const xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
      xhr.open('POST', 'https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages', true);
      xhr.setRequestHeader('Content-Type', 'application/json');
      xhr.setRequestHeader('anthropic-version', '2023-06-01');
      xhr.setRequestHeader('anthropic-dangerous-direct-browser-access', 'true');
      xhr.setRequestHeader('x-api-key', ST.settings.ak);
      xhr.timeout = 60000;
      xhr.onload = () => resolve({ status: xhr.status, text: xhr.responseText });
      xhr.onerror = () => reject(new Error('XHR network error: ' + xhr.status));
      xhr.ontimeout = () => reject(new Error('XHR timeout after 60s'));
      xhr.send(JSON.stringify({
        model: 'claude-haiku-4-5-20251001',
        max_tokens: 6000,
        system: 'You are a JSON API. Output ONLY raw JSON with no markdown, no backticks, no code fences, no explanation. Start your response with { and end with }.',
        messages: [{ role: 'user', content: prompt }]
      }));
    });
    // (debug display removed)
    console.log('Brief XHR status:', xhrResult.status, xhrResult.text.slice(0,200));
    if (xhrResult.status !== 200) throw new Error('API ' + xhrResult.status + ': ' + xhrResult.text.slice(0,300));
    const raw = JSON.parse(xhrResult.text);
    const allText = (raw.content||[]).filter(b=>b.type==='text').map(b=>b.text).join('\n');
    console.log('Brief raw response (first 500):', allText.slice(0,500));
    if (!allText.trim()) throw new Error('Empty response: ' + JSON.stringify(raw).slice(0,200));
    // Aggressively strip any markdown fencing before parsing
    const data = extractJSON(allText);
    if (!data) {
      setBriefStatus('error');
      const bc = document.getElementById('brief-content');
      if (bc) bc.innerHTML = '<div class="brief-empty"><div class="brief-empty-icon">⚡</div>'
        + '<div class="brief-empty-txt">Brief parse failed — tap Refresh to retry</div></div>';
      return;
    }

    // Validate minimum structure — fill in missing keys gracefully
    if (!data.movers) data.movers = [];
    if (!data.stealth) data.stealth = [];
    if (!data.summary) data.summary = 'Market intelligence loading. Refresh to retry.';
    if (!data.candidates) data.candidates = [];

    // Cache it
    try { localStorage.setItem(BRIEF_CACHE_KEY, JSON.stringify({ ts: Date.now(), data })); } catch(e) {}
    renderBriefContent(data);
    setBriefStatus('ready', Date.now());

  } catch(err) {
    console.error('Brief error:', err);
    try {
      setBriefStatus('error');
      const bc = document.getElementById('brief-content');
      if (bc) bc.innerHTML = '<div class="brief-empty"><div class="brief-empty-icon">⚡</div><div class="brief-empty-txt" style="font-size:11px;word-break:break-all">ERROR: ' + (err.message||'Unknown error').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;') + '</div></div>';
    } catch(innerErr) { console.warn('Brief catch handler error:', innerErr); }
  }
}

function setBriefStatus(state, ts) {
  const el = document.getElementById('brief-status');
  const age = document.getElementById('brief-age');
  if (!el) return;
  if (state === 'loading') {
    el.className = 'brief-status bs-loading';
    el.textContent = 'LOADING…';
    if (age) age.textContent = '';
  } else if (state === 'ready') {
    el.className = 'brief-status bs-ready';
    el.textContent = 'LIVE';
    if (age && ts) {
      const mins = Math.floor((Date.now() - ts) / 60000);
      age.textContent = mins < 1 ? 'Just updated' : `${mins}m ago`;
    }
  } else if (state === 'error') {
    el.className = 'brief-status bs-stale';
    el.textContent = 'ERROR';
    if (age) age.textContent = 'tap refresh to retry';
  } else {
    el.className = 'brief-status bs-stale';
    el.textContent = 'OFFLINE';
  }
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// BOOT
