window.onerror = function(msg, src, line, col, err) {
  // Catch all uncaught errors including Safari's cross-context "Script error"
  console.warn('onerror:', msg, 'L'+line+':'+col, err ? err.message : '');
  return true; // prevent default browser error display
};
window.addEventListener('unhandledrejection', function(e) {
  const msg = e.reason?.message || String(e.reason || '');
  if (msg && msg !== 'Script error' && !msg.includes('Script error')) {
    console.warn('Rejected promise:', msg);
  }
  e.preventDefault();
  e.stopImmediatePropagation();
  return false;
});
// Also catch synchronous errors from cross-origin contexts
window.addEventListener('error', function(e) {
  if (e.message === 'Script error.' || e.message === 'Script error') {
    e.preventDefault();
    e.stopImmediatePropagation();
    return false;
  }
}, true); // capture phase
window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', init);

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════
// TICKER ANALYSIS TAB
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════
// TAB object removed - use TA_S


function setTATF(tf,btn){
  TAB.tf=tf;
  document.querySelectorAll('#ta-tf-row .tf-btn').forEach(b=>b.classList.toggle('on',b===btn));
  if(TAB.ticker) loadTAData(TAB.ticker);
}

function tfDays(tf){return({'1D':2,'1W':10,'1M':35,'3M':100,'6M':190,'1Y':370,'2Y':740,'5Y':1830})[tf]||100;}

async function loadTAData(t){
  const isCG={BTC:'bitcoin',ETH:'ethereum',SOL:'solana',AVAX:'avalanche-2',BNB:'binancecoin'};
  let ohlc=null,quote=null,news=[],analyst=null;
  try{
    if(isCG[t]){
      const days=tfDays(TAB.tf)+20;
      const r=await fetch('https://api.coingecko.com/api/v3/coins/'+isCG[t]+'/ohlc?vs_currency=usd&days='+Math.min(days,365),{signal:AbortSignal.timeout(10000)});
      if(r.ok){const raw=await r.json();ohlc=raw.map(d=>({date:new Date(d[0]).toISOString().split('T')[0],ts:d[0],o:d[1],h:d[2],l:d[3],c:d[4],v:0})).sort((a,b)=>a.ts-b.ts);}
    } else if(ST.settings.fh){
      const days=tfDays(TAB.tf)+20;
      const to=Math.floor(Date.now()/1000),from=to-days*86400;
      const res=TAB.tf==='1D'?'60':'D';
      const r=await fetch('https://finnhub.io/api/v1/stock/candle?symbol='+t+'&resolution='+res+'&from='+from+'&to='+to+'&token='+ST.settings.fh,{signal:AbortSignal.timeout(12000)});
      if(r.ok){const d=await r.json();if(d.s==='ok'&&d.c?.length>2)ohlc=d.t.map((_,i)=>({date:new Date(d.t[i]*1000).toISOString().split('T')[0],ts:d.t[i]*1000,o:d.o[i],h:d.h[i],l:d.l[i],c:d.c[i],v:d.v[i]})).sort((a,b)=>a.ts-b.ts);}
    }
  }catch(e){}
  // Quote
  if(isCG[t]){const cd=ST.cryptoData?.[isCG[t]];if(cd)quote={price:cd.usd,pct:cd.usd_24h_change};}
  else{quote=ST.quotes[t]||await fhGet('quote?symbol='+t).then(d=>d&&d.c?{price:d.c,pct:d.dp,open:d.o,high:d.h,low:d.l,prev:d.pc}:null).catch(()=>null);if(quote)ST.quotes[t]=quote;}
  // News
  if(ST.settings.fh&&!isCG[t]){try{const to=new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0],from=new Date(Date.now()-30*86400000).toISOString().split('T')[0];const r=await fetch('https://finnhub.io/api/v1/company-news?symbol='+t+'&from='+from+'&to='+to+'&token='+ST.settings.fh,{signal:AbortSignal.timeout(8000)});if(r.ok){const d=await r.json();news=d.slice(0,6);}}catch(e){}}
  // Analyst
  if(ST.settings.fh&&!isCG[t]){try{const[rr,pt]=await Promise.all([fetch('https://finnhub.io/api/v1/stock/recommendation?symbol='+t+'&token='+ST.settings.fh,{signal:AbortSignal.timeout(8000)}),fetch('https://finnhub.io/api/v1/stock/price-target?symbol='+t+'&token='+ST.settings.fh,{signal:AbortSignal.timeout(8000)})]);const rec=rr.ok?await rr.json():[];const ptt=pt.ok?await pt.json():null;analyst={rec:rec[0]||null,pt:ptt};}catch(e){}}
  TAB.data=ohlc;
  renderTAScreen(t,quote,ohlc,news,analyst);
}

function renderTAScreen(t,quote,ohlc,news,analyst){
  const price=quote?.price,pct=quote?.pct||0;
  const pc=pct>=0?'var(--green)':'var(--red)';
  const fp2=p=>!p&&p!==0?'—':p>=1000?'$'+Math.round(p).toLocaleString():p>=1?'$'+p.toFixed(2):p>=0.01?'$'+p.toFixed(4):'$'+p.toFixed(6);
  const fpp=p=>p==null?'':((p>=0?'+':'')+p.toFixed(2)+'%');

  // Stats
  let high52=null,low52=null;
  if(ohlc&&ohlc.length){const yr=ohlc.slice(-252);high52=Math.max(...yr.map(c=>c.h));low52=Math.min(...yr.map(c=>c.l));}

  // Technicals
  let techHtml='';
  if(ohlc&&ohlc.length>20){
    const cls=ohlc.map(c=>c.c),n=cls.length;
    const ema=(d,p)=>{const k=2/(p+1);let e=d.slice(0,Math.min(p,d.length)).reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0)/Math.min(p,d.length);for(let i=p;i<d.length;i++)e=d[i]*k+e*(1-k);return e;};
    const e20=ema(cls,20),e50=ema(cls,50),e200=cls.length>200?ema(cls,200):null;
    const rsi14=(()=>{const p=14;if(n<p+2)return null;let ag=0,al=0;for(let i=1;i<=p;i++){const d=cls[i]-cls[i-1];d>0?ag+=d:al-=d;}ag/=p;al/=p;for(let i=p+1;i<n;i++){const d=cls[i]-cls[i-1];const g=Math.max(0,d),l=Math.max(0,-d);ag=(ag*(p-1)+g)/p;al=(al*(p-1)+l)/p;}return al===0?100:Math.round(100-100/(1+ag/al));})();
    const lc=cls[n-1];
    const sigs=[
      {n:'RSI(14)',v:rsi14!=null?rsi14+'':'—',bull:rsi14&&rsi14<40,bear:rsi14&&rsi14>65,lbl:rsi14?(rsi14<30?'Oversold':rsi14>70?'Overbought':'Neutral'):'—'},
      {n:'EMA 20',v:fp2(e20),bull:lc>e20,bear:lc<e20,lbl:lc>e20?'Price above':'Price below'},
      {n:'EMA 50',v:fp2(e50),bull:lc>e50,bear:lc<e50,lbl:lc>e50?'Bullish':'Bearish'},
      {n:'EMA 200',v:e200?fp2(e200):'—',bull:e200&&lc>e200,bear:e200&&lc<e200,lbl:e200?(lc>e200?'Bull market':'Bear market'):'Insufficient data'},
      {n:'52W HIGH',v:fp2(high52),bull:high52&&lc>high52*0.9,bear:false,lbl:high52?((lc/high52*100).toFixed(0)+'% of high'):'—'},
      {n:'52W LOW',v:fp2(low52),bull:false,bear:low52&&lc<low52*1.15,lbl:low52?(((lc/low52-1)*100).toFixed(0)+'% above low'):'—'},
    ];
    techHtml='<div class="ta-sig-grid">'+sigs.map(s=>'<div class="ta-sig-card"><div class="ta-sig-name">'+s.n+'</div><div class="ta-sig-val" style="color:'+(s.bull?'var(--green)':s.bear?'var(--red)':'var(--tx2)')+'">'+s.v+'</div><div class="ta-sig-lbl">'+s.lbl+'</div></div>').join('')+'</div>';
  }

  // Analyst
  let analystHtml='';
  if(analyst?.rec){
    const r=analyst.rec,total=(r.strongBuy||0)+(r.buy||0)+(r.hold||0)+(r.sell||0)+(r.strongSell||0)||1;
    analystHtml+='<div class="ta-rat-bar">';
    if(r.strongBuy)analystHtml+='<div class="ta-rat-seg" style="width:'+(r.strongBuy/total*100).toFixed(0)+'%;background:var(--green)">'+r.strongBuy+'</div>';
    if(r.buy)analystHtml+='<div class="ta-rat-seg" style="width:'+(r.buy/total*100).toFixed(0)+'%;background:#7ecf6e">'+r.buy+'</div>';
    if(r.hold)analystHtml+='<div class="ta-rat-seg" style="width:'+(r.hold/total*100).toFixed(0)+'%;background:var(--amber)">'+r.hold+'</div>';
    if(r.sell)analystHtml+='<div class="ta-rat-seg" style="width:'+((r.sell+r.strongSell)/total*100).toFixed(0)+'%;background:var(--red)">'+(r.sell+r.strongSell)+'</div>';
    analystHtml+='</div><div style="display:flex;gap:8px;font-family:var(--f2);font-size:8px"><span style="color:var(--green)">■ Buy:'+(r.strongBuy+r.buy)+'</span><span style="color:var(--amber)">■ Hold:'+r.hold+'</span><span style="color:var(--red)">■ Sell:'+(r.sell+r.strongSell)+'</span></div>';
  }
  if(analyst?.pt?.targetMean){
    const pt=analyst.pt,up=price?((pt.targetMean/price-1)*100).toFixed(0):null;
    analystHtml+='<div class="ta-pt-row">'
      +'<div class="ta-pt-box"><div class="ta-pt-l">BEAR</div><div class="ta-pt-v" style="color:var(--red)">'+fp2(pt.targetLow)+'</div></div>'
      +'<div class="ta-pt-box"><div class="ta-pt-l">CONSENSUS</div><div class="ta-pt-v" style="color:var(--blue)">'+fp2(pt.targetMean)+'</div>'+(up?'<div class="ta-pt-up" style="color:'+(up>0?'var(--green)':'var(--red)')+'">'+( up>0?'+':'')+up+'%</div>':'')+'</div>'
      +'<div class="ta-pt-box"><div class="ta-pt-l">BULL</div><div class="ta-pt-v" style="color:var(--green)">'+fp2(pt.targetHigh)+'</div></div>'
      +'</div>';
  }

  // News
  let newsHtml=news.length?news.map(n=>{
    const sent=n.sentiment?.score>0.1?'bull':n.sentiment?.score<-0.1?'bear':'neut';
    const ago=n.datetime?Math.floor((Date.now()-n.datetime*1000)/3600000)+'h ago':'';
    return '<div class="ta-news-item"'+(n.url?' onclick="window.open(\''+n.url+'\',\'_blank\')"':'')+'>'
      +'<div class="ta-news-hl">'+n.headline+'</div>'
      +'<div class="ta-news-meta"><span>'+n.source+'</span><span>'+ago+'</span>'
      +'<span class="ta-sent ta-sent-'+sent+'">'+( sent==='bull'?'BULLISH':sent==='bear'?'BEARISH':'NEUTRAL')+'</span></div></div>';
  }).join(''):'<div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:9px;color:var(--tx3);padding:8px 0">No news — add Finnhub key for live news</div>';

  // Build HTML
  const html=
    '<div class="ta-hero">'
    +'<div class="ta-hero-row"><div><div class="ta-hero-ticker">'+t+'</div></div>'
    +'<div><div class="ta-hero-price" style="color:var(--tx)">'+(price?fp2(price):'—')+'</div>'
    +'<div class="ta-hero-chg" style="color:'+pc+'">'+fpp(pct)+'</div></div></div>'
    +'<div style="display:flex;gap:6px;flex-wrap:wrap;margin-top:8px">'
    +'<button class="ph-btn g" onclick="addToWL(\''+t+'\',\''+t+'\')">+ WATCHLIST</button>'
    +'<button class="ph-btn b" onclick="openChart(\''+t+'\')">📈 CHARTS</button>'
    +(ST.settings.ak?'<button class="ph-btn a" onclick="runTAI(\''+t+'\')">⚡ AI ANALYZE</button>':'')
    +'</div></div>'
    // Stats
    +'<div class="ta-stat-grid">'
    +'<div class="ta-stat"><div class="ta-stat-l">OPEN</div><div class="ta-stat-v">'+(quote?.open?fp2(quote.open):'—')+'</div></div>'
    +'<div class="ta-stat"><div class="ta-stat-l">PREV</div><div class="ta-stat-v">'+(quote?.prev?fp2(quote.prev):'—')+'</div></div>'
    +'<div class="ta-stat"><div class="ta-stat-l">52W HIGH</div><div class="ta-stat-v" style="color:var(--green)">'+(high52?fp2(high52):'—')+'</div></div>'
    +'<div class="ta-stat"><div class="ta-stat-l">52W LOW</div><div class="ta-stat-v" style="color:var(--red)">'+(low52?fp2(low52):'—')+'</div></div>'
    +'</div>'
    // Chart canvas
    +'<div class="ta-chart-box"><canvas id="ta-canvas" class="ta-canvas"></canvas></div>'
    // Overlay buttons
    +'<div class="ta-ind-row">'
    +'<button class="tf-btn on" id="ta-ov-e20" onclick="toggleTAOv(\'ema20\',this)">EMA20</button>'
    +'<button class="tf-btn on" id="ta-ov-e50" onclick="toggleTAOv(\'ema50\',this)">EMA50</button>'
    +'<button class="tf-btn" id="ta-ov-e200" onclick="toggleTAOv(\'ema200\',this)">EMA200</button>'
    +'<button class="tf-btn" id="ta-ov-bb" onclick="toggleTAOv(\'bb\',this)">BB</button>'
    +'<button class="tf-btn on" id="ta-ind-vol" onclick="toggleTAInd(\'vol\',this)">VOL</button>'
    +'<button class="tf-btn" id="ta-ind-rsi" onclick="toggleTAInd(\'rsi\',this)">RSI</button>'
    +'<button class="tf-btn" id="ta-ind-macd" onclick="toggleTAInd(\'macd\',this)">MACD</button>'
    +'</div>'
    // Technicals
    +(techHtml?'<div class="ta-sec"><div class="ta-sec-hdr">TECHNICAL SIGNALS</div>'+techHtml+'</div>':'')
    // Analyst
    +(analystHtml?'<div class="ta-sec"><div class="ta-sec-hdr">ANALYST RATINGS & PRICE TARGETS</div>'+analystHtml+'</div>':'')
    // News
    +'<div class="ta-sec"><div class="ta-sec-hdr">RECENT NEWS</div>'+newsHtml+'</div>'
    // AI section
    +'<div class="ta-sec"><div id="ta-ai-sec">'
    +(ST.settings.ak?'<button class="ph-btn g" style="width:100%" onclick="runTAI(\''+t+'\')">⚡ RUN AI DEEP DIVE — '+t+'</button>':'<div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:9px;color:var(--tx3)">Add Anthropic key in Settings for AI analysis</div>')
    +'</div></div>'
    +'<div style="height:20px"></div>';

  setHtml('ta-body',html);
  setTimeout(()=>drawTAChart(ohlc),80);
}


async function runTAI(t){
  const sec=document.getElementById('ta-ai-sec');
  if(!sec||!ST.settings.ak){showToast('Add Anthropic key in Settings');return;}
  sec.innerHTML='<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px;padding:10px 0"><div class="spin"></div><span style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:9px;color:var(--tx3)">AI ANALYZING '+t+'...</span></div>';
  const q=ST.quotes[t];
  const prompt=`Analyze ${t} for a US expat investor in Dubai. ${q?'Price: $'+q.price?.toFixed(2)+' ('+( q.pct>=0?'+':'')+q.pct?.toFixed(2)+'% today)':''}\nPortfolio: CLOV 90K @$2.05, UNH 140 @$288, $475K cash.\n1. VERDICT: Buy/Hold/Sell with confidence %\n2. CRASH ODDS: probability falls 30%+ in 6 months\n3. Bull case & price target\n4. Bear case & downside\n5. Key levels to watch\n6. One catalyst to watch in next 30 days\nBe direct and specific. Max 300 words.`;
  try{
    const text=await callAI('You are a direct, concise investment analyst.',prompt);
    sec.innerHTML='<div class="ta-ai-out">'+text+'</div>';
  }catch(e){
    sec.innerHTML='<div style="color:var(--red);font-family:var(--f2);font-size:10px;padding:10px">ERROR: '+e.message+'</div>';
  }
}


// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════
// PERIOD PERFORMANCE TRACKER
// Tracks Daily / WTD / MTD / YTD for watchlist
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════
const PERF_KEY = 'forge_perf_base';

function savePerfBaseline() {
  // Save current prices as baseline for periods
  const now = new Date();
  const stored = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(PERF_KEY) || '{}');
  const dayKey = now.toISOString().split('T')[0];
  const weekKey = getWeekStart();
  const monthKey = now.getFullYear() + '-' + String(now.getMonth()+1).padStart(2,'0');
  const yearKey = now.getFullYear() + '';

  const tickers = ['SPY','CLOV','UNH','HMBL','BTC','ETH','SOL'];
  tickers.forEach(t => {
    const q = ST.quotes[t] || ST.lastClose[t];
    const price = q?.price || q?.c;
    if (!price) return;
    // Only save if not already saved for this period
    if (!stored[dayKey]) stored[dayKey] = {};
    if (!stored[weekKey]) stored[weekKey] = {};
    if (!stored[monthKey]) stored[monthKey] = {};
    if (!stored[yearKey]) stored[yearKey] = {};
    // Save open of day/week/month/year (first price seen)
    if (!stored[dayKey][t]) stored[dayKey][t] = price;
    if (!stored[weekKey][t]) stored[weekKey][t] = price;
    if (!stored[monthKey][t]) stored[monthKey][t] = price;
    if (!stored[yearKey][t]) stored[yearKey][t] = price;
  });
  // Also save BTC from cryptoData
  const btc = ST.cryptoData?.bitcoin || ST.cryptoData?.btc;
  if (btc?.usd) {
    ['BTC'].forEach(t => {
      if (!stored[dayKey][t]) stored[dayKey][t] = btc.usd;
      if (!stored[weekKey][t]) stored[weekKey][t] = btc.usd;
      if (!stored[monthKey][t]) stored[monthKey][t] = btc.usd;
      if (!stored[yearKey][t]) stored[yearKey][t] = btc.usd;
    });
  }
  try { localStorage.setItem(PERF_KEY, JSON.stringify(stored)); } catch(e) {}
}

function getWeekStart() {
  const now = new Date();
  const day = now.getDay(); // 0=Sun
  const diff = now.getDate() - day + (day === 0 ? -6 : 1); // Monday
  const mon = new Date(now.setDate(diff));
  return mon.toISOString().split('T')[0];
}

function switchPerfTab(period, btn) {
  if(btn) btn.blur();
  document.querySelectorAll('.perf-tab').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('on'));
  if (btn) btn.classList.add('on');
  renderPerfContent(period);
}

function renderPerfContent(period) {
  const el = document.getElementById('perf-content');
  if (!el) return;

  const stored = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(PERF_KEY) || '{}');
  const now = new Date();
  let baseKey;
  if (period === 'daily') baseKey = now.toISOString().split('T')[0];
  else if (period === 'wtd') baseKey = getWeekStart();
  else if (period === 'mtd') baseKey = now.getFullYear() + '-' + String(now.getMonth()+1).padStart(2,'0');
  else baseKey = now.getFullYear() + '';

  const base = stored[baseKey] || {};
  const tickers = [
    {t:'SPY',  lbl:'S&P 500'},
    {t:'CLOV', lbl:'CLOV'},
    {t:'UNH',  lbl:'UNH'},
    {t:'BTC',  lbl:'BTC'},
  ];

  const rows = tickers.map(({t, lbl}) => {
    const q = ST.quotes[t] || ST.lastClose[t];
    const btcCG = ST.cryptoData?.bitcoin || ST.cryptoData?.btc;
    const cur = t === 'BTC' ? (btcCG?.usd || q?.price) : (q?.price || q?.c);
    const open = base[t];
    if (!cur && !open) return '';
    const pct = (open && cur) ? ((cur - open) / open * 100) : null;
    const col = pct == null ? 'var(--tx3)' : pct >= 0 ? 'var(--green)' : 'var(--red)';
    const curStr = cur ? (t==='BTC' ? '$'+Math.round(cur).toLocaleString() : '$'+cur.toFixed(t==='CLOV'?3:2)) : '—';
    const pctStr = pct != null ? (pct>=0?'+':'')+pct.toFixed(2)+'%' : (open ? '—' : 'No baseline');
    return '<div class="perf-row">'
      + '<span class="perf-name">'+lbl+'</span>'
      + '<span style="display:flex;gap:10px;align-items:center">'
      + '<span style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:9px;color:var(--tx3)">'+curStr+'</span>'
      + '<span class="perf-val" style="color:'+col+'">'+pctStr+'</span>'
      + '</span></div>';
  }).join('');

  el.innerHTML = rows || '<div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:9px;color:var(--tx3);padding:8px 0">Prices loading — tap Refresh</div>';
}

// Call savePerfBaseline after data loads

// ── ANALYSIS sub-tab for Charts ──────────────────────────

// ── setHtml helper ──
function setHtml(id, html) { const e = document.getElementById(id); if(e) e.innerHTML = html; }

// ── AI analysis for current chart asset ──

let TA_S = {
  asset: 'CLOV',
  tf: '1M',
  chartType: 'line',
  avKey: localStorage.getItem('forge_av') || 'IHBPWVYIUIM8M2UQ',
  overlays: { ema20:true, ema50:true, ema200:true, bb:false, fib:false, sr:false },
  indicators: { vol:true, rsi:true, macd:true },
  data: {},       // asset → array of {date,o,h,l,c,v}
  cache: {},      // asset+tf → precomputed indicators
  mouseX: -1,
  mouseIdx: -1,
  tab: 'chart',
  _rafPending: false,   // RAF throttle flag
  _lastW: 0,            // canvas resize guard
  _lastH: 0,            // canvas resize guard
};
// ── Charts sub-tab functions ──────────────────────────

async function taGetData(asset) {
  const isCG={BTC:'bitcoin',ETH:'ethereum',SOL:'solana',AVAX:'avalanche-2',BNB:'binancecoin'};
  let quote=null, news=[], analyst=null;
  if(isCG[asset]){const cd=ST.cryptoData?.[isCG[asset]]||ST.crypto?.[isCG[asset]];if(cd)quote={price:cd.usd,pct:cd.usd_24h_change};}
  else{quote=ST.quotes[asset];}
  if(ST.settings.fh && !isCG[asset]){
    try{
      const to=new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
      const from=new Date(Date.now()-30*86400000).toISOString().split('T')[0];
      const [nRes,rRes,ptRes]=await Promise.allSettled([
        fetch('https://finnhub.io/api/v1/company-news?symbol='+asset+'&from='+from+'&to='+to+'&token='+ST.settings.fh,{signal:AbortSignal.timeout(8000)}),
        fetch('https://finnhub.io/api/v1/stock/recommendation?symbol='+asset+'&token='+ST.settings.fh,{signal:AbortSignal.timeout(8000)}),
        fetch('https://finnhub.io/api/v1/stock/price-target?symbol='+asset+'&token='+ST.settings.fh,{signal:AbortSignal.timeout(8000)})
      ]);
      if(nRes.status==='fulfilled'&&nRes.value.ok) news=(await nRes.value.json()).slice(0,8);
      const rec=rRes.status==='fulfilled'&&rRes.value.ok?await rRes.value.json():[];
      const pt=ptRes.status==='fulfilled'&&ptRes.value.ok?await ptRes.value.json():null;
      analyst={rec:rec[0]||null,pt};
    }catch(e){}
  }
  return {quote, news, analyst};
}

function taLoading(bodyId, asset) {
  setHtml(bodyId,'<div style="padding:40px;text-align:center"><div class="spin"></div><div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:9px;color:var(--tx3);margin-top:12px;letter-spacing:2px">LOADING '+asset+'...</div></div>');
}

function taNoAsset(bodyId) {
  setHtml(bodyId,'<div style="padding:30px;text-align:center;font-family:var(--f2);font-size:9px;color:var(--tx3);letter-spacing:2px">SELECT AN ASSET ABOVE</div>');
}

// TECHNICALS tab
async function taShowTechnicals() {
  const asset = TA_S.asset; if(!asset){taNoAsset('ta-tech-body');return;}
  taLoading('ta-tech-body', asset);
  const ohlc = TA_S.data[asset];
  if(!ohlc||ohlc.length<20){setHtml('ta-tech-body','<div style="padding:20px;font-family:var(--f2);font-size:9px;color:var(--tx3);text-align:center">Load chart first — select asset above</div>');return;}
  const {quote} = await taGetData(asset);
  const cls=ohlc.map(c=>c.c), n=cls.length;
  const fmtP=p=>!p&&p!==0?'—':p>=1000?'$'+Math.round(p).toLocaleString():p>=1?'$'+p.toFixed(2):'$'+p.toFixed(4);
  const ema=(d,p)=>{const k=2/(p+1);let e=d.slice(0,Math.min(p,d.length)).reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0)/Math.min(p,d.length);for(let i=p;i<d.length;i++)e=d[i]*k+e*(1-k);return e;};
  const e20=ema(cls,20),e50=ema(cls,50),e200=cls.length>200?ema(cls,200):null;
  const rsiV=(()=>{const p=14;if(n<p+2)return null;let ag=0,al=0;for(let i=1;i<=p;i++){const d=cls[i]-cls[i-1];d>0?ag+=d:al-=d;}ag/=p;al/=p;for(let i=p+1;i<n;i++){const d=cls[i]-cls[i-1];const g=Math.max(0,d),l=Math.max(0,-d);ag=(ag*(p-1)+g)/p;al=(al*(p-1)+l)/p;}return al===0?100:Math.round(100-100/(1+ag/al));})();
  const lc=cls[n-1];
  const yr=ohlc.slice(-252); const h52=Math.max(...yr.map(c=>c.h)); const l52=Math.min(...yr.map(c=>c.l));
  const sigs=[
    {n:'RSI(14)',v:rsiV!=null?rsiV+'':'—',bull:rsiV&&rsiV<40,bear:rsiV&&rsiV>65,lbl:rsiV?(rsiV<30?'Oversold — potential buy zone':rsiV>70?'Overbought — potential sell zone':'Neutral momentum'):'—'},
    {n:'EMA 20',v:fmtP(e20),bull:lc>e20,bear:lc<e20,lbl:lc>e20?'Price above — short term bullish':'Price below — short term bearish'},
    {n:'EMA 50',v:fmtP(e50),bull:lc>e50,bear:lc<e50,lbl:lc>e50?'Price above — medium term bullish':'Price below — medium term bearish'},
    {n:'EMA 200',v:e200?fmtP(e200):'—',bull:e200&&lc>e200,bear:e200&&lc<e200,lbl:e200?(lc>e200?'Above 200d — long term bull market':'Below 200d — long term bear market'):'Need 200+ candles'},
    {n:'52W HIGH',v:fmtP(h52),bull:lc>h52*0.9,bear:false,lbl:(lc/h52*100).toFixed(0)+'% of 52-week high'},
    {n:'52W LOW',v:fmtP(l52),bull:false,bear:lc<l52*1.1,lbl:((lc/l52-1)*100).toFixed(0)+'% above 52-week low'},
  ];
  const bullCount=sigs.filter(s=>s.bull).length, bearCount=sigs.filter(s=>s.bear).length;
  const score=Math.round((bullCount/(bullCount+bearCount||1))*100);
  const scoreCol=score>=60?'var(--green)':score>=40?'var(--amber)':'var(--red)';
  let html='<div style="padding:12px 14px;border-bottom:1px solid var(--b1);display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center">'
    +'<div><div style="font-family:var(--f1);font-size:24px;letter-spacing:2px">'+asset+'</div>'
    +'<div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:8px;color:var(--tx3)">TECHNICAL ANALYSIS</div></div>'
    +'<div style="text-align:right"><div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:22px;color:'+scoreCol+'">'+score+'</div>'
    +'<div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:8px;color:'+scoreCol+'">'+(score>=60?'BULLISH':score>=40?'NEUTRAL':'BEARISH')+'</div></div>'
    +'</div>'
    +'<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:8px;padding:12px 14px">'
    +sigs.map(s=>'<div style="background:var(--bg2);border:1px solid '+(s.bull?'var(--gbrd)':s.bear?'var(--rbrd)':'var(--b1)')+';border-radius:8px;padding:10px">'
      +'<div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:7.5px;color:var(--tx3);margin-bottom:4px">'+s.n+'</div>'
      +'<div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:14px;color:'+(s.bull?'var(--green)':s.bear?'var(--red)':'var(--tx)')+'">'+s.v+'</div>'
      +'<div style="font-family:var(--f3);font-size:9px;color:var(--tx3);margin-top:3px;line-height:1.4">'+s.lbl+'</div>'
      +'</div>').join('')
    +'</div>';
  setHtml('ta-tech-body', html);
}

// NEWS tab
async function taShowNews() {
  const asset = TA_S.asset; if(!asset){taNoAsset('ta-news-body');return;}
  taLoading('ta-news-body', asset);
  const {news} = await taGetData(asset);
  let html='<div style="padding:12px 14px;border-bottom:1px solid var(--b1)">'
    +'<div style="font-family:var(--f1);font-size:22px;letter-spacing:2px">'+asset+' NEWS</div>'
    +'<div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:8px;color:var(--tx3)">LAST 30 DAYS</div>'
    +'</div>';
  if(!news.length){
    html+='<div style="padding:30px;text-align:center;font-family:var(--f2);font-size:9px;color:var(--tx3)">No news found — add Finnhub key in Settings</div>';
  } else {
    html+='<div style="padding:0 14px">'+news.map(n=>{
      const ago=n.datetime?Math.floor((Date.now()-n.datetime*1000)/3600000)+'h ago':'';
      const sent=n.sentiment?.score>0.1?'bull':n.sentiment?.score<-0.1?'bear':'neut';
      const sentCol=sent==='bull'?'var(--green)':sent==='bear'?'var(--red)':'var(--tx3)';
      const sentLbl=sent==='bull'?'BULLISH':sent==='bear'?'BEARISH':'NEUTRAL';
      return '<div style="padding:12px 0;border-bottom:1px solid var(--b1)" '
        +(n.url?'onclick="window.open(\''+n.url+'\',\'_blank\')" style="cursor:pointer"':'')+'>'
        +'<div style="display:flex;gap:6px;align-items:center;margin-bottom:5px">'
        +'<span style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:7.5px;color:var(--tx3)">'+n.source+'</span>'
        +'<span style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:7.5px;color:var(--tx3)">'+ago+'</span>'
        +'<span style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:7px;padding:1px 5px;border-radius:2px;border:1px solid;color:'+sentCol+';border-color:'+sentCol+'40">'+sentLbl+'</span>'
        +'</div>'
        +'<div style="font-family:var(--f3);font-size:12px;line-height:1.5;color:var(--tx)">'+n.headline+'</div>'
        +'</div>';
    }).join('')+'</div>';
  }
  setHtml('ta-news-body', html);
}

// RATINGS tab
async function taShowRatings() {
  const asset = TA_S.asset; if(!asset){taNoAsset('ta-ratings-body');return;}
  taLoading('ta-ratings-body', asset);
  const {quote, analyst} = await taGetData(asset);
  const fmtP=p=>!p&&p!==0?'—':p>=1000?'$'+Math.round(p).toLocaleString():p>=1?'$'+p.toFixed(2):'$'+p.toFixed(4);
  let html='<div style="padding:12px 14px;border-bottom:1px solid var(--b1)">'
    +'<div style="font-family:var(--f1);font-size:22px;letter-spacing:2px">'+asset+' RATINGS</div>'
    +'<div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:8px;color:var(--tx3)">ANALYST CONSENSUS</div>'
    +'</div>';
  if(!analyst?.rec && !analyst?.pt?.targetMean){
    html+='<div style="padding:30px;text-align:center;font-family:var(--f2);font-size:9px;color:var(--tx3)">No analyst data — crypto assets or add Finnhub key</div>';
  } else {
    if(analyst.rec){
      const r=analyst.rec,total=(r.strongBuy||0)+(r.buy||0)+(r.hold||0)+(r.sell||0)+(r.strongSell||0)||1;
      const bullPct=Math.round((r.strongBuy+r.buy)/total*100);
      const rating=bullPct>60?'STRONG BUY':bullPct>45?'BUY':bullPct>35?'HOLD':'SELL';
      const ratingCol=rating==='STRONG BUY'||rating==='BUY'?'var(--green)':rating==='HOLD'?'var(--amber)':'var(--red)';
      html+='<div style="padding:14px">'
        +'<div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:24px;color:'+ratingCol+';margin-bottom:4px">'+rating+'</div>'
        +'<div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:9px;color:var(--tx3);margin-bottom:12px">'+total+' analysts · '+bullPct+'% bullish</div>'
        +'<div style="display:flex;height:10px;border-radius:5px;overflow:hidden;margin-bottom:8px">'
        +(r.strongBuy?'<div style="width:'+(r.strongBuy/total*100).toFixed(0)+'%;background:#1a7f4b"></div>':'')
        +(r.buy?'<div style="width:'+(r.buy/total*100).toFixed(0)+'%;background:var(--green)"></div>':'')
        +(r.hold?'<div style="width:'+(r.hold/total*100).toFixed(0)+'%;background:var(--amber)"></div>':'')
        +((r.sell+r.strongSell)?'<div style="width:'+((r.sell+r.strongSell)/total*100).toFixed(0)+'%;background:var(--red)"></div>':'')
        +'</div>'
        +'<div style="display:flex;gap:14px;font-family:var(--f2);font-size:9px">'
        +'<span style="color:var(--green)">■ Strong Buy: '+r.strongBuy+'</span>'
        +'<span style="color:var(--green)">■ Buy: '+r.buy+'</span>'
        +'<span style="color:var(--amber)">■ Hold: '+r.hold+'</span>'
        +'<span style="color:var(--red)">■ Sell: '+(r.sell+r.strongSell)+'</span>'
        +'</div></div>';
    }
    if(analyst?.pt?.targetMean){
      const pt=analyst.pt, price=quote?.price;
      const up=price?((pt.targetMean/price-1)*100).toFixed(0):null;
      html+='<div style="padding:0 14px 14px;border-top:1px solid var(--b1);padding-top:14px">'
        +'<div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:8px;color:var(--tx3);letter-spacing:2px;margin-bottom:10px">PRICE TARGETS</div>'
        +'<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr 1fr;gap:8px">'
        +'<div style="background:var(--bg2);border:1px solid var(--rbrd);border-radius:8px;padding:12px;text-align:center">'
        +'<div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:7.5px;color:var(--tx3);margin-bottom:6px">BEAR</div>'
        +'<div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:16px;color:var(--red)">'+fmtP(pt.targetLow)+'</div></div>'
        +'<div style="background:var(--bg2);border:1px solid var(--bbrd);border-radius:8px;padding:12px;text-align:center">'
        +'<div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:7.5px;color:var(--tx3);margin-bottom:6px">CONSENSUS</div>'
        +'<div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:16px;color:var(--blue)">'+fmtP(pt.targetMean)+'</div>'
        +(up?'<div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:9px;color:'+(up>0?'var(--green)':'var(--red)')+'">'+( up>0?'+':'')+up+'%</div>':'')
        +'</div>'
        +'<div style="background:var(--bg2);border:1px solid var(--gbrd);border-radius:8px;padding:12px;text-align:center">'
        +'<div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:7.5px;color:var(--tx3);margin-bottom:6px">BULL</div>'
        +'<div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:16px;color:var(--green)">'+fmtP(pt.targetHigh)+'</div></div>'
        +'</div></div>';
    }
  }
  setHtml('ta-ratings-body', html);
}

// AI tab
async function taShowAI() {
  const asset = TA_S.asset; if(!asset){taNoAsset('ta-ai-body');return;}
  const el = document.getElementById('ta-ai-body');
  if(!el) return;
  if(!ST.settings.ak){
    el.innerHTML='<div style="padding:30px;text-align:center;font-family:var(--f2);font-size:9px;color:var(--tx3)">ADD ANTHROPIC KEY IN SETTINGS TO ENABLE AI</div>';
    return;
  }
  // Check if already loaded for this asset
  if(el.dataset.asset===asset && el.innerHTML.length > 200 && !el.innerHTML.includes('RUN AI')) return;
  el.innerHTML='<div style="padding:20px 14px">'
    +'<div style="font-family:var(--f1);font-size:22px;letter-spacing:2px;margin-bottom:4px">'+asset+' · AI ANALYSIS</div>'
    +'<div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:8px;color:var(--tx3);margin-bottom:16px">POWERED BY CLAUDE</div>'
    +'<button id="ta-ai-run" class="ph-btn g" style="width:100%;padding:14px;font-size:14px">⚡ RUN AI DEEP DIVE</button>'
    +'</div>';
  el.dataset.asset = asset;
  setTimeout(()=>{
    const btn=document.getElementById('ta-ai-run');
    if(btn) btn.onclick=()=>runTAI(asset);
  },50);
}

// ── Add custom ticker to Charts tab ──────────────────
function addChartTicker() {
  const inp = document.getElementById('chart-ticker-inp');
  const t = (inp?.value || '').trim().toUpperCase();
  if (!t) { showToast('Enter a ticker'); return; }
  inp.value = '';
  inp.blur();
  if (!TA_S.customTickers) TA_S.customTickers = [];
  if (!TA_S.customTickers.includes(t)) TA_S.customTickers.push(t);
  renderTAAssetRow();
  selectAsset(t);
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// DIVIDEND ENGINE
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// Fetches upcoming + recent dividend data for every position via Finnhub.
// Stores results in ST.dividends[ticker]. Renders alerts in Deploy tab
// and summary rows in Portfolio tab. Window is configurable via Settings.

async function loadDividends() {
  if (!ST.settings.fh) return;
  if (!ST.positions || !ST.positions.length) return;
  if (!ST.dividends) ST.dividends = {};

  const today = new Date();
  today.setHours(0,0,0,0);
  const windowDays = parseInt(ST.settings.divAlert) || 14;

  // Fetch dividends for all positions in parallel
  const results = await Promise.allSettled(
    ST.positions.map(async p => {
      try {
        const data = await fhGet(`stock/dividends2?symbol=${encodeURIComponent(p.ticker)}`);
        if (!data || !data.data || !data.data.length) return { ticker: p.ticker, divs: [] };
        // Sort by ex-date descending
        const sorted = data.data
          .filter(d => d.exDate)
          .sort((a,b) => new Date(b.exDate) - new Date(a.exDate));
        return { ticker: p.ticker, divs: sorted };
      } catch(e) {
        return { ticker: p.ticker, divs: [] };
      }
    })
  );

  results.forEach(r => {
    if (r.status !== 'fulfilled') return;
    const { ticker, divs } = r.value;
    if (!divs.length) { ST.dividends[ticker] = { upcoming: null, last: null, annual: null }; return; }

    // Next upcoming ex-date (in future)
    const upcoming = divs.find(d => new Date(d.exDate) >= today) || null;
    // Last paid (most recent past ex-date)
    const last = divs.find(d => new Date(d.exDate) < today) || null;
    // Estimate annual yield: sum of last 4 dividends
    const last4 = divs.filter(d => new Date(d.exDate) < today).slice(0, 4);
    const annualAmt = last4.reduce((s, d) => s + (d.amount || 0), 0);

    ST.dividends[ticker] = { upcoming, last, annualAmt, allDivs: divs };
  });

  // Persist lightweight summary to localStorage
  try {
    const toSave = {};
    Object.keys(ST.dividends).forEach(t => {
      const d = ST.dividends[t];
      toSave[t] = { upcoming: d.upcoming, last: d.last, annualAmt: d.annualAmt };
    });
    localStorage.setItem('forge_dividends', JSON.stringify({ ts: Date.now(), data: toSave }));
  } catch(e) {}

  renderDividendAlerts();
  renderDividendSummary();
}

function loadDividendsCache() {
  try {
    const cached = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('forge_dividends') || 'null');
    if (cached && cached.data && (Date.now() - cached.ts) < 6 * 3600 * 1000) {
      ST.dividends = cached.data;
      renderDividendAlerts();
      renderDividendSummary();
    }
  } catch(e) {}
}

function renderDividendAlerts() {
  if (!ST.dividends) return;
  const today = new Date(); today.setHours(0,0,0,0);
  const windowDays = parseInt(ST.settings.divAlert) || 14;

  ST.positions.forEach(p => {
    const d = ST.dividends[p.ticker];
    if (!d || !d.upcoming) return;

    const exDate = new Date(d.upcoming.exDate);
    const daysUntil = Math.round((exDate - today) / 86400000);
    const amount = d.upcoming.amount || 0;
    const payout = (amount * p.shares).toLocaleString('en-US', { minimumFractionDigits: 2, maximumFractionDigits: 2 });
    const exDateFmt = exDate.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { month: 'short', day: 'numeric', year: 'numeric' });
    const freq = d.upcoming.freq ? ` · ${d.upcoming.freq}` : '';

    // ── Deploy tab alert box (UNH detail uses id unh-div-alert-box; generic fallback) ──
    const alertBoxId = p.ticker.toLowerCase() + '-div-alert-box';
    const alertBoxEl = document.getElementById(alertBoxId);
    if (alertBoxEl) {
      if (daysUntil >= 0 && daysUntil <= windowDays) {
        const urgency = daysUntil <= 3 ? 'var(--red)' : daysUntil <= 7 ? 'var(--amber)' : 'var(--blue)';
        const urgencyBrd = daysUntil <= 3 ? 'var(--rbrd)' : daysUntil <= 7 ? 'var(--abrd)' : 'var(--bbrd)';
        const urgencyDim = daysUntil <= 3 ? 'var(--rdim)' : daysUntil <= 7 ? 'var(--adim)' : 'var(--bdim)';
        const dayLabel = daysUntil === 0 ? 'TODAY' : daysUntil === 1 ? 'TOMORROW' : `IN ${daysUntil} DAYS`;
        alertBoxEl.innerHTML = `<div class="alert-box" style="margin-bottom:12px;border-color:${urgencyBrd};background:${urgencyDim}">
          <div style="font-size:18px">💰</div>
          <div>
            <div class="alert-box-title" style="color:${urgency}">DIVIDEND EX-DATE: ${exDateFmt.toUpperCase()} — ${dayLabel}</div>
            <div class="alert-box-body">$${amount.toFixed(2)}/share × ${p.shares.toLocaleString()} shares = <strong>$${payout} free cash</strong>${freq}. Must hold through ex-date to collect. Do NOT sell before then.</div>
          </div>
        </div>`;
      } else if (daysUntil > windowDays) {
        // Upcoming but outside alert window — show quiet info
        alertBoxEl.innerHTML = `<div style="padding:8px 12px;background:var(--bg2);border:1px solid var(--b1);border-radius:6px;margin-bottom:12px;font-family:var(--f2);font-size:8.5px;color:var(--tx3)">
          NEXT DIVIDEND · Ex-date ${exDateFmt} · $${amount.toFixed(2)}/sh · Est. payout $${payout} · ${daysUntil} days away
        </div>`;
      } else {
        alertBoxEl.innerHTML = '';
      }
    }

    // ── Deploy tab inline az-note span ──
    const noteSpanId = p.ticker.toLowerCase() + '-div-deploy-note';
    const noteEl = document.getElementById(noteSpanId);
    if (noteEl) {
      if (daysUntil >= 0 && daysUntil <= windowDays) {
        const dayLabel = daysUntil === 0 ? 'TODAY' : daysUntil === 1 ? 'tomorrow' : `in ${daysUntil} days`;
        noteEl.innerHTML = `<strong style="color:var(--amber)">⚡ Div ex-date ${exDateFmt} (${dayLabel}) — hold to collect $${payout}.</strong>`;
      } else {
        noteEl.textContent = '';
      }
    }
  });
}

function renderDividendSummary() {
  // Renders a dividend summary section inside Portfolio → POSITIONS tab
  const container = document.getElementById('div-summary-section');
  if (!container) return;
  if (!ST.dividends) { container.style.display = 'none'; return; }

  const today = new Date(); today.setHours(0,0,0,0);
  const rows = [];

  ST.positions.forEach(p => {
    const d = ST.dividends[p.ticker];
    if (!d) return;
    const hasAny = d.upcoming || d.last;
    if (!hasAny) return;

    const upcomingStr = d.upcoming
      ? (() => {
          const exDate = new Date(d.upcoming.exDate);
          const daysUntil = Math.round((exDate - today) / 86400000);
          const payout = ((d.upcoming.amount || 0) * p.shares).toLocaleString('en-US', { minimumFractionDigits: 2, maximumFractionDigits: 2 });
          const dayLabel = daysUntil < 0 ? `${Math.abs(daysUntil)}d ago` : daysUntil === 0 ? 'TODAY' : `in ${daysUntil}d`;
          const col = daysUntil >= 0 && daysUntil <= (parseInt(ST.settings.divAlert)||14) ? 'var(--amber)' : 'var(--tx2)';
          return `<span style="color:${col}">Ex: ${exDate.toLocaleDateString('en-US',{month:'short',day:'numeric'})} (${dayLabel}) · $${(d.upcoming.amount||0).toFixed(2)}/sh · <strong>$${payout}</strong></span>`;
        })()
      : '—';

    const lastStr = d.last
      ? `Last paid $${(d.last.amount||0).toFixed(2)}/sh on ${new Date(d.last.exDate).toLocaleDateString('en-US',{month:'short',day:'numeric',year:'numeric'})}`
      : '—';

    const annualStr = d.annualAmt
      ? `~$${d.annualAmt.toFixed(2)}/yr per share`
      : '';

    rows.push(`<div style="padding:10px 14px;border-bottom:1px solid var(--b1);display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:4px">
      <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center">
        <div style="font-family:var(--f1);font-size:16px;letter-spacing:2px">${p.ticker}</div>
        ${annualStr ? `<div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:8px;color:var(--tx3)">${annualStr}</div>` : ''}
      </div>
      <div style="font-family:var(--f3);font-size:11px;line-height:1.5">${upcomingStr}</div>
      <div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:9px;color:var(--tx3)">${lastStr}</div>
    </div>`);
  });

  if (!rows.length) { container.style.display = 'none'; return; }

  container.style.display = 'block';
  container.innerHTML = `
    <div style="padding:10px 14px 6px;border-bottom:1px solid var(--b1);display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px">
      <div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:9px;letter-spacing:2px;color:var(--tx2)">💰 DIVIDEND TRACKER</div>
      <div style="flex:1;height:1px;background:var(--b1)"></div>
      <div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:8px;color:var(--tx3)">LIVE · ALL POSITIONS</div>
    </div>
    ${rows.join('')}
  `;
}

function savePositions(){try{localStorage.setItem('forge_positions',JSON.stringify(ST.positions));}catch(e){}}
function saveCashPosition(){
  const usd=parseFloat(document.getElementById('edit-cash-usd')?.value)||0;
  const aed=parseFloat(document.getElementById('edit-cash-aed')?.value)||0;
  ST.cash={usd,aed};
  try{localStorage.setItem('forge_cash',JSON.stringify(ST.cash));}catch(e){}
  ST.settings.portSize=Math.round(usd+aed/3.67);
  showToast('Cash saved ✓');renderEditPositions();
}
function addPosition(){
  const ticker=document.getElementById('edit-new-ticker')?.value.trim().toUpperCase();
  const shares=parseFloat(document.getElementById('edit-new-shares')?.value);
  const avgCost=parseFloat(document.getElementById('edit-new-cost')?.value);
  if(!ticker){showToast('Enter ticker');return;}
  if(!shares||shares<=0){showToast('Enter shares');return;}
  if(!avgCost||avgCost<=0){showToast('Enter cost');return;}
  const ex=ST.positions.find(p=>p.ticker===ticker);
  if(ex){ex.shares=shares;ex.avgCost=avgCost;}
  else ST.positions.push({ticker,shares,avgCost});
  savePositions();
  ['edit-new-ticker','edit-new-shares','edit-new-cost'].forEach(id=>{const el=document.getElementById(id);if(el)el.value='';});
  showToast(ticker+' saved ✓');renderEditPositions();
}
function removePosition(ticker){
  ST.positions=ST.positions.filter(p=>p.ticker!==ticker);
  savePositions();renderEditPositions();showToast(ticker+' removed');
}
function editPositionForm(idx){
  const p=ST.positions[idx];if(!p)return;
  const t=document.getElementById('edit-new-ticker'),s=document.getElementById('edit-new-shares'),c=document.getElementById('edit-new-cost');
  if(t)t.value=p.ticker;if(s)s.value=p.shares;if(c)c.value=p.avgCost;
  t&&t.scrollIntoView({behavior:'smooth'});
}
function renderEditPositions(){
  const el=document.getElementById('edit-positions-list');if(!el)return;
  const cu=document.getElementById('edit-cash-usd'),ca=document.getElementById('edit-cash-aed');
  if(cu)cu.value=ST.cash?ST.cash.usd:40000;
  if(ca)ca.value=ST.cash?ST.cash.aed:1600000;
  if(!ST.positions||!ST.positions.length){el.innerHTML='<div style="padding:14px;font-family:var(--f2);font-size:9px;color:var(--tx3);text-align:center">No positions yet</div>';return;}
  el.innerHTML=ST.positions.map(function(p,i){
    const q=ST.quotes[p.ticker];const price=q?(q.price||q.c):null;
    const val=price?(price*p.shares):null;
    const pnl=price?((price-p.avgCost)/p.avgCost*100):null;
    const pc=pnl==null?'var(--tx3)':pnl>=0?'var(--green)':'var(--red)';
    return '<div style="padding:12px 14px;border-bottom:1px solid var(--b1);display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px">'
      +'<div style="flex:1"><div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:13px">'+p.ticker+'</div>'
      +'<div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:9px;color:var(--tx3)">'+p.shares.toLocaleString()+' shs @ $'+p.avgCost+(val?' · $'+Math.round(val).toLocaleString():'')+'</div></div>'
      +(pnl!=null?'<div style="font-family:var(--f2);font-size:11px;color:'+pc+'">'+(pnl>=0?'+':'')+pnl.toFixed(1)+'%</div>':'')
      +'<button onclick="editPositionForm('+i+')" style="background:var(--bdim);border:1px solid var(--bbrd);border-radius:4px;color:var(--blue);font-family:var(--f2);font-size:8px;padding:4px 8px;cursor:pointer">EDIT</button>'
      +'<button data-ticker="'+p.ticker+'" onclick="removePosition(this.dataset.ticker)" class="rm-btn">✕</button>'
      +'</div>';
  }).join('');
}
function loadPositions(){
  const s=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('forge_positions')||'null');
  if(s&&s.length) ST.positions=s;
  const c=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('forge_cash')||'null');
  if(c) ST.cash=c;
}

function goToChart(ticker) {
  showScreen('charts', document.getElementById('nb-charts'));
  setTimeout(() => {
    if (!TA_S.customTickers) TA_S.customTickers = [];
    if (!TA_S.customTickers.includes(ticker)) TA_S.customTickers.push(ticker);
    renderTAAssetRow();
    selectAsset(ticker);
  }, 200);
}
